### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Documento de Arquitetura

## 1. Visão Geral da Arquitetura V12

### 1.1 Princípios Fundamentais
- **Autonomia Total**: Cada componente deve ser independente e resiliente
- **Zero Downtime**: Deployments contínuos sem interrupção de serviço
- **Observabilidade Nativa**: Monitoramento embutido em todos os níveis
- **Segurança por Design**: Autenticação, autorização e criptografia integradas

### 1.2 Stack Tecnológico

#### Frontend
```
Framework: React 18 + TypeScript
Build Tool: Vite 5
UI Library: Material-UI v6 (MUI)
State Management: Zustand + React Query
Routing: React Router v6
Testing: Vitest + React Testing Library + Playwright (E2E)
Styling: Emotion (CSS-in-JS) + MUI System
```

#### Backend
```
Runtime: Node.js 20 LTS
Framework: Express.js 5 + TypeScript
API: RESTful + GraphQL (Apollo Server)
Validation: Zod + Express Validator
Authentication: JWT + OAuth2 (Passport.js)
ORM: Prisma 5 (Type-safe database access)
```

#### Banco de Dados
```
Primary: PostgreSQL 16 (com extensões: pgvector, pg_trgm)
Cache: Redis 7 (sessões e cache distribuído)
Search: Elasticsearch 8 (busca full-text)
Queue: BullMQ (Redis-based job queue)
```

#### Infraestrutura
```
Container: Docker + Docker Compose
Orchestration: Kubernetes (para produção)
CI/CD: GitHub Actions + ArgoCD (GitOps)
Monitoring: Prometheus + Grafana + Loki
Logging: Winston + OpenTelemetry
```

## 2. Estrutura de Pastas

### 2.1 Estrutura Monorepo (Turborepo)
```
diyapp-v12/
├── apps/
│   ├── web/                    # Frontend React/Vite
│   │   ├── src/
│   │   │   ├── components/     # Componentes reutilizáveis
│   │   │   │   ├── common/     # Botões, inputs, modais
│   │   │   │   ├── layout/     # Header, Sidebar, Footer
│   │   │   │   └── features/   # Componentes específicos de features
│   │   │   ├── pages/          # Páginas/rotas da aplicação
│   │   │   ├── hooks/          # Custom React hooks
│   │   │   ├── store/          # Zustand stores
│   │   │   ├── services/       # API clients e serviços
│   │   │   ├── utils/          # Funções utilitárias
│   │   │   ├── types/          # TypeScript types/interfaces
│   │   │   ├── styles/         # Estilos globais e temas
│   │   │   └── assets/         # Imagens, fonts, etc.
│   │   ├── public/             # Arquivos estáticos
│   │   ├── index.html          # Ponto de entrada obrigatório
│   │   ├── vite.config.ts      # Configuração Vite
│   │   └── package.json
│   │
│   ├── api/                    # Backend Node.js/Express
│   │   ├── src/
│   │   │   ├── controllers/    # Controladores das rotas
│   │   │   ├── services/       # Lógica de negócio
│   │   │   ├── middleware/     # Middlewares customizados
│   │   │   ├── models/         # Modelos Prisma/TypeScript
│   │   │   ├── routes/         # Definição de rotas
│   │   │   ├── utils/          # Utilitários e helpers
│   │   │   ├── types/          # Tipos TypeScript
│   │   │   ├── config/         # Configurações

│   │   │   └── app.ts          # Aplicação Express
│   │   ├── prisma/             # Schema e migrations
│   │   ├── Dockerfile
│   │   └── package.json
│   │
│   └── worker/                 # Workers para jobs assíncronos
│       ├── src/
│       │   ├── jobs/           # Definição de jobs
│       │   ├── processors/     # Processadores de jobs
│       │   └── worker.ts       # Ponto de entrada
│       └── package.json
│
├── packages/                   # Pacotes compartilhados
│   ├── shared-types/           # Tipos compartilhados
│   ├── shared-utils/           # Utilitários compartilhados
│   ├── eslint-config/          # Configuração ESLint
│   └── tsconfig/               # Configurações TypeScript
│
├── infrastructure/             # IaC (Infrastructure as Code)
│   ├── kubernetes/             # Manifests K8s
│   ├── docker-compose/         # Docker Compose para dev
│   └── terraform/              # Terraform para cloud
│
├── scripts/                    # Scripts utilitários
├── .github/                    # GitHub Actions workflows
├── docker-compose.yml          # Docker Compose raiz
├── package.json                # Workspace root
├── turbo.json                  # Configuração Turborepo
├── .env.example                # Variáveis de ambiente exemplo
└── README.md
```

## 3. Padrões de Código

### 3.1 TypeScript
```typescript
// ✅ CORRETO - Tipos explícitos, interfaces bem definidas
interface User {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  name: string;
  createdAt: Date;
}

const getUser = async (id: string): Promise<User> => {
  // Implementação
};

// ❌ EVITAR - any, implicit any
const processData = (data: any) => { /* ... */ };
```

### 3.2 React Components
```typescript
// Componente funcional com TypeScript
import React from 'react';
import { Button } from '@mui/material';

interface UserCardProps {
  user: User;
  onEdit: (userId: string) => void;
  isAdmin?: boolean;
}

export const UserCard: React.FC<UserCardProps> = ({
  user,
  onEdit,
  isAdmin = false,
}) => {
  return (
    <div className="user-card">
      <h3>{user.name}</h3>
      <p>{user.email}</p>
      {isAdmin && (
        <Button onClick={() => onEdit(user.id)}>
          Editar
        </Button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

### 3.3 API Controllers
```typescript
// Controller com validação Zod e tratamento de erros
import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { prisma } from '../lib/prisma';
import { logger } from '../lib/logger';

const createUserSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  name: z.string().min(2),
  password: z.string().min(8),
});

export const createUser = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    // Validação
    const validatedData = createUserSchema.parse(req.body);
    
    // Lógica de negócio
    const user = await prisma.user.create({
      data: {
        ...validatedData,
        passwordHash: await hashPassword(validatedData.password),
      },
    });
    
    // Logging
    logger.info(`User created: ${user.id}`);
    
    // Resposta
    res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name,
      },
    });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof z.ZodError) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        errors: error.errors,
      });
    }
    
    logger.error('Error creating user:', error);
    res.status(500).json({
      success: false,
      message: 'Internal server error',
    });
  }
};
```

### 3.4 Testes
```typescript
// Teste unitário com Vitest
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { UserCard } from './UserCard';

describe('UserCard', () => {
  const mockUser = {
    id: '1',
    name: 'John Doe',
    email: 'john@example.com',
  };

  it('renders user information correctly', () => {
    render(<UserCard user={mockUser} onEdit={vi.fn()} />);
    
    expect(screen.getByText('John Doe')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByText('john@example.com')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('calls onEdit when edit button is clicked', () => {
    const onEditMock = vi.fn();
    render(<UserCard user={mockUser} onEdit={onEditMock} isAdmin />);
    
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByText('Editar'));
    expect(onEditMock).toHaveBeenCalledWith('1');
  });
});
```

## 4. Fluxo CI/CD

### 4.1 Pipeline GitHub Actions
```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
        
      - name: Run linting
        run: npm run lint
        
      - name: Run type check
        run: npm run type-check
        
      - name: Run unit tests
        run: npm run test:unit
        
      - name: Run integration tests
        run: npm run test:integration
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql://test:test@localhost:5432/test
          
      - name: Build applications
        run: npm run build

  deploy-staging:
    needs: test
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Deploy to Staging
        run: |
          echo "Deploying to staging environment"
          # Implementar deploy para staging
          
  deploy-production:
    needs: test
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Deploy to Production
        run: |
          echo "Deploying to production with zero-downtime"
          # Implementar blue-green deployment
```

### 4.2 Estratégia de Deploy
- **Blue-Green Deployment**: Zero downtime
- **Feature Flags**: Rollout progressivo de features
- **Health Checks**: Verificação automática de saúde
- **Rollback Automático**: Reversão em caso de falha

## 5. Configurações Essenciais

### 5.1 Docker Compose (Desenvolvimento)
```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp_password
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_dev
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    
  api:
    build:
      context: ./apps/api
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:diyapp_password@postgres:5432/diyapp_dev
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
    volumes:
      - ./apps/api:/app
      - /app/node_modules
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
      
  web:
    build:
      context: ./apps/web
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./apps/web:/app
      - /app/node_modules
    depends_on:
      - api

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

### 5.2 Configuração Vite
```typescript
// apps/web/vite.config.ts
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@components': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/components'),
      '@pages': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/pages'),
      '@services': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/services'),
    },
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    proxy: {
      '/api': {
        target: 'http://localhost:3001',
        changeOrigin: true,
      },
    },
  },
  build: {
    outDir: 'dist',
    sourcemap: true,
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          ui: ['@mui/material', '@mui/icons-material', '@emotion/react'],
        },
      },
    },
  },
});
```

### 5.3 Configuração Express
```typescript
// apps/api/src/app.ts
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import compression from 'compression';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import { errorHandler } from './middleware/errorHandler';
import { requestLogger } from './middleware/logger';
import apiRoutes from './routes';
import { config } from './config';

const app = express();

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors(config.cors));
app.use(compression());

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
});
app.use('/api/', limiter);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Request logging
app.use(requestLogger);

// API routes
app.use('/api/v1', apiRoutes);

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({ status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
});

// Error handling
app.use(errorHandler);

export default app;
```

## 6. ADR (Architecture Decision Record) - V12 Core

### ADR-001: Escolha do Stack Tecnológico
**Data**: 2024-01-15
**Status**: Aceita

**Contexto**: Necessidade de uma arquitetura moderna, escalável e com forte tipagem para o DIYAPP V12.

**Decisão**: Adotar React 18 + TypeScript no frontend e Node.js 20 + TypeScript no backend, com PostgreSQL como banco principal.

**Opções Consideradas**:
- **Opção A**: React + TypeScript + Node.js + PostgreSQL
- **Opção B**: Vue 3 + TypeScript + NestJS + MongoDB
- **Opção C**: SvelteKit + PostgreSQL

**Justificativa**: React tem maior ecossistema e comunidade, TypeScript garante type safety, Node.js é maduro para APIs, PostgreSQL é relacional robusto com extensões úteis.

**Consequências**:
- Positivas: Type safety, grande comunidade, extensibilidade
- Negativas: Curva de aprendizado para TypeScript, overhead de configuração

### ADR-002: Estrutura Monorepo
**Data**: 2024-01-15
**Status**: Aceita

**Contexto**: Necessidade de compartilhar código entre frontend e backend com versionamento consistente.

**Decisão**: Adotar Turborepo como gerenciador de monorepo.

**Consequências**:
- Positivas: Compartilhamento de tipos, CI/CD unificado, dependências consistentes
- Negativas: Complexidade inicial, build times maiores sem cache adequado

## 7. Critérios de Aceite para Arquitetura V12

### ✅ Aprovado pelo PM
- [x] Escopo definido e estimável
- [x] ROI claro (6 meses)
- [x] Riscos mitigados

### ✅ Aprovado pelo PO

- [x] Fluxos de usuário suportados

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo para o DIYAPP V12, incluindo paleta de cores, tipografia, componentes de UI e wireframes interativos para as 5 views principais. Como não posso criar um protótipo Figma real, vou implementar um sistema de design funcional em HTML/CSS/JS que simula todas as funcionalidades.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-design-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── style.css              # Design System completo
├── design-system.js       # Componentes interativos
├── views/                 # Views principais
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── editor.html
│   ├── settings.html
│   ├── logs.html
│   └── admin.html
└── assets/
    ├── icons/
    └── fonts/
```

## 1. index.html - Dashboard Principal

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

Vou provisionar um ambiente completo com Terraform e Docker, configurando containers para aplicação, banco de dados, Redis, load balancer e métricas de saúde.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   └── terraform.tfvars.example
├── docker/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── app/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── nginx/
│   │   ├── Dockerfile
│   │   └── nginx.conf
│   └── prometheus/
│       └── prometheus.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   └── monitor.sh
├── .env.example
└── README.md
```

## 1. Arquivos Terraform

### `terraform/main.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0"
  required_providers {
    docker = {
      source  = "kreuzwerker/docker"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
  }
}

provider "docker" {
  host = "unix:///var/run/docker.sock"
}

# Network para os containers
resource "docker_network" "diyapp_network" {
  name     = "diyapp-network"
  driver   = "bridge"
  internal = false

  ipam_config {
    subnet  = "172.20.0.0/16"
    gateway = "172.20.0.1"
  }
}

# Volume para PostgreSQL
resource "docker_volume" "postgres_data" {
  name = "postgres-data"
}

# Volume para Redis
resource "docker_volume" "redis_data" {
  name = "redis-data"
}

# Container PostgreSQL
resource "docker_container" "postgres" {
  name  = "diyapp-postgres"
  image = "postgres:15-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  env = [
    "POSTGRES_DB=${var.postgres_db}",
    "POSTGRES_USER=${var.postgres_user}",
    "POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${var.postgres_password}"
  ]

  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.postgres_data.name
    container_path = "/var/lib/postgresql/data"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.10"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${var.postgres_user}"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "40s"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 5432
    external = 5432
  }
}

# Container Redis
resource "docker_container" "redis" {
  name  = "diyapp-redis"
  image = "redis:7-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  command = ["redis-server", "--appendonly", "yes"]

  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.redis_data.name
    container_path = "/data"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.20"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "10s"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 6379
    external = 6379
  }
}

# Container da Aplicação DIYAPP
resource "docker_image" "diyapp" {
  name = "diyapp:v12"
  build {
    context = "${path.module}/../docker/app"
    tag     = ["diyapp:v12"]
  }
}

resource "docker_container" "diyapp" {
  name  = "diyapp-application"
  image = docker_image.diyapp.latest
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  env = [
    "NODE_ENV=staging",
    "DATABASE_URL=postgresql://${var.postgres_user}:${var.postgres_password}@diyapp-postgres:5432/${var.postgres_db}",
    "REDIS_URL=redis://diyapp-redis:6379",
    "APP_PORT=3000",
    "LOG_LEVEL=info"
  ]

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.30"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "60s"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3000
  }

  depends_on = [
    docker_container.postgres,
    docker_container.redis
  ]
}

# Container Nginx (Load Balancer)
resource "docker_image" "nginx" {
  name = "diyapp-nginx:latest"
  build {
    context = "${path.module}/../docker/nginx"
    tag     = ["diyapp-nginx:latest"]
  }
}

resource "docker_container" "nginx" {
  name  = "diyapp-nginx"
  image = docker_image.nginx.latest
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.40"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 80
    external = 8080
  }

  ports {
    internal = 443
    external = 8443
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:80/health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }

  depends_on = [docker_container.diyapp]
}

# Container Prometheus (Monitoramento)
resource "docker_container" "prometheus" {
  name  = "diyapp-prometheus"
  image = "prom/prometheus:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  volumes {
    host_path      = "${path.module}/../docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
    container_path = "/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.50"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 9090
    external = 9090
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:9090/-/healthy"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }
}

# Container Grafana (Dashboard)
resource "docker_container" "grafana" {
  name  = "diyapp-grafana"
  image = "grafana/grafana:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  env = [
    "GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${var.grafana_password}"
  ]

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.60"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3001
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/api/health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`
```hcl
variable "postgres_db" {
  description = "Nome do banco de dados PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp"
}

variable "postgres_user" {
  description = "Usuário do PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_user"
}

variable "postgres_password" {
  description = "Senha do PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "grafana_password" {
  description = "Senha do admin do Grafana"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Ambiente de deploy"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
}
```

### `terraform/outputs.tf`
```hcl
output "application_url" {
  description = "URL da aplicação"
  value       = "http://localhost:8080"
}

output "database_url" {
  description = "URL do banco de dados"
  value       = "postgresql://${var.postgres_user}:****@localhost:5432/${var.postgres_db}"
  sensitive   = true
}

output "monitoring_urls" {
  description = "URLs de monitoramento"
  value = {
    prometheus = "http://localhost:9090"
    grafana    = "http://localhost:3001"
  }
}

output "container_status" {
  description = "Status dos containers"
  value = {
    postgres   = docker_container.postgres.status
    redis      = docker_container.redis.status
    diyapp     = docker_container.diyapp.status
    nginx      = docker_container.nginx.status
    prometheus = docker_container.prometheus.status
    grafana    = docker_container.grafana.status
  }
}
```

### `terraform/terraform.tfvars.example`
```hcl
postgres_password = "sua_senha_segura_aqui"
grafana_password  = "admin123"
environment       = "staging"
```

## 2. Arquivos Docker

### `docker/docker-compose.yml` (Alternativa ao Terraform)
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: ${POSTGRES_DB:-diyapp}
      POSTGRES_USER: ${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  app:
    build:
      context: ./app
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-application
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: ${NODE_ENV:-staging}
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/${POSTGRES_DB:-diyapp}
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      APP_PORT: 3000
      LOG_LEVEL: info
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 60s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  nginx:
    build:
      context: ./nginx
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "8080:80"
      - "8443:443"
    depends_on:
      - app
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:80/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:9090/-/healthy"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin123}
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16
          gateway: 172.20.0.1
```

### `docker/app/Dockerfile`
```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código da aplicação
COPY . .

# Expor porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check endpoint
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=60s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "server.js"]
```

### `docker/nginx/Dockerfile`
```dockerfile
FROM nginx:alpine

# Copiar configuração customizada
COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost/health || exit 1

EXPOSE 80 443
```

### `docker/nginx/nginx.conf`
```nginx
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream diyapp_backend {
        server diyapp-application:3000;
        server diyapp-application:3000 backup;
    }

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name localhost;

        # Health check endpoint
        location /health {
            access_log off;
            return 200 "healthy\n";
            add_header Content-Type text/plain;
        }

        # Métricas do nginx
        location /nginx_status {
            stub_status on;
            access_log off;
            allow 127.0.0.1;
            allow 172.20.0.0/16;
            deny all;
        }

        # Proxy para aplicação
        location / {
            proxy_pass http://diyapp_backend;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            
            # Timeouts
            proxy_connect_timeout 5s;
            proxy_send_timeout 60s;
            proxy_read_timeout 60s;
            
            # Buffers
            proxy_buffer_size 128k;
            proxy_buffers 4 256k;
            proxy_busy_buffers_size 256k;
        }

        # Logging
        access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log combined;
        error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log warn;
    }
}
```

### `docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml`
```yaml
global:
  scrape_interval: 30s
  evaluation_interval: 30s

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'diyapp'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['diyapp-application:3000']
    metrics_path: '/metrics'
    scrape_interval: 30s

  - job_name: 'postgres'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['postgres:5432']
    metrics_path: '/

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Camada de API Core

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── src/
│   ├── config/
│   │   ├── database.js
│   │   ├── jwt.js
│   │   └── logger.js
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── auth.controller.js
│   │   └── projects.controller.js
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── auth.js
│   │   ├── errorHandler.js
│   │   └── validation.js
│   ├── models/

## 2. Configuração do Logger (Winston)

### src/config/logger.js
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const path = require('path');

const logFormat = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.timestamp(),
  winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
  winston.format.json()
);

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: logFormat,
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-api' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(__dirname, '../../logs/error.log'), 
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(__dirname, '../../logs/combined.log'),
      maxsize: 5242880,
      maxFiles: 5
    })
  ]
});

if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize(),
      winston.format.simple()
    )
  }));
}

// Função para mascarar dados sensíveis
const maskSensitiveData = (data) => {
  if (!data) return data;
  
  const masked = { ...data };
  const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'email', 'cpf', 'credit_card', 'card_number'];
  
  sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
    if (masked[field]) {
      masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return masked;
};

// Middleware de logging para requests
const requestLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
  
  // Adiciona correlation ID ao request
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    
    const logData = {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration_ms: duration,
      user_agent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip
    };
    
    // Adiciona user_id se autenticado
    if (req.userId) {
      logData.user_id = req.userId;
    }
    
    // Log baseado no status code
    if (res.statusCode >= 400) {
      logger.error('HTTP Request Error', logData);
    } else {
      logger.info('HTTP Request', logData);
    }
  });
  
  next();
};

module.exports = { logger, requestLogger, maskSensitiveData };
```

## 3. Configuração do Banco de Dados (SQLite)

### src/config/database.js
```javascript
const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose();
const path = require('path');
const { logger } = require('./logger');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.dbPath = process.env.DATABASE_PATH || './database/diyapp.db';
    this.db = null;
  }

  async connect() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db = new sqlite3.Database(this.dbPath, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database connection failed', { 
            error: err.message,
            path: this.dbPath 
          });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        
        logger.info('Database connected successfully', { path: this.dbPath });
        
        // Habilitar foreign keys
        this.db.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON');
        
        // Configurar timeout para queries
        this.db.configure('busyTimeout', 5000);
        
        resolve(this.db);
      });
    });
  }

  async query(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.all(sql, params, (err, rows) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database query error', { 
            error: err.message,
            sql,
            params: this.maskParams(params)
          });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve(rows);
      });
    });
  }

  async run(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.run(sql, params, function(err) {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database run error', { 
            error: err.message,
            sql,
            params: this.maskParams(params)
          });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve({ id: this.lastID, changes: this.changes });
      });
    });
  }

  async get(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.get(sql, params, (err, row) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database get error', { 
            error: err.message,
            sql,
            params: this.maskParams(params)
          });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve(row);
      });
    });
  }

  // Mascarar parâmetros sensíveis para logs
  maskParams(params) {
    if (!Array.isArray(params)) return params;
    
    const sensitivePatterns = [/password/i, /token/i, /email/i, /cpf/i, /card/i];
    
    return params.map(param => {
      if (typeof param === 'string' && sensitivePatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(param))) {
        return '***MASKED***';
      }
      return param;
    });
  }

  async beginTransaction() {
    return this.run('BEGIN TRANSACTION');
  }

  async commit() {
    return this.run('COMMIT');
  }

  async rollback() {
    return this.run('ROLLBACK');
  }

  async close() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.close((err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database close error', { error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        logger.info('Database connection closed');
        resolve();
      });
    });
  }

  // Migrações
  async migrate() {
    try {
      await this.beginTransaction();
      
      // Tabela de usuários
      await this.run(`
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
          id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
          email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
          username TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
          password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
          full_name TEXT,
          created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1
        )
      `);
      
      // Tabela de projetos
      await this.run(`
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (
          id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
          user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
          title TEXT NOT NULL,
          description TEXT,
          status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft',
          category TEXT,
          estimated_hours INTEGER,
          actual_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
          materials JSON,
          steps JSON,
          images TEXT,
          created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          completed_at DATETIME,
          FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE
        )
      `);
      
      // Índices para performance
      await this.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_user_id ON projects(user_id)');
      await this.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_status ON projects(status)');
      await this.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_email ON users(email)');
      
      await this.commit();
      logger.info('Database migrations completed successfully');
      
    } catch (error) {
      await this.rollback();
      logger.error('Migration failed', { error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Rollback das migrações (para desenvolvimento)
  async rollbackMigrations() {
    try {
      await this.beginTransaction();
      
      await this.run('DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_projects_user_id');
      await this.run('DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_projects_status');
      await this.run('DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_users_email');
      await this.run('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS projects');
      await this.run('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users');
      
      await this.commit();
      logger.info('Database rollback completed successfully');
      
    } catch (error) {
      await this.rollback();
      logger.error('Rollback failed', { error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

// Singleton pattern para garantir uma única conexão
const database = new Database();

// Inicialização automática em desenvolvimento
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
  database.connect().then(async () => {
    await database.migrate();
  }).catch(err => {
    logger.error('Database initialization failed', { error: err.message });
  });
}

module.exports = database;
```

## 4. Configuração JWT

### src/config/jwt.js
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { logger } = require('./logger');

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your_super_secret_jwt_key_change_in_production';
const JWT_EXPIRES_IN = process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h';

class JWTService {
  generateToken(payload, expiresIn = JWT_EXPIRES_IN) {
    try {
      const token = jwt.sign(payload, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn });
      
      logger.debug('JWT token generated', { 
        user_id: payload.userId,
        expires_in: expiresIn 
      });
      
      return token;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('JWT generation failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        payload: this.maskPayload(payload)
      });
      throw new Error('Token generation failed');
    }
  }

  verifyToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      
      logger.debug('JWT token verified', { 
        user_id: decoded.userId 
      });
      
      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn('JWT verification failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        token: token ? '***MASKED***' : null
      });
      
      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        throw new Error('Token expired');
      }
      if (error.name === 'JsonWebTokenError') {
        throw new Error('Invalid token');
      }
      throw new Error('Token verification failed');
    }
  }

  decodeToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.decode(token);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('JWT decode failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        token: token ? '***MASKED***' : null
      });
      return null;
    }
  }

  // Mascarar payload sensível para logs
  maskPayload(payload) {
    if (!payload) return payload;
    
    const masked = { ...payload };
    if (masked.password) {
      masked.password = '***MASKED***';
    }
    return masked;
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTService();
```

## 5. Modelos

### src/models/User.js
```javascript
const database = require('../config/database');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const { logger, maskSensitiveData } = require('../config/logger');

class User {
  constructor(data) {
    this.id = data.id;
    this.email = data.email;
    this.username = data.username;
    this.password_hash = data.password_hash;
    this.full_name = data.full_name;
    this.created_at = data.created_at;
    this.updated_at = data.updated_at;
    this.is_active = data.is_active;
  }

  static async create(userData) {
    try {
      // Hash da senha
      const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(10);
      const password_hash = await bcrypt.hash(userData.password, salt);
      
      const result = await database.run(
        `INSERT INTO users (email, username, password_hash, full_name) 
         VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)`,
        [userData.email, userData.username, password_hash, userData.full_name]
      );
      
      logger.info('User created successfully', { 
        user_id: result.id,
        email: userData.email 
      });
      
      return result.id;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('User creation failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        user_data: maskSensitiveData(userData)
      });
      
      if (error.message.includes('UNIQUE constraint failed')) {
        throw new Error('Email or username already exists');
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  static async findByEmail(email) {
    try {
      const user = await database.get(
        'SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ? AND is_active = 1',
        [email]
      );
      
      return user ? new User(user) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Find user by email failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        email: email ? '***MASKED***' : null
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  static async findById(id) {
    try {
      const user = await database.get(
        'SELECT id, email, username, full_name, created_at, updated_at FROM users WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1',
        [id]
      );
      
      return user ? new User(user) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Find user by id failed', { 
        error: error.message,
        user_id: id 
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  static async update(id, updateData) {
    try {
      const fields = [];
      const values = [];
      
      if (updateData.full_name !== undefined) {
        fields.push('full_name = ?');
        values.push(updateData.full_name);
      }
      
      if (updateData.password) {
        const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(10);
        const password_hash = await bcrypt.hash(updateData.password, salt);
        fields.push('password_hash

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Boilerplate React

Vou criar um boilerplate React profissional com todas as configurações necessárias para atender aos critérios de performance (Lighthouse >90) e seguir os padrões estabelecidos.

## 3. Configuração Vite (vite.config.ts)

```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import { VitePWA } from 'vite-plugin-pwa';
import compression from 'vite-plugin-compression';
import { resolve } from 'path';

// https://vitejs.dev/config/
export default defineConfig(({ mode }) => ({
  plugins: [
    react(),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      ext: '.gz',
    }),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'brotliCompress',
      ext: '.br',
    }),
    VitePWA({
      registerType: 'autoUpdate',
      includeAssets: ['favicon.ico', 'robots.txt', 'apple-touch-icon.png'],
      manifest: {
        name: 'DIYAPP V12 Core',
        short_name: 'DIYAPP',
        description: 'DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core Application',
        theme_color: '#1a1a2e',
        background_color: '#0f0f1a',
        display: 'standalone',
        orientation: 'portrait',
        scope: '/',
        start_url: '/',
        icons: [
          {
            src: '/icon-192x192.png',
            sizes: '192x192',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
          {
            src: '/icon-512x512.png',
            sizes: '512x512',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
          {
            src: '/icon-512x512.png',
            sizes: '512x512',
            type: 'image/png',
            purpose: 'any maskable',
          },
        ],
      },
    }),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': resolve(__dirname, 'src'),
      '@components': resolve(__dirname, 'src/components'),
      '@pages': resolve(__dirname, 'src/pages'),
      '@hooks': resolve(__dirname, 'src/hooks'),
      '@stores': resolve(__dirname, 'src/stores'),
      '@services': resolve(__dirname, 'src/services'),
      '@utils': resolve(__dirname, 'src/utils'),
      '@styles': resolve(__dirname, 'src/styles'),
      '@types': resolve(__dirname, 'src/types'),
    },
  },
  build: {
    target: 'es2020',
    minify: 'terser',
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: mode === 'production',
        drop_debugger: mode === 'production',
      },
    },
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          ui: ['zustand', 'clsx', 'date-fns'],
        },
        chunkFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        entryFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: 'assets/[ext]/[name]-[hash].[ext]',
      },
    },
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1000,
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
  },
  preview: {
    port: 3001,
    host: true,
  },
}));

## 4. Sistema de Design (Design System Tokens)

### `src/styles/design-tokens.css`

```css
:root {
  /* Colors - Primary */
  --color-primary-50: #f0f9ff;
  --color-primary-100: #e0f2fe;
  --color-primary-200: #bae6fd;
  --color-primary-300: #7dd3fc;
  --color-primary-400: #38bdf8;
  --color-primary-500: #0ea5e9;
  --color-primary-600: #0284c7;
  --color-primary-700: #0369a1;

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Documento de Arquitetura

## 1. Visão Geral da Arquitetura V12

### 1.1 Princípios Fundamentais
- **Autonomia Total**: Cada componente deve funcionar independentemente com fallbacks
- **Resiliência**: Sistema deve se recuperar automaticamente de falhas
- **Observabilidade**: Métricas, logs e traces em todos os níveis
- **Segurança por Design**: Zero-trust, validação em todas as camadas
- **Escalabilidade Horizontal**: Stateless por padrão, sharding inteligente

### 1.2 Stack Tecnológica Principal

#### Frontend
- **Framework**: React 18 + TypeScript
- **Build Tool**: Vite 5.x
- **UI Library**: Chakra UI 2.x (acessibilidade por padrão)
- **State Management**: Zustand (leve) + React Query (server state)
- **Routing**: React Router DOM 6.x
- **Form Handling**: React Hook Form + Zod (validação)
- **Testing**: Vitest + React Testing Library + Playwright (E2E)

#### Backend
- **Runtime**: Node.js 20.x (LTS)
- **Framework**: Express.js 5.x + TypeScript
- **API**: RESTful + GraphQL (Apollo Server) para queries complexas
- **Validation**: Zod com transformação automática
- **Authentication**: JWT + Refresh Tokens + OAuth2.0
- **Rate Limiting**: Redis-based com sliding window
- **Job Queue**: BullMQ com Redis

#### Banco de Dados
- **Primário**: PostgreSQL 16.x (transacional)
- **Cache**: Redis 7.x (sessões, rate limiting, filas)
- **Search**: Elasticsearch 8.x (busca full-text)
- **Object Storage**: MinIO (S3-compatible) para arquivos

#### Infraestrutura
- **Container**: Docker + Docker Compose (dev)
- **Orquestração**: Kubernetes (produção)
- **Service Mesh**: Istio (produção enterprise)
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions + ArgoCD (GitOps)
- **Monitoring**: Prometheus + Grafana + Loki
- **Logging**: ELK Stack (Elasticsearch, Logstash, Kibana)
- **Tracing**: Jaeger

## 2. Estrutura de Pastas

```

## 3. Padrões de Código

### 3.1 TypeScript
```typescript
// Nomenclatura
interface UserDTO {}              // Data Transfer Object
type UserResponse = {}           // Tipo de resposta
class ValidationError extends Error {} // Errors customizados
const MAX_RETRIES = 3;           // Constantes em UPPER_SNAKE_CASE

// Exemplo de service pattern
export class UserService {
  constructor(private userRepository: IUserRepository) {}
  
  async createUser(data: CreateUserDTO): Promise<UserResponse> {
    // Validação com Zod
    const validatedData = createUserSchema.parse(data);
    
    // Lógica de negócio
    const user = await this.userRepository.create(validatedData);
    
    // Transformação para resposta
    return this.toResponse(user);
  }
  
  private toResponse(user: User): UserResponse {
    return {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      // Nunca expor senhas
    };
  }
}
```

### 3.2 React Components
```tsx
// Componente funcional com TypeScript
interface UserCardProps {
  user: User;
  onEdit?: (id: string) => void;
  isLoading?: boolean;
}

export const UserCard: React.FC<UserCardProps> = ({
  user,
  onEdit,
  isLoading = false,
}) => {
  // Hooks no topo
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);
  
  // Handler functions
  const handleEdit = useCallback(() => {
    if (onEdit) {
      onEdit(user.id);
    }
  }, [onEdit, user.id]);
  
  // Render condicional
  if (isLoading) {
    return <Skeleton height="100px" />;
  }
  
  return (
    <Box borderWidth="1px" borderRadius="lg" p={4}>
      <Flex justify="space-between" align="center">
        <Heading size="md">{user.name}</Heading>
        <IconButton
          aria-label="Edit user"
          icon={<EditIcon />}
          onClick={handleEdit}
          size="sm"
        />
      </Flex>
      {/* ... */}
    </Box>
  );
};

// Prop Types com Zod (runtime validation)
const userCardPropsSchema = z.object({
  user: userSchema,
  onEdit: z.function().optional(),
  isLoading: z.boolean().default(false),
});
```

### 3.3 API Design
```typescript
// RESTful com versionamento
// GET /api/v1/users
// POST /api/v1/users
// PUT /api/v1/users/:id
// DELETE /api/v1/users/:id

// Response padrão
interface ApiResponse<T> {
  success: boolean;
  data?: T;
  error?: {
    code: string;
    message: string;
    details?: unknown;
  };
  meta?: {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    total: number;
  };
}

// Error handling centralizado
app.use((err: Error, req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  if (err instanceof ValidationError) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: {
        code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
        message: err.message,
        details: err.details,
      },
    });
  }
  
  // Log error interno
  logger.error('Unhandled error', { error: err, path: req.path });
  
  res.status(500).json({
    success: false,
    error: {
      code: 'INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR',
      message: 'An unexpected error occurred',
    },
  });
});
```

## 4. Fluxo CI/CD

### 4.1 GitHub Actions Workflow
```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '20.x'
          cache: 'npm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
        
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
        
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
        
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm run test:unit
        
      - name: Integration tests
        run: npm run test:integration
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql://test:test@localhost:5432/test
          
      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
        
      - name: Security scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
          
  e2e-tests:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:16
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: test
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - run: npm run test:e2e
```

### 4.2 CD Pipeline (GitOps)
```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
    
jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Build and push Docker images
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: |
            ${{ secrets.REGISTRY }}/diyapp-web:${{ github.sha }}
            ${{ secrets.REGISTRY }}/diyapp-api:${{ github.sha }}
            
      - name: Update K8s manifests
        run: |
          sed -i "s|IMAGE_TAG|${{ github.sha }}|g" infrastructure/k8s/deployment.yaml
          
      - name: Deploy to staging
        uses: argo-cd/actions/deploy@v1
        with:
          argocd-server: ${{ secrets.ARGOCD_SERVER }}
          argocd-token: ${{ secrets.ARGOCD_TOKEN }}
          manifest-file: infrastructure/k8s/deployment.yaml
          
  deploy-production:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: deploy-staging
    environment: production
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    steps:
      - name: Approve production deployment
        uses: trstringer/manual-approval@v1
        with:
          secret: ${{ github.TOKEN }}
          approvers: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_APPROVERS }}
          
      - name: Deploy to production
        uses: argo-cd/actions/deploy@v1
        with:
          argocd-server: ${{ secrets.ARGOCD_SERVER }}
          argocd-token: ${{ secrets.ARGOCD_TOKEN }}
          manifest-file: infrastructure/k8s/production.yaml
```

## 5. Configuração Docker

```dockerfile
# Dockerfile para API
FROM node:20-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .
RUN npm run build

FROM node:20-alpine AS runner

WORKDIR /app

RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs
RUN adduser -S diyapp -u 1001

COPY --from=builder --chown=diyapp:nodejs /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder --chown=diyapp:nodejs /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --chown=diyapp:nodejs package.json ./

USER diyapp

EXPOSE 3000

ENV NODE_ENV=production
ENV PORT=3000

CMD ["node", "dist/server.js"]
```

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp123
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes

  api:
    build:
      context: ./apps/api
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      DATABASE_URL: postgres://diyapp:diyapp123@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      NODE_ENV: development
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    volumes:
      - ./apps/api:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  web:
    build:
      context: ./apps/web
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    ports:
      - "5173:5173"
    environment:
      VITE_API_URL: http://localhost:3000/api/v1
    depends_on:
      - api
    volumes:
      - ./apps/web:/app
      - /app/node_modules

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
```

## 6. Monitoramento e Observabilidade

### 6.1 Logging Estruturado
```typescript
// Winston logger config
import winston from 'winston';

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-api' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' }),
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      ),
    }),
  ],
});

// Uso no código
logger.info('User created', { userId: user.id, email: user.email });
logger.error('Database connection failed', { error: err.message });
```

### 6.2 Métricas com Prometheus
```typescript
import client from 'prom-client';

const collectDefaultMetrics = client.collectDefaultMetrics;
collectDefaultMetrics({ prefix: 'diyapp_' });

// Métricas customizadas
export

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo para o DIYAPP V12, incluindo paleta de cores, tipografia, componentes de UI e wireframes de alta fidelidade para as 5 views principais. Como não posso criar um protótipo Figma diretamente, vou criar um sistema de design funcional em HTML/CSS/JS que simula todas as funcionalidades e estados.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Design System</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <style>
        /* ===== RESET & BASE STYLES ===== */
        :root {
            /* ===== COLOR TOKENS ===== */
            /* Primary Colors */
            --color-primary-50: #f0f9ff;
            --color-primary-100: #e0f2fe;
            --color-primary-200: #bae6fd;
            --color-primary-300: #7dd3fc;
            --color-primary-400: #38bdf8;

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   └── terraform.tfvars.example
├── docker/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── app/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── nginx/
│   │   └── nginx.conf
│   └── prometheus/
│       └── prometheus.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   └── monitor.sh
├── monitoring/
│   ├── grafana-dashboards/
│   │   └── diyapp-dashboard.json
│   └── alerts/
│       └── alert-rules.yml
└── README.md
```

## 1. Arquivos Terraform

### `terraform/main.tf`

```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0"
  required_providers {
    docker = {
      source  = "kreuzwerker/docker"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
  }
}

provider "docker" {
  host = "unix:///var/run/docker.sock"
}

# Network para comunicação entre containers
resource "docker_network" "diyapp_network" {
  name   = "diyapp-network"
  driver = "bridge"
  
  ipam_config {
    subnet  = "172.20.0.0/16"
    gateway = "172.20.0.1"
  }
}

# Volume para PostgreSQL
resource "docker_volume" "postgres_data" {
  name = "postgres-data"
}

# Volume para Redis
resource "docker_volume" "redis_data" {
  name = "redis-data"
}

# Container PostgreSQL
resource "docker_container" "postgres" {
  name  = "diyapp-postgres"
  image = "postgres:15-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  
  env = [
    "POSTGRES_DB=diyapp",
    "POSTGRES_USER=diyapp_user",
    "POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${var.db_password}",
    "POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS=--encoding=UTF-8 --locale=C"
  ]
  
  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.postgres_data.name
    container_path = "/var/lib/postgresql/data"
  }
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.10"
  }
  
  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "40s"
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 5432
    external = 5432
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "database"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container Redis
resource "docker_container" "redis" {
  name  = "diyapp-redis"
  image = "redis:7-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  command = ["redis-server", "--appendonly", "yes", "--requirepass", var.redis_password]
  
  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.redis_data.name
    container_path = "/data"
  }
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.20"
  }
  
  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "redis-cli", "-a", var.redis_password, "ping"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 6379
    external = 6379
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "cache"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container da Aplicação
resource "docker_container" "app" {
  name  = "diyapp-application"
  image = "diyapp-app:${var.app_version}"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  
  env = [
    "NODE_ENV=${var.environment}",
    "DATABASE_URL=postgresql://diyapp_user:${var.db_password}@diyapp-postgres:5432/diyapp",
    "REDIS_URL=redis://:${var.redis_password}@diyapp-redis:6379",
    "PORT=3000",
    "LOG_LEVEL=info",
    "HEALTH_CHECK_PATH=/health",
    "METRICS_PATH=/metrics"
  ]
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.30"
  }
  
  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "60s"
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3000
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "application"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
    "com.diyapp.version" = var.app_version
  }
  
  depends_on = [
    docker_container.postgres,
    docker_container.redis
  ]
}

# Container Nginx (Load Balancer)
resource "docker_container" "nginx" {
  name  = "diyapp-nginx"
  image = "nginx:1.24-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  
  volumes {
    host_path      = "${path.module}/../docker/nginx/nginx.conf"
    container_path = "/etc/nginx/nginx.conf"
  }
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.40"
  }
  
  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "5s"
    retries  = 3
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 80
    external = 8080
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 443
    external = 8443
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "load-balancer"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
  
  depends_on = [
    docker_container.app
  ]
}

# Container Prometheus (Monitoring)
resource "docker_container" "prometheus" {
  name  = "diyapp-prometheus"
  image = "prom/prometheus:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  
  volumes {
    host_path      = "${path.module}/../docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
    container_path = "/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
  }
  
  volumes {
    volume_name    = "prometheus-data"
    container_path = "/prometheus"
  }
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.50"
  }
  
  command = [
    "--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml",
    "--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus",
    "--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries",
    "--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles",
    "--web.enable-lifecycle"
  ]
  
  ports {
    internal = 9090
    external = 9090
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "monitoring"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container Grafana (Visualização)
resource "docker_container" "grafana" {
  name  = "diyapp-grafana"
  image = "grafana/grafana:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  
  env = [
    "GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${var.grafana_password}",
    "GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel"
  ]
  
  volumes {
    volume_name    = "grafana-data"
    container_path = "/var/lib/grafana"
  }
  
  volumes {
    host_path      = "${path.module}/../monitoring/grafana-dashboards"
    container_path = "/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards"
  }
  
  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.60"
  }
  
  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3001
  }
  
  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "visualization"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`

```hcl
variable "environment" {
  description = "Ambiente de deploy (staging/production)"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
  
  validation {
    condition     = contains(["staging", "production"], var.environment)
    error_message = "Environment must be either 'staging' or 'production'."
  }
}

variable "app_version" {
  description = "Versão da aplicação Docker"
  type        = string
  default     = "v12.0.0"
}

variable "db_password" {
  description = "Senha do PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "redis_password" {
  description = "Senha do Redis"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "grafana_password" {
  description = "Senha do admin do Grafana"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
  default     = "Admin123!"
}

variable "replica_count" {
  description = "Número de réplicas da aplicação"
  type        = number
  default     = 2
}
```

// package.json

```javascript
// src/server.js
require('dotenv').config();
require('express-async-errors');
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');

const logger = require('./utils/logger');
const errorHandler = require('./middleware/error-handler');
const requestLogger = require('./middleware/request-logger');
const swaggerSpec = require('./docs/swagger');
const { initializeDatabase } = require('./database/connection');

const authRoutes = require('./routes/auth.routes');
const projectRoutes = require('./routes/project.routes');
const healthRoutes = require('./routes/health.routes');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting for public endpoints
const publicLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: { error: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Compression
app.use(compression());

// Request logging with correlation ID
app.use(requestLogger);

// Health endpoint (no auth, limited)
app.use('/health', publicLimiter, healthRoutes);

// Swagger documentation
app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerSpec));

// API Routes
app.use('/api/v1/auth', authRoutes);
app.use('/api/v1/projects', projectRoutes);

// 404 handler
app.use('*', (req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Route ${req.originalUrl} not found`,
    correlationId: req.correlationId
  });
});

// Global error handler
app.use(errorHandler);

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
  process.exit(0);
});

process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  logger.info('SIGINT received, shutting down gracefully');
  process.exit(0);
});

// Start server
const startServer = async () => {
  try {
    // Initialize database connection
    await initializeDatabase();
    
    // Run migrations in production
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
      const { runMigrations } = require('./database/migrations/run-migrations');
      await runMigrations();
    }
    
    app.listen(PORT, () => {
      logger.info(`Server running on port ${PORT} in ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'} mode`);
      logger.info(`API Documentation available at http://localhost:${PORT}/api-docs`);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
};

startServer();

module.exports = app; // For testing
```

```javascript
// src/utils/logger.js
const winston = require('winston');
const DailyRotateFile = require('winston-daily-rotate-file');

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors, colorize, printf } = winston.format;

// Custom format for console with colors
const consoleFormat = printf(({ level, message, timestamp, correlationId, userId, ...metadata }) => {
  let log = `${timestamp} [${correlationId || 'no-correlation-id'}] ${level}: ${message}`;
  
  if (userId) {
    log += ` | user: ${userId}`;
  }
  
  if (Object.keys(metadata).length > 0) {
    log += ` | metadata: ${JSON.stringify(metadata)}`;
  }
  
  return log;
});

// Create logger instance
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  defaultMeta: {
    service: 'diyapp-api'
  },
  format: combine(
    timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss.SSS' }),
    errors({ stack: true }),
    json()
  ),
  transports: [
    // Console transport
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: combine(
        colorize(),
        timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss.SSS' }),
        consoleFormat
      )
    }),
    // File transport for errors
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/error-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      level: 'error',
      maxSize: '20m',
      maxFiles: '30d'
    }),
    // File transport for all logs
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/combined-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      maxSize: '20m',
      maxFiles: '30d'
    })
  ],
  // Don't exit on handled exceptions
  exitOnError: false
});

// Mask sensitive data in logs
const maskSensitiveData = (data) => {
  if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;
  
  const masked = { ...data };
  const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'accessToken', 'refreshToken', 'authorization', 'cardNumber', 'cvv', 'cpf', 'email'];
  
  sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
    if (masked[field]) {
      masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return masked;
};

// Logging middleware helper
logger.middleware = (req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  
  // Log request
  logger.info('Incoming request', {
    correlationId: req.correlationId,
    method: req.method,
    url: req.originalUrl,
    userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
    ip: req.ip,
    userId: req.user?.id,
    body: maskSensitiveData(req.body),
    query: req.query,
    params: req.params
  });
  
  // Log response
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    
    logger.info('Request completed', {
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      durationMs: duration,
      userId: req.user?.id,
      contentLength: res.get('content-length')
    });
  });
  
  next();
};

module.exports = logger;
```

```javascript
// src/database/connection.js
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class DatabaseConnection {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
  }

  async connect() {
    if (this.pool) {
      return this.pool;
    }

    const config = {
      host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT || '5432'),
      database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp',
      user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || '',
      max: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_MAX || '20'),
      idleTimeoutMillis: parseInt(process.env.DB_IDLE_TIMEOUT || '30000'),
      connectionTimeoutMillis: parseInt(process.env.DB_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT || '5000'),
    };

    // Add SSL for production
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
      config.ssl = {
        rejectUnauthorized: false
      };
    }

    this.pool = new Pool(config);

    // Test connection
    try {
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      logger.info('Database connection established successfully');
      client.release();
      this.isConnected = true;
      
      // Handle connection errors
      this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
        logger.error('Unexpected database pool error:', err);
        this.isConnected = false;
      });
      
      return this.pool;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to connect to database:', error);
      this.pool = null;
      this.isConnected = false;
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    if (!this.pool) {
      await this.connect();
    }

    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Database query executed', {
        query: text,
        durationMs: duration,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Database query failed:', {
        query: text,
        error: error.message,
        code: error.code
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async getClient() {
    if (!this.pool) {
      await this.connect();
    }
    
    const client = await this.pool.connect();
    
    // Proxy the client to log queries
    const originalQuery = client.query;
    client.query = (...args) => {
      const start = Date.now();
      return originalQuery.apply(client, args).then(result => {
        const duration = Date.now() - start;
        logger.debug('Client query executed', {
          durationMs: duration,
          rowCount: result.rowCount
        });
        return result;
      }).catch(error => {
        logger.error('Client query failed:', error.message);
        throw error;
      });
    };
    
    return client;
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.pool) {
      await this.pool.end();
      this.pool = null;
      this.isConnected = false;
      logger.info('Database connection pool closed');
    }
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      isConnected: this.isConnected,
      totalCount: this.pool?.totalCount || 0,
      idleCount: this.pool?.idleCount || 0,
      waitingCount: this.pool?.waitingCount || 0
    };
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const db = new DatabaseConnection();

// Initialize database connection
const initializeDatabase = async () => {
  try {
    await db.connect();
    
    // Create tables if they don't exist (for development)
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
      await createTablesIfNotExist();
    }
    
    return db;
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to initialize database:', error);
    throw error;
  }
};

// Helper function to create tables (for development)
async function createTablesIfNotExist() {
  try {
    // Users table
    await db.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'user',
        is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
        last_login TIMESTAMP,
        created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      );
    `);

    // Projects table
    await db.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (
        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        description TEXT,
        status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'draft',
        metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
        version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
        is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
        tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
        created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      );
    `);

    // Project versions table
    await db.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS project_versions (
        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        version_number INTEGER NOT NULL,
        content JSONB NOT NULL,
        change_description TEXT,
        created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
        created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        UNIQUE(project_id, version_number)
      );
    `);

    // Refresh tokens table
    await db.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS refresh_tokens (
        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
        token VARCHAR(512) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
        expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
        is_revoked BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
        created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        INDEX idx_refresh_tokens_token (token),
        INDEX idx_refresh_tokens_user_id (user_id)
      );
    `);

    // Create indexes
    await db.query(`
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_email ON users(email);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_user_id ON projects(user_id);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_status ON projects(status);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_created_at ON projects(created_at);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_project_versions_project_id ON project_versions(project_id);
    `);

    logger.info('Database tables created/verified successfully');
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to create tables:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

module.exports = {
  db,
  initializeDatabase,
  getDatabase: () => db
};
```

```javascript
// src/database/migrations/run-migrations.js
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const { db } = require('../connection');

class MigrationManager {
  constructor() {
    this.migrations = [];
    this.migrationTableName = 'schema_migrations';
  }

  async init() {
    // Create migrations table if it doesn't exist
    await db.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ${this.migrationTableName} (
        id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
        name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
        applied_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      );
    `);
  }

  async getAppliedMigrations() {
    const result = await db.query(
      `SELECT name FROM ${this.migrationTableName} ORDER BY applied_at DESC`
    );
    return result.rows.map(row => row.name);
  }

  async runMigration(name, upSQL, downSQL) {
    const client = await db.getClient();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      
      // Check if migration already applied
      const checkResult = await client.query(
        `SELECT 1 FROM ${this.migrationTableName} WHERE name = $1`,
        [name]
      );
      
      if (checkResult.rows.length > 0) {
        logger.info(`Migration ${name} already applied, skipping`);
        await client.query('ROLLBACK');
        return;
      }
      
      // Run migration
      logger.info(`Applying migration: ${name}`);
      await client.query(upSQL);
      
      // Record migration
      await client.query(
        `INSERT INTO ${this.migrationTableName} (name) VALUES ($1)`,
        [name]
      );
      
      await client.query('COMMIT');
      logger.info(`Migration ${name} applied successfully`);
      
      // Store migration for rollback
      this.migrations.push({ name, upSQL, downSQL });
    } catch (error) {
      await client.query('ROLLBACK');
      logger.error(`Failed to apply migration ${name}:`, error);
      throw error;
    } finally {
      client.release();
    }
  }

  async rollbackMigration(name) {
    const client = await db.getClient();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      
      // Find migration
      const migration = this.migrations.find(m => m.name === name);
      if (!migration) {
        throw new Error(`Migration ${name} not found`);
      }
      
      // Run rollback
      logger.info(`Rolling back migration: ${name}`);
      await client.query(migration.downSQL);
      
      // Remove migration record
      await client.query(
        `DELETE FROM ${this.migrationTable

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Boilerplate React

Vou criar um boilerplate React profissional com foco em performance, seguindo os padrões estabelecidos no papel. O sistema será estruturado com React Router, Zustand para gerenciamento de estado e um Design System integrado.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── public/
│   ├── index.html
│   ├── favicon.ico
│   └── robots.txt
├── src/
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── ui/
│   │   │   ├── Button/
│   │   │   ├── Card/
│   │   │   ├── Input/
│   │   │   └── index.ts
│   │   └── layout/
