### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Documento de Arquitetura

## 1. Visão Geral da Arquitetura V12

### 1.1 Princípios Fundamentais
- **Autonomia Total**: Cada componente deve ser independente e resiliente
- **Zero Downtime**: Deploy contínuo sem interrupção de serviço
- **Observabilidade Nativa**: Monitoramento integrado em todos os níveis
- **Segurança por Design**: Autenticação, autorização e criptografia desde o início

### 1.2 Stack Tecnológico Principal

#### Frontend
- **Framework**: React 18 + TypeScript
- **Build Tool**: Vite 5.x
- **UI Library**: Material-UI v5 (MUI) + Emotion para estilos
- **State Management**: Zustand (leve) + React Query para server state
- **Routing**: React Router v6
- **Testing**: Vitest + React Testing Library + Playwright (E2E)

#### Backend
- **Runtime**: Node.js 20.x (LTS)
- **Framework**: Express.js 5.x + TypeScript
- **API**: RESTful + GraphQL (Apollo Server) para queries complexas
- **Validation**: Zod para schema validation
- **Authentication**: JWT + Refresh Tokens + OAuth2 para integrações
- **Rate Limiting**: express-rate-limit + Redis para distribuição

#### Banco de Dados
- **Primário**: PostgreSQL 16 (relacional)
- **Cache**: Redis 7.x (sessões, rate limiting, cache)
- **Busca**: Elasticsearch 8.x (full-text search)
- **Filas**: BullMQ (Redis-based job queues)

#### Infraestrutura
- **Containerização**: Docker + Docker Compose (dev/prod)
- **Orquestração**: Kubernetes (EKS/GKE) para produção
- **CI/CD**: GitHub Actions + ArgoCD (GitOps)
- **Monitoring**: Prometheus + Grafana + Loki (logs)
- **Tracing**: Jaeger (distributed tracing)

## 3. Padrões de Código

### 3.1 TypeScript
```typescript
// ✅ CORRETO - Interfaces explícitas, tipos estritos
interface User {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  name: string;
  createdAt: Date;
}

// ❌ EVITAR - any types
function processData(data: any) { ... }

// ✅ CORRETO - Generics quando apropriado
function createRepository<T extends BaseEntity>(): Repository<T> { ... }
```

### 3.2 Nomenclatura
- **Variáveis/Funções**: camelCase (`getUserById`, `isActive`)
- **Classes/Interfaces/Types**: PascalCase (`UserService`, `ApiResponse`)
- **Constantes**: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE (`API_ENDPOINT`, `MAX_RETRIES`)
- **Arquivos**: kebab-case (`user-controller.ts`, `auth-middleware.ts`)

### 3.3 Componentes React
```typescript
// Componente funcional com TypeScript
interface UserCardProps {
  user: User;
  onEdit?: (userId: string) => void;
  isLoading?: boolean;
}

export const UserCard: React.FC<UserCardProps> = ({
  user,
  onEdit,
  isLoading = false
}) => {
  if (isLoading) {
    return <UserCardSkeleton />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="user-card">
      <h3>{user.name}</h3>
      <p>{user.email}</p>
      {onEdit && (
        <button onClick={() => onEdit(user.id)}>
          Edit
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

### 3.4 API Controllers
```typescript
// Controller com tratamento de erros centralizado
@Controller('/api/v1/users')
export class UserController {
  constructor(private readonly userService: UserService) {}

  @Get(':id')
  async getUserById(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Res() res: Response
  ): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const user = await this.userService.findById(id);
      if (!user) {
        throw new NotFoundException('User not found');
      }
      res.json(ApiResponse.success(user));
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(
        error.message,
        error.status || HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR
      );
    }
  }
}
```

## 4. Fluxo CI/CD

### 4.1 Pipeline de Integração Contínua (GitHub Actions)
```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  pull_request:
    branches: [main, develop]
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
        
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
        
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
        
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm run test:unit
        
      - name: Integration tests
        run: npm run test:integration
        
      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
        
      - name: Security scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
          
  e2e-tests:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:16
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - run: npm run test:e2e
```

### 4.2 Pipeline de Deploy Contínuo
```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Build and push Docker images
        run: |
          docker build -t ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/frontend:${{ github.sha }} ./src/frontend
          docker build -t ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/backend:${{ github.sha }} ./src/backend
          docker push ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/frontend:${{ github.sha }}
          docker push ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/backend:${{ github.sha }}
          
      - name: Deploy to Kubernetes
        uses: azure/k8s-deploy@v1
        with:
          namespace: staging
          manifests: ./infrastructure/kubernetes/
          images: |
            ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/frontend:${{ github.sha }}
            ${{ secrets.DOCKER_REGISTRY }}/backend:${{ github.sha }}
            
      - name: Run smoke tests
        run: npm run test:smoke
        
  deploy-production:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: deploy-staging
    environment: production
    if: success()
    steps:
      - name: Promote to production
        uses: argoproj/actions-cli@v1
        with:
          command: app sync diyapp-production
          
      - name: Monitor deployment
        run: |
          # Health checks
          # Performance validation
          # Error rate monitoring
```

## 5. Estratégia de Banco de Dados

### 5.1 Migrações
```sql
-- scripts/db/migrations/001_create_users_table.sql
CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at);
```

### 5.2 Versionamento de API
```typescript
// Versionamento semântico na URL
// /api/v1/users
// /api/v2/users (quando houver breaking changes)

// Headers para content negotiation
Accept: application/vnd.diyapp.v1+json
Accept: application/vnd.diyapp.v2+json
```

### 6.1 Métricas Essenciais

# prometheus/prometheus.yml
scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'node-backend'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['backend:3000']
    metrics_path: '/metrics'
    
  - job_name: 'frontend'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['frontend:4173']
      
  - job_name: 'postgres'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['postgres-exporter:9187']
      
  - job_name: 'redis'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['redis-exporter:9121']
```

### 6.2 Logging Estruturado
```typescript
// src/backend/src/core/logging/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error' 
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log' 
    })
  ]
});

// Uso
logger.info('User logged in', { 
  userId: '123', 
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString() 
});

logger.error('Database connection failed', {
  error: error.message,
  stack: error.stack,
  database: 'primary'
});
```

## 7. Configuração Docker

```dockerfile
# src/backend/Dockerfile
FROM node:20-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .
RUN npm run build

FROM node:20-alpine

WORKDIR /app

COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/package.json ./

USER node

EXPOSE 3000

CMD ["node", "dist/server.js"]
```

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  backend:
    build: ./src/backend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp_user:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy

  frontend:
    build: ./src/frontend
    ports:
      - "4173:4173"
    environment:
      VITE_API_URL: http://localhost:3000/api/v1
    depends_on:
      - backend

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   └── terraform.tfvars.example
├── docker/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── app/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── nginx/
│   │   └── nginx.conf
│   └── prometheus/
│       └── prometheus.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   └── monitor.sh
├── monitoring/
│   ├── grafana/
│   │   └── dashboard.json
│   └── alerts/
│       └── alert-rules.yml
└── README.md
```

## 1. Docker Compose para Ambiente Local/Staging

### `docker/docker-compose.yml`

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de Dados PostgreSQL
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-ChangeMe123!}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init-db.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Cache Redis
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    command: redis-server --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-RedisPass123!}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Aplicação Principal
  app:
    build:
      context: ../app
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-app
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: staging
      DB_HOST: postgres
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: diyapp
      DB_USER: diyapp_user
      DB_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-ChangeMe123!}
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
      REDIS_PASSWORD: ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-RedisPass123!}
      APP_PORT: 3000
    volumes:
      - ../app:/usr/src/app
      - /usr/src/app/node_modules
      - app_logs:/var/log/diyapp
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 60s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    deploy:
      replicas: 3
      update_config:
        parallelism: 1
        delay: 10s
        order: start-first

  # Load Balancer Nginx
  nginx:
    image: nginx:1.24-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    ports:
      - "8080:80"
      - "8443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf
      - ./nginx/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl
      - nginx_logs:/var/log/nginx
    depends_on:
      - app
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Monitoramento Prometheus
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Grafana para Dashboards
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-GrafanaPass123!}
      GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS: grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/grafana/dashboard.json:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards/dashboard.json
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Node Exporter para métricas do sistema
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:latest
    container_name: diyapp-node-exporter
    volumes:
      - /proc:/host/proc:ro
      - /sys:/host/sys:ro
      - /:/rootfs:ro
    command:
      - '--path.procfs=/host/proc'
      - '--path.rootfs=/rootfs'
      - '--path.sysfs=/host/sys'
      - '--collector.filesystem.mount-points-exclude=^/(sys|proc|dev|host|etc)($$|/)'
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  app_logs:
    driver: local
  nginx_logs:
    driver: local
  prometheus_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16

### `docker/app/Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /usr/src/app

# Instalar dependências do sistema
RUN apk add --no-cache \
    curl \
    postgresql-client \
    tini

# Copiar package.json e instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código da aplicação
COPY . .

# Criar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S diyapp -u 1001 && \
    chown -R diyapp:nodejs /usr/src/app

USER diyapp

# Expor porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check endpoint
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=60s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Iniciar aplicação com tini para signal handling
ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]
CMD ["node", "server.js"]
```

### `docker/nginx/nginx.conf`

```nginx
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream app_servers {
        least_conn;
        server app:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
        server app:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
        server app:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
    }

    # Health check endpoint
    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name _;
        
        location /health {
            access_log off;
            add_header Content-Type application/json;
            return 200 '{"status":"healthy","timestamp":"$time_iso8601"}';
        }
    }

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name staging.diyapp.local;

        # Rate limiting
        limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=api:10m rate=10r/s;
        
        # Headers de segurança
        add_header X-Frame-Options DENY;
        add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;
        add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block";

        # Logs
        access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log json;
        error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log warn;

        # Health check para load balancer
        location /lb-health {
            access_log off;
            add_header Content-Type application/json;
            
            # Verificar backend
            proxy_pass http://app_servers/health;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            
            # Timeouts
            proxy_connect_timeout 2s;
            proxy_read_timeout 5s;
        }

        # API endpoints
        location /api/ {
            limit_req zone=api burst=20 nodelay;
            
            proxy_pass http://app_servers;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            
            # Timeouts
            proxy_connect_timeout 5s;
            proxy_send_timeout 10s;
            proxy_read_timeout 30s;
            
            # Buffer
            proxy_buffering on;
            proxy_buffer_size 4k;
            proxy_buffers 8 4k;
            
            # Health check interno
            proxy_next_upstream error timeout invalid_header http_500 http_502 http_503 http_504;
            proxy_next_upstream_tries 3;
            proxy_next_upstream_timeout 10s;
        }

        # Static files
        location / {
            root /usr/share/nginx/html;
            try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
            
            # Cache estático
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, immutable";
        }

        # Status do nginx
        location /nginx-status {
            stub_status on;
            access_log off;
            allow 127.0.0.1;
            deny all;
        }
    }
}
```

## 2. Scripts de Health Check e Monitoramento

### `scripts/health-check.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# DIYAPP Health Check Script
# SRE Senior - Autonomous Squad

set -e

# Colors for output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Configuration
TIMEOUT=10
RETRIES=3
SLO_AVAILABILITY=99.9
ERROR_BUDGET_PERCENT=0.1

# Log function
log() {
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] $1"
}

# Health check function
health_check() {
    local service=$1
    local url=$2
    local expected_status=${3:-200}
    
    log "Checking $service at $url..."
    
    for i in $(seq 1 $RETRIES); do
        if response=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" -m $TIMEOUT "$url" 2>/dev/null); then
            if [ "$response" -eq "$expected_status" ]; then
                log "${GREEN}✓ $service is healthy (HTTP $response)${NC}"
                return 0
            else
                log "${YELLOW}⚠ $service returned HTTP $response (expected $expected_status)${NC}"
            fi
        else
            log "${YELLOW}⚠ $service connection failed (attempt $i/$RETRIES)${NC}"
        fi
        
        if [ $i -lt $RETRIES ]; then
            sleep 2
        fi
    done
    
    log "${RED}✗ $service health check failed after $RETRIES attempts${NC}"
    return 1
}

# Database health check
check_database() {
    log "Checking PostgreSQL database..."
    
    if docker exec diyapp-postgres pg_isready -U diyapp_user -h localhost -t 5 > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        log "${GREEN}✓ PostgreSQL is healthy${NC}"
        
        # Test query
        if docker exec diyapp-postgres psql -U diyapp_user -d diyapp -c "SELECT 1" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
            log "${GREEN}✓ Database queries working${NC}"
            return 0
        else
            log "${RED}✗ Database queries failing${NC}"
            return 1
        fi
    else
        log "${RED}✗ PostgreSQL is not ready${NC}"
        return 1
    fi
}

# Redis health check
check_redis() {
    log "Checking Redis cache..."
    
    if docker exec diyapp-redis redis-cli --raw incr ping > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        log "${GREEN}✓ Redis is healthy${NC}"
        return 0
    else
        log "${RED}✗ Redis health check failed${NC}"
        return 1
    fi
}

# Application metrics check
check_metrics() {
    log "Checking application metrics..."
    
    if response=$(curl -s -m $TIMEOUT http://localhost:3000/metrics 2>/dev/null); then
        if echo "$response" | grep -q "nodejs_version_info"; then
            log "${GREEN}✓ Application metrics available${NC}"
            
            # Check for critical metrics
            for metric in "http_request_duration_seconds" "process_cpu_user_seconds_total" "nodejs_heap_space_size_total_bytes"; do
                if echo "$response" | grep -q "^$metric"; then
                    log "${GREEN}  ✓ Metric '$metric' present${NC}"
                else
                    log "${YELLOW}  ⚠ Metric '$metric' missing${NC}"
                fi
            done
            
            return 0
        else
            log "${YELLOW}⚠ Metrics endpoint accessible but format may be incorrect${NC}"
            return 1
        fi
    else
        log "${RED}✗ Metrics endpoint not accessible${NC}"
        return 1
    fi
}

# SLO Compliance Check
check_slo_compliance() {
    log "Checking SLO compliance..."
    
    # Simulate SLO check (in production, this would query Prometheus)
    local total_checks=1000
    local failed_checks=$((RANDOM % 5)) # Simulate 0-4 failures
    
    local error_rate=$(echo "scale=4; $failed_checks / $total_checks * 100" | bc)
    local availability=$(echo "scale=2; 100 - $error_rate" | bc)
    
    log "Simulated check: $total_checks requests, $failed_checks failures"
    log "Error rate: ${error_rate}%"
    log "Availability: ${availability}%"
    
    if (( $(echo "$availability >= $SLO_AVAIL

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]

## 2. Configurações Core

### src/config/database.js
```javascript
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const logger = require('./logger');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = new Pool({
      host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT) || 5432,
      database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v12',
      user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
      ssl: process.env.DB_SSL === 'true' ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false,
      max: 20,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    });

    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.pool.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Database connection established');
    });

    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected database error', { error: err.message });
    });
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Database query executed', {
        query: text,
        duration: `${duration}ms`,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      logger.error('Database query failed', {
        query: text,
        duration: `${duration}ms`,
        error: error.message,
        code: error.code
      });
      
      // Não exponha detalhes internos do banco
      const safeError = new Error('Database operation failed');
      safeError.code = error.code;
      throw safeError;
    }
  }

  async transaction(callback) {
    const client = await this.pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      const result = await callback(client);
      await client.query('COMMIT');
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      await client.query('ROLLBACK');
      throw error;
    } finally {
      client.release();
    }
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      const result = await this.query('SELECT NOW() as time');
      return { healthy: true, timestamp: result.rows[0].time };
    } catch (error) {
      return { healthy: false, error: error.message };
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new Database();
```

### src/config/logger.js
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = winston.format;

// Formatação para mascarar dados sensíveis
const maskSensitiveData = winston.format((info) => {
  const maskedInfo = { ...info };
  
  // Campos sensíveis para mascarar
  const sensitiveFields = [
    'password', 'token', 'access_token', 'refresh_token',
    'authorization', 'card_number', 'cvv', 'cpf', 'email'
  ];
  
  sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
    if (maskedInfo[field]) {
      maskedInfo[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
    
    // Também mascarar em objetos aninhados
    if (maskedInfo.meta && maskedInfo.meta[field]) {
      maskedInfo.meta[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return maskedInfo;
});

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: combine(
    errors({ stack: true }),
    timestamp(),
    maskSensitiveData(),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v12-core' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log',
      maxsize: 5242880,
      maxFiles: 5
    })
  ],
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/exceptions.log' })
  ],
  rejectionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/rejections.log' })
  ]
});

// Middleware para logging de requests
logger.requestLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4();
  
  // Adiciona correlation ID ao request
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    
    const logData = {
      correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      duration: `${duration}ms`,
      userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip,
      userId: req.user ? req.user.id : null
    };
    
    if (res.statusCode >= 400) {
      logger.warn('HTTP Request', logData);
    } else {
      logger.info('HTTP Request', logData);
    }
  });
  
  next();
};

module.exports = logger;
```

### src/config/jwt.js
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const logger = require('./logger');

class JWTService {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;
    this.refreshSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET;
    this.accessTokenExpiry = process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h';
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN || '7d';
    
    if (!this.secret || !this.refreshSecret) {
      logger.error('JWT secrets not configured');
      throw new Error('JWT configuration missing');
    }
  }

  generateAccessToken(payload) {
    return jwt.sign(
      { 
        ...payload,
        type: 'access'
      },
      this.secret,
      { expiresIn: this.accessTokenExpiry }
    );
  }

  generateRefreshToken(payload) {
    return jwt.sign(
      { 
        ...payload,
        type: 'refresh'
      },
      this.refreshSecret,
      { expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry }
    );
  }

  verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.secret);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn('Invalid access token', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired access token');
    }
  }

  verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.refreshSecret);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn('Invalid refresh token', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired refresh token');
    }
  }

  decodeToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.decode(token);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to decode token', { error: error.message });
      return null;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTService();
```

## 3. Modelos de Dados

### src/models/User.js
```javascript
const Joi = require('joi');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');

class User {
  constructor(data) {
    this.id = data.id;
    this.email = data.email;
    this.password = data.password;
    this.name = data.name;
    this.role = data.role || 'user';
    this.is_active = data.is_active !== undefined ? data.is_active : true;
    this.created_at = data.created_at;
    this.updated_at = data.updated_at;
    this.last_login = data.last_login;
  }

  static validationSchema() {
    return Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string()
        .email()
        .required()
        .messages({
          'string.email': 'Email must be a valid email address',
          'any.required': 'Email is required'
        }),
      password: Joi.string()
        .min(8)
        .pattern(/^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)/)
        .required()
        .messages({
          'string.min': 'Password must be at least 8 characters long',
          'string.pattern.base': 'Password must contain at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, and one number',
          'any.required': 'Password is required'
        }),
      name: Joi.string()
        .min(2)
        .max(100)
        .required()
        .messages({
          'string.min': 'Name must be at least 2 characters long',
          'string.max': 'Name cannot exceed 100 characters',
          'any.required': 'Name is required'
        }),
      role: Joi.string()
        .valid('user', 'admin')
        .default('user')
    });
  }

  static loginSchema() {
    return Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string()
        .email()
        .required(),
      password: Joi.string()
        .required()
    });
  }

  async hashPassword() {
    if (this.password) {
      const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(10);
      this.password = await bcrypt.hash(this.password, salt);
    }
  }

  async validatePassword(candidatePassword) {
    return bcrypt.compare(candidatePassword, this.password);
  }

  toJSON() {
    return {
      id: this.id,
      email: this.email,
      name: this.name,
      role: this.role,
      is_active: this.is_active,
      created_at: this.created_at,
      last_login: this.last_login
    };
  }
}

module.exports = User;
```

### src/models/Project.js
```javascript
const Joi = require('joi');

class Project {
  constructor(data) {
    this.id = data.id;
    this.user_id = data.user_id;
    this.title = data.title;
    this.description = data.description;
    this.status = data.status || 'draft';
    this.metadata = data.metadata || {};
    this.is_public = data.is_public !== undefined ? data.is_public : false;
    this.created_at = data.created_at;
    this.updated_at = data.updated_at;
    this.deleted_at = data.deleted_at;
  }

  static validationSchema() {
    return Joi.object({
      title: Joi.string()
        .min(3)
        .max(200)
        .required()
        .messages({
          'string.min': 'Title must be at least 3 characters long',
          'string.max': 'Title cannot exceed 200 characters',
          'any.required': 'Title is required'
        }),
      description: Joi.string()
        .max(1000)
        .allow('')
        .default(''),
      status: Joi.string()
        .valid('draft', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'archived')
        .default('draft'),
      metadata: Joi.object()
        .default({}),
      is_public: Joi.boolean()
        .default(false)
    });
  }

  static updateSchema() {
    return Joi.object({
      title: Joi.string()
        .min(3)
        .max(200),
      description: Joi.string()
        .max(1000)
        .allow(''),
      status: Joi.string()
        .valid('draft', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'archived'),
      metadata: Joi.object(),
      is_public: Joi.boolean()
    }).min(1);
  }

  toJSON() {
    return {
      id: this.id,
      user_id: this.user_id,
      title: this.title,
      description: this.description,
      status: this.status,
      metadata: this.metadata,
      is_public: this.is_public,
      created_at: this.created_at,
      updated_at: this.updated_at
    };
  }
}

module.exports = Project;
```

## 4. Repositórios

### src/repositories/user.repository.js
```javascript
const db = require('../config/database');
const User = require('../models/User');
const logger = require('../config/logger');

class UserRepository {
  async create(userData) {
    const query = `
      INSERT INTO users (email, password, name, role, is_active)
      VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)
      RETURNING id, email, name, role, is_active, created_at, updated_at
    `;
    
    const values = [
      userData.email,
      userData.password,
      userData.name,
      userData.role || 'user',
      userData.is_active !== undefined ? userData.is_active : true
    ];
    
    try {
      const result = await db.query(query, values);
      return new User(result.rows[0]);
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.code === '23505') { // Unique violation
        throw new Error('Email already exists');
      }
      logger.error('Failed to create user', { error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async findByEmail(email) {
    const query = `
      SELECT * FROM users 
      WHERE email = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL
      LIMIT 1
    `;
    
    const result = await db.query(query, [email]);
    return result.rows

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Boilerplate React

Vou criar um boilerplate React profissional com foco em performance, acessibilidade e fidelidade ao design system. Vou configurar roteamento, gerenciamento de estado e garantir uma estrutura escalável.

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## ADR-001: Arquitetura V12 Core
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Backend

## CONTEXTO:
DIYAPP evoluiu para uma plataforma complexa com múltiplos serviços. A versão V12 precisa estabelecer uma arquitetura moderna, escalável e 100% autônoma. O sistema atual sofre com:
- Acoplamento excessivo entre componentes
- CI/CD manual e propenso a erros
- Padrões de código inconsistentes entre squads
- Dificuldade em deploy independente de serviços
- Observabilidade limitada

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microserviços com frontend unificado, containerização completa e pipeline CI/CD automatizado. Cada squad terá autonomia sobre seus serviços, mas seguirá padrões técnicos unificados.

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Monólito modularizado
- **Prós:** Simplicidade inicial, deploy único, debug mais fácil
- **Contras:** Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento técnico, deploy lento
- **Avaliação:** Não atende requisito de autonomia por squad

### Opção B: Microserviços completos
- **Prós:** Autonomia total por squad, escalabilidade independente, resiliência
- **Contras:** Complexidade operacional, latência de rede, consistência de dados
- **Avaliação:** Complexidade excessiva para estágio atual

### Opção C: Arquitetura híbrida (ESCOLHIDA)
- **Prós:** Equilíbrio entre autonomia e simplicidade, frontend unificado, serviços especializados
- **Contras:** Necessidade de gateway bem definido
- **Justificativa:** Oferece autonomia para squads com frontend consistente e operação simplificada

## ARQUITETURA V12 - ESPECIFICAÇÃO TÉCNICA

### 1. Stack Tecnológica Principal

#### Frontend (DIYAPP Dashboard)
```yaml
framework: React 18 + TypeScript
build_tool: Vite 5
state_management: Zustand + React Query
styling: Tailwind CSS + shadcn/ui
testing: Vitest + React Testing Library + Playwright
bundling: Vite (ES modules)
linting: ESLint + Prettier + Biome
```

#### Backend (Core Services)
```yaml
runtime: Node.js 20 LTS
framework: Express.js + TypeScript
api_spec: OpenAPI 3.1 (Swagger)
validation: Zod
authentication: JWT + OAuth2 (Keycloak)
database_orm: Prisma 5
testing: Jest + Supertest
```

#### Banco de Dados
```yaml
primary: PostgreSQL 16 (com replicação)
caching: Redis 7 (sessões e cache)
search: Elasticsearch 8 (quando necessário)
migrations: Prisma Migrate
backup: WAL-E + S3 compatível
```

#### Infraestrutura
```yaml
containerization: Docker + Docker Compose
orchestration: Kubernetes (EKS/GKE) para produção
service_mesh: Istio (futuro)
monitoring: Prometheus + Grafana
logging: Loki + Grafana
tracing: Jaeger
ci_cd: GitHub Actions + ArgoCD
```

### 2. Estrutura de Pastas Padrão

```
diyapp-v12/
├── .github/
│   ├── workflows/
│   │   ├── ci-frontend.yml
│   │   ├── ci-backend.yml
│   │   └── cd-argocd.yml

├── apps/

│   │   │   ├── lib/               # Utilities, configurações
│   │   │   ├── pages/             # Rotas da aplicação
│   │   │   ├── stores/            # Zustand stores
│   │   │   ├── types/             # TypeScript definitions
│   │   │   └── main.tsx
│   │   ├── public/

│   │   ├── vite.config.ts
│   │   └── package.json
│   │
│   ├── api-gateway/                # Gateway unificado
│   │   ├── src/
│   │   │   ├── middleware/        # Auth, rate limiting, logging
│   │   │   ├── routes/           # Rotas proxy para serviços
│   │   │   └── index.ts
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   │
│   └── services/                   # Serviços por domínio
│       ├── auth-service/          # Autenticação e autorização
│       ├── user-service/          # Gestão de usuários
│       ├── project-service/       # Gestão de projetos
│       └── notification-service/  # Notificações em tempo real
│
├── packages/                       # Bibliotecas compartilhadas
│   ├── eslint-config/             # Configurações ESLint
│   ├── tsconfig/                  # Configurações TypeScript

│
├── docs/

│   ├── api/                       # Documentação OpenAPI

│
└── docker-compose.yml             # Ambiente local
```

### 3. Engineering Standards

#### Código
```typescript
// .eslintrc.js - Padrão de código
module.exports = {
  extends: ['@diyapp/eslint-config'],
  rules: {
    '@typescript-eslint/explicit-function-return-type': 'error',
    'no-console': ['warn', { allow: ['warn', 'error'] }],
    'complexity': ['error', { max: 10 }],
  }
};

// tsconfig.json - Configuração TypeScript
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "target": "ES2022",
    "module": "ESNext",
    "lib": ["ES2022", "DOM"],
    "strict": true,
    "skipLibCheck": true,
    "forceConsistentCasingInFileNames": true,
    "noUnusedLocals": true,
    "noUnusedParameters": true,
    "exactOptionalPropertyTypes": true
  }
}
```

#### Commits (Conventional Commits)
```bash
# Padrão: type(scope): description
# Exemplos:
feat(auth): implement OAuth2 login
fix(api): resolve memory leak in file upload
docs(architecture): update ADR-001
refactor(ui): extract Button component
test(projects): add unit tests for validation
chore(deps): update React to 18.2.0
```

#### Branch Strategy (Git Flow simplificado)
```yaml
main:           # Produção (protected)
staging:        # Pré-produção (protected)
develop:        # Integração contínua
feature/*:      # Novas funcionalidades
bugfix/*:       # Correções de bugs
hotfix/*:       # Correções urgentes para produção
release/*:      # Preparação de release
```

### 4. Pipeline CI/CD

#### GitHub Actions Workflow (frontend-ci.yml)
```yaml
name: Frontend CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
        
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
        
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
        
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm run test:unit
        
      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
        
      - name: E2E tests
        run: npm run test:e2e
        
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3

  security:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Snyk Security Scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
          
      - name: Dependency review
        uses: actions/dependency-review-action@v3
```

#### Dockerfile Padrão (Frontend)
```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM node:20-alpine AS builder
WORKDIR /app
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci
COPY . .
RUN npm run build

# Production stage
FROM nginx:alpine
COPY --from=builder /app/dist /usr/share/nginx/html
COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf
EXPOSE 80
CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]
```

### 5. Observabilidade

#### Logging Estruturado
```typescript
// src/lib/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error' 
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log' 
    })
  ],
  defaultMeta: {
    service: 'diyapp-frontend',
    environment: process.env.NODE_ENV
  }
});
```

#### Métricas e Health Checks
```typescript
// src/lib/metrics.ts
import client from 'prom-client';

const collectDefaultMetrics = client.collectDefaultMetrics;
collectDefaultMetrics({ timeout: 5000 });

export const httpRequestDuration = new client.Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
});

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime(),
    memory: process.memoryUsage(),
    version: process.env.npm_package_version
  });
});
```

### 6. Segurança

#### Hardening Checklist
```yaml
authentication:
  - JWT com tempo de expiração curto (15min)
  - Refresh tokens com revogação
  - Rate limiting por IP e usuário
  - MFA obrigatório para admin

authorization:
  - RBAC com roles e permissions
  - Validação em nível de endpoint e dados
  - Princípio do menor privilégio

data_protection:
  - TLS 1.3 em todas as comunicações
  - Dados sensíveis criptografados em repouso
  - Secrets em HashiCorp Vault/AWS Secrets Manager
  - Sanitização de inputs contra XSS/SQLi

infrastructure:
  - Network policies no Kubernetes
  - Pod security standards
  - Scanning de vulnerabilidades em imagens
  - WAF na frente do API Gateway
```

### 7. Protocolos de Desenvolvimento

#### Code Review Checklist
```markdown
## PR Checklist
- [ ] Código resolve o problema descrito
- [ ] Testes cobrem caminho feliz e edge cases
- [ ] Cobertura de testes > 80%
- [ ] Seguindo padrões de código (ESLint/Prettier)
- [ ] Sem dados sensíveis expostos
- [ ] Performance otimizada (N+1 queries, loops)
- [ ] Documentação atualizada (README, JSDoc)
- [ ] Commits seguem Conventional Commits
- [ ] Dependências novas justificadas
- [ ] Migrações de banco testadas e reversíveis
```

#### Definition of Done (DoD)
```yaml
development:
  - Código revisado e aprovado por Tech Lead
  - Todos os testes passando
  - Cobertura de testes mantida ou aumentada
  - Build passando no CI
  - Sem vulnerabilidades críticas

deployment:
  - Deploy automático para staging
  - Smoke tests passando em staging
  - Aprovado por QA (quando aplicável)
  - Rollback plan documentado
  - Métricas de saúde monitoradas

documentation:
  - README atualizado
  - API docs atualizados (OpenAPI)
  - ADR criado para mudanças arquiteturais
  - Changelog atualizado
```

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:

### Positivas:
1. **Autonomia por squad**: Cada squad gerencia seus serviços independentemente
2. **Escalabilidade**: Serviços escalam conforme demanda específica
3. **Resiliência**: Falhas isoladas não derrubam sistema inteiro
4. **Velocidade de deploy**: Deploys independentes e mais rápidos
5. **Observabilidade completa**: Monitoramento granular por serviço

### Negativas:
1. **Complexidade operacional**: Mais componentes para gerenciar
2. **Latência de rede**: Comunicação entre serviços adiciona overhead
3. **Consistência eventual**: Dados distribuídos requerem patterns específicos
4. **Custo inicial**: Infraestrutura mais complexa e cara

### Riscos e Mitigações:
1. **Risco**: Falha no API Gateway paralisa todo sistema
   **Mitigação**: Health checks automáticos + failover + cache local
   
2. **Risco**: Inconsistência de dados entre serviços
   **Mitigação**: Event sourcing + sagas + compensação
   
3. **Risco**: Complexidade de debug em produção
   **Mitigação**: Distributed tracing (Jaeger) + logs centralizados
   
4. **Risco**: Custos de infraestrutura exponenciais
   **Mitigação**: Auto-scaling baseado em métricas + budget alerts

## REVISÃO:
Esta arquitetura será reavaliada em 6 meses ou quando:
- Número de serviços exceder 15
- Latência p95 exceder 500ms consistentemente
- Custos de infra excederem 30% do orçamento

---

## IMPLEMENTAÇÃO INICIAL

### index.html (Ponto de Entrada - Dashboard)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Dashboard</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/src/styles/globals.css">
    <link rel="icon" type="image/x-icon" href="/favicon.ico">
</head>
<body>
    <div id="root">
        <div class="loading-container">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Carregando DIYAPP V12...</p>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
    
    <!-- Health check badge -->
    <div class="health-badge" id="healthStatus">
        <span class="status-dot"></span>
        <span class="status-text">Verificando saúde do sistema...</span>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        // Health check simples
        async function checkHealth() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/health');
                const data = await response.json();
                const badge = document.getElementById('healthStatus');
                const dot = badge.querySelector('.status-dot');
                const text = badge.querySelector('.status-text');
                
                if (data.status === 'healthy') {
                    dot.classList.add('healthy');
                    text.textContent = `Sistema saudável • v${data.version}`;
                } else {
                    dot.classList.add('unhealthy');
                    text.textContent = 'Sistema com problemas';
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Health check failed:', error);
            }
        }
        
        // Verificar saúde a cada 30 segundos
        checkHealth();
        setInterval(checkHealth, 30000);
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

### package.json (Frontend)
```json
{
  "name": "@diyapp/frontend",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "private": true,
  "type": "module",
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "vite",
    "build": "tsc && vite build",
    "preview": "vite preview",
    "lint": "eslint src --ext ts,tsx --report-unused-disable-directives --max-warnings 0",
    "type-check": "tsc --noEmit",
    "test:unit": "vitest",
    "test:e2e": "playwright test",
    "test:coverage": "vitest run --coverage",
    "format": "prettier --write \"src

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo para o DIYAPP V12, incluindo paleta de cores, tipografia, componentes de UI e wireframes de alta fidelidade para as 5 views principais. Como não posso criar um protótipo Figma diretamente, vou implementar um Design System funcional em HTML/CSS/JS que simula todas as funcionalidades e inclui um protótipo navegável.

```html

        }
        
        .form-help {
            display: block;
            margin-top: var(--spacing-1);
            font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
            color: var(--color-neutral-500);
        }
        
        .form-error {
            display: block;
            margin-top: var(--spacing-1);
            font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
            color: var(--color-error);
        }
        
        /* ===== MODAL COMPONENTS ===== */
        .modal-overlay {
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            right: 0;
            bottom: 0;
            background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            z-index: 100;
            opacity: 0;
            visibility: hidden;
            transition: all var(--transition-normal);
        }
        
        .modal-overlay.active {
            opacity: 1;
            visibility: visible;
        }
        
        .modal {
            background-color: white;
            border-radius: var(--radius-lg);
            box-shadow: var(--shadow-xl);
            width: 90%;
            max-width: 500px;
            max-height: 90vh;
            overflow-y: auto;
            transform: translateY(20px);
            transition: transform var(--transition-normal);
        }

            transform: translateY(0);
        }

            padding: var(--spacing-4) var(--spacing-6);

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   └── terraform.tfvars.example
├── docker/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── app/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── nginx/
│   │   ├── Dockerfile
│   │   └── nginx.conf
│   └── prometheus/
│       └── prometheus.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   └── monitor.sh
├── monitoring/
│   ├── grafana/
│   │   └── dashboards/
│   └── alerts/
│       └── alert-rules.yml
└── README.md
```

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura Principal

### `terraform/main.tf`

```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0"
  required_providers {
    docker = {
      source  = "kreuzwerker/docker"
      version = "~> 3.0"
    }
    local = {
      source = "hashicorp/local"
      version = "~> 2.4"
    }
  }
}

provider "docker" {
  host = "unix:///var/run/docker.sock"
}

# Network para comunicação entre containers
resource "docker_network" "diyapp_network" {
  name     = "diyapp-network"
  driver   = "bridge"
  internal = false

  ipam_config {
    subnet  = "172.20.0.0/16"
    gateway = "172.20.0.1"
  }
}

# Volume para PostgreSQL
resource "docker_volume" "postgres_data" {
  name = "postgres-data"
}

# Volume para Redis
resource "docker_volume" "redis_data" {
  name = "redis-data"
}

# Container PostgreSQL
resource "docker_container" "postgres" {
  name  = "diyapp-postgres"
  image = "postgres:15-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  env = [
    "POSTGRES_DB=${var.postgres_db}",
    "POSTGRES_USER=${var.postgres_user}",
    "POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${var.postgres_password}"
  ]

  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.postgres_data.name
    container_path = "/var/lib/postgresql/data"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.10"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${var.postgres_user}"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "40s"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 5432
    external = 5432
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "database"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container Redis
resource "docker_container" "redis" {
  name  = "diyapp-redis"
  image = "redis:7-alpine"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  command = ["redis-server", "--appendonly", "yes"]

  volumes {
    volume_name    = docker_volume.redis_data.name
    container_path = "/data"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.20"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }

  ports {
    internal = 6379
    external = 6379
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "cache"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container da Aplicação Principal
resource "docker_container" "app" {
  name  = "diyapp-application"
  image = "diyapp-app:${var.app_version}"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  depends_on = [
    docker_container.postgres,
    docker_container.redis
  ]

  env = [
    "NODE_ENV=${var.environment}",
    "DATABASE_URL=postgresql://${var.postgres_user}:${var.postgres_password}@diyapp-postgres:5432/${var.postgres_db}",
    "REDIS_URL=redis://diyapp-redis:6379",
    "APP_PORT=3000",
    "LOG_LEVEL=info"
  ]

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.30"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "60s"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3000
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "application"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
    "com.diyapp.version" = var.app_version
  }
}

# Container Nginx (Load Balancer)
resource "docker_container" "nginx" {
  name  = "diyapp-nginx"
  image = "diyapp-nginx:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"
  depends_on = [docker_container.app]

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.40"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8080/nginx-health"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 3
  }

  ports {
    internal = 80
    external = 8080
  }

  ports {
    internal = 443
    external = 8443
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "load-balancer"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}

# Container Prometheus (Monitoring)
resource "docker_container" "prometheus" {
  name  = "diyapp-prometheus"
  image = "prom/prometheus:latest"
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  volumes {
    host_path      = "${path.module}/../monitoring/prometheus.yml"
    container_path = "/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
    ipv4_address = "172.20.0.50"
  }

  ports {
    internal = 9090
    external = 9090
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "monitoring"
    "com.diyapp.environment" = var.environment
  }
}
```

### `terraform/variables.tf`

```hcl
variable "environment" {
  description = "Ambiente de deploy (staging/production)"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
}

variable "app_version" {
  description = "Versão da aplicação"
  type        = string
  default     = "v12.0.0"
}

variable "postgres_db" {
  description = "Nome do banco de dados PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_staging"
}

variable "postgres_user" {
  description = "Usuário do PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_user"
}

variable "postgres_password" {
  description = "Senha do PostgreSQL"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "redis_password" {
  description = "Senha do Redis"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
  default     = ""
}
```

### `terraform/outputs.tf`

```hcl
output "application_url" {
  description = "URL da aplicação"
  value       = "http://localhost:8080"
}

output "database_url" {
  description = "URL de conexão com o banco de dados"
  value       = "postgresql://${var.postgres_user}:${var.postgres_password}@localhost:5432/${var.postgres_db}"
  sensitive   = true
}

output "monitoring_url" {
  description = "URL do Prometheus"
  value       = "http://localhost:9090"
}

output "network_name" {
  description = "Nome da rede Docker"
  value       = docker_network.diyapp_network.name
}

output "containers_status" {
  description = "Status dos containers"
  value = {
    postgres  = docker_container.postgres.status
    redis     = docker_container.redis.status
    app       = docker_container.app.status
    nginx     = docker_container.nginx.status
    prometheus = docker_container.prometheus.status
  }
}
```

## 2. Docker Compose - Orquestração Local

### `docker/docker-compose.yml`

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: ${POSTGRES_DB:-diyapp_staging}
      POSTGRES_USER: ${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=database"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=cache"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"

  app:
    build:
      context: ../app
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-application
    restart: unless-stopped
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: ${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://${POSTGRES_USER:-diyapp_user}:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/${POSTGRES_DB:-diyapp_staging}
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      APP_PORT: 3000
      LOG_LEVEL: info
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 60s
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=application"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"
      - "com.diyapp.version=${APP_VERSION:-v12.0.0}"

  nginx:
    build:
      context: ./nginx
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    restart: unless-stopped
    depends_on:
      - app
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8080/nginx-health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    ports:
      - "8080:80"
      - "8443:443"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=load-balancer"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"

  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=monitoring"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ../monitoring/grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    labels:
      - "com.diyapp.service=monitoring"
      - "com.diyapp.environment=${ENVIRONMENT:-staging}"

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    ipam:
      config:
        - subnet: 172.20.0.0/16
```

### `docker/app/Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código da aplicação
COPY . .

# Criar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S diyapp -u 1001

# Configurar permissões
RUN chown -R diyapp:nodejs /app
USER diyapp

# Expor porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check endpoint
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --retries=3 --start-period=60s \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "server.js"]
```

### `docker/nginx/Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM nginx:alpine

# Remover configuração padrão
RUN rm /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

# Copiar configuração customizada
COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf

# Criar diretório para health check
RUN mkdir -p /var/www/html && \
    echo "nginx is healthy" > /var/www/html/nginx-health

# Expor portas
EXPOSE 80 443

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:8080/nginx-health || exit 1
```

### `docker/nginx/nginx.conf`

```nginx
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream app_servers {
        least_conn;
        server diyapp-application:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
        
        # Para staging, podemos adicionar mais instâncias se necessário
        # server diyapp-application-2:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
        # server diyapp-application-3:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
    }

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name localhost;

        # Health check endpoint
        location /nginx-health {
            access_log off;
            return 200 "healthy\n";
            add_header Content-Type text/plain;
        }

        # Health check da aplicação (usado pelo load balancer)
        location /health {
            proxy_pass http://app_servers/health;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            
            # Timeouts otimizados para health checks
            proxy_connect_timeout 5s;
            proxy_send_timeout 5s;
            proxy_read_timeout 5s;
        }

        # Métricas Prometheus
        location /metrics {
            proxy_pass http://app_servers/metrics;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        }

        # API endpoints
        location /api/ {
            proxy_pass http://app_servers/api/;
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            
            # Timeouts para API
            proxy_connect_timeout 15s;
            proxy_send_timeout 30s;
            proxy_read_timeout 30s;
            
            # Buffer sizes
            proxy_buffer_size 

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```javascript
// ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO
// diyapp-v12-core/
// ├── src/
// │   ├── config/
// │   │   ├── database.js
// │   │   ├── jwt.js
// │   │   └── logger.js
// │   ├── controllers/
// │   │   ├── auth.controller.js
// │   │   └── projects.controller.js
// │   ├── middleware/
// │   │   ├── auth.js
// │   │   ├── errorHandler.js
// │   │   ├── rateLimiter.js
// │   │   └── validation.js
// │   ├── models/
// │   │   ├── Project.js
// │   │   └── User.js
// │   ├── routes/
// │   │   ├── auth.routes.js
// │   │   └── projects.routes.js
// │   ├── services/
// │   │   ├── auth.service.js
// │   │   ├── project.service.js
// │   │   └── database.service.js
// │   ├── utils/
// │   │   ├── apiResponse.js
// │   │   └── validators.js
// │   ├── tests/
// │   │   ├── auth.test.js
// │   │   ├── projects.test.js
// │   │   └── setup.js
// │   ├── docs/
// │   │   └── swagger.js
// │   └── app.js
// ├── .env
// ├── package.json
// ├── index.html (dashboard)
// └── README.md

// 1. package.json
const packageJson = {
  name: "diyapp-v12-core",
  version: "1.0.0",
  description: "DIYAPP Evolution V12 - Core API Layer",
  main: "src/app.js",
  scripts: {
    "start": "node src/app.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/app.js",
    "test": "jest --coverage --coverageThreshold='{\"global\":{\"branches\":85,\"functions\":85,\"lines\":85,\"statements\":85}}'",
    "test:watch": "jest --watch",
    "migrate": "node src/services/database.service.js --migrate",
    "seed": "node src/services/database.service.js --seed"
  },
  dependencies: {
    "express": "^4.18.2",
    "express-rate-limit": "^7.1.5",
    "helmet": "^7.0.0",
    "cors": "^2.8.5",
    "dotenv": "^16.3.1",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.2",
    "bcryptjs": "^2.4.3",
    "sqlite3": "^5.1.6",
    "winston": "^3.10.0",
    "express-winston": "^4.2.0",
    "joi": "^17.9.2",
    "swagger-ui-express": "^5.0.0",
    "swagger-jsdoc": "^6.2.8",
    "uuid": "^9.0.0",
    "express-async-errors": "^3.1.1"
  },
  devDependencies: {
    "jest": "^29.6.2",
    "supertest": "^6.3.3",
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1"
  },
  jest: {
    "testEnvironment": "node",
    "coveragePathIgnorePatterns": [
      "/node_modules/",
      "/src/tests/"
    ],
    "collectCoverageFrom": [
      "src/**/*.js",
      "!src/app.js",
      "!src/docs/**"
    ]
  }
};

// 2. .env
const envFile = `# Database
DB_PATH=./data/diyapp.db
DB_MIGRATIONS_PATH=./src/migrations

# JWT
JWT_SECRET=your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production
JWT_EXPIRES_IN=24h
JWT_REFRESH_SECRET=your-refresh-secret-key-change-in-production
JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN=7d

# Server
PORT=3000
NODE_ENV=development

# Rate Limiting
RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS=900000
RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS=100

# Logging
LOG_LEVEL=info
LOG_FILE_PATH=./logs/app.log

# Security
BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS=12
SESSION_TIMEOUT=3600`;

// 3. src/config/database.js
const databaseConfig = `
const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose();
const path = require('path');
const logger = require('./logger');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.db = null;
    this.initPromise = null;
  }

  async init() {
    if (this.initPromise) return this.initPromise;
    
    this.initPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const dbPath = process.env.DB_PATH || './data/diyapp.db';
      
      // Ensure directory exists
      const fs = require('fs');
      const dir = path.dirname(dbPath);
      if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
        fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
      }
      
      this.db = new sqlite3.Database(dbPath, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database connection failed:', err);
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        
        logger.info('Connected to SQLite database');
        this.runMigrations()
          .then(() => this.runSeed())
          .then(() => resolve(this.db))
          .catch(reject);
      });
    });
    
    return this.initPromise;
  }

  async runMigrations() {
    const migrations = [
      // Users table
      \`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
        id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        username TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
        full_name TEXT,
        role TEXT DEFAULT 'user',
        is_active INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      )\`,
      
      // Projects table
      \`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (
        id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
        user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        description TEXT,
        status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft',
        config_json TEXT,
        version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
        is_public INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        tags TEXT,
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE
      )\`,
      
      // Indexes
      \`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_user_id ON projects(user_id)\`,
      \`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_projects_status ON projects(status)\`,
      \`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_email ON users(email)\`
    ];
    
    for (const migration of migrations) {
      await this.query(migration);
    }
    
    logger.info('Database migrations completed');
  }

  async runSeed() {
    // Only seed in development
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'development') return;
    
    const count = await this.query('SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM users');
    if (count[0].count > 0) return;
    
    const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
    const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
    
    const adminPassword = await bcrypt.hash('admin123', 12);
    const userPassword = await bcrypt.hash('user123', 12);
    
    const seedData = [
      // Admin user
      \`INSERT OR IGNORE INTO users (id, email, username, password_hash, full_name, role) 
       VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\`,
      [uuidv4(), 'admin@diyapp.com', 'admin', adminPassword, 'System Admin', 'admin'],
      
      // Regular user
      \`INSERT OR IGNORE INTO users (id, email, username, password_hash, full_name) 
       VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\`,
      [uuidv4(), 'user@diyapp.com', 'user', userPassword, 'Regular User'],
      
      // Sample project
      \`INSERT OR IGNORE INTO projects (id, user_id, name, description, status, config_json) 
       VALUES (?, (SELECT id FROM users WHERE username = 'user'), ?, ?, ?, ?)\`,
      [uuidv4(), 'My First Project', 'A sample DIY project', 'active', JSON.stringify({
        components: [],
        theme: 'light',
        version: '1.0'
      })]
    ];
    
    for (let i = 0; i < seedData.length; i += 2) {
      await this.query(seedData[i], seedData[i + 1]);
    }
    
    logger.info('Database seeded with initial data');
  }

  query(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.all(sql, params, (err, rows) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database query error:', { sql, params, error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve(rows);
      });
    });
  }

  run(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.run(sql, params, function(err) {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database run error:', { sql, params, error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve({ lastID: this.lastID, changes: this.changes });
      });
    });
  }

  close() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.close((err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database close error:', err);
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        logger.info('Database connection closed');
        resolve();
      });
    });
  }
}

module.exports = new Database();
`;

// 4. src/config/jwt.js
const jwtConfig = `
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const logger = require('./logger');

class JWTService {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key';
    this.refreshSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || 'your-refresh-secret';
    this.accessExpiresIn = process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h';
    this.refreshExpiresIn = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN || '7d';
  }

  generateAccessToken(payload) {
    if (!this.secret) {
      throw new Error('JWT_SECRET not configured');
    }
    
    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: this.accessExpiresIn,
      issuer: 'diyapp-api',
      audience: 'diyapp-client'
    });
  }

  generateRefreshToken(payload) {
    if (!this.refreshSecret) {
      throw new Error('JWT_REFRESH_SECRET not configured');
    }
    
    return jwt.sign(payload, this.refreshSecret, {
      expiresIn: this.refreshExpiresIn,
      issuer: 'diyapp-api',
      audience: 'diyapp-client'
    });
  }

  verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
        issuer: 'diyapp-api',
        audience: 'diyapp-client'
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn('JWT verification failed:', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired token');
    }
  }

  verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.refreshSecret, {
        issuer: 'diyapp-api',
        audience: 'diyapp-client'
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn('Refresh token verification failed:', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired refresh token');
    }
  }

  decodeToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.decode(token);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Token decode error:', error);
      return null;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTService();
`;

// 5. src/config/logger.js
const loggerConfig = `
const winston = require('winston');
const path = require('path');

const logLevel = process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info';
const logFilePath = process.env.LOG_FILE_PATH || './logs/app.log';

// Ensure logs directory exists
const fs = require('fs');
const logDir = path.dirname(logFilePath);
if (!fs.existsSync(logDir)) {
  fs.mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true });
}

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: logLevel,
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp({
      format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss.SSS'
    }),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-api' },
  transports: [
    // File transport for errors
    new winston.transports.File({
      filename: logFilePath.replace('.log', '.error.log'),
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5
    }),
    // File transport for all logs
    new winston.transports.File({
      filename: logFilePath,
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 10
    })
  ]
});

// Console transport for non-production
if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize(),
      winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message, correlationId, userId, ...meta }) => {
        return \`\${timestamp} [\${level}] [correlationId:\${correlationId || 'none'}] [userId:\${userId || 'none'}] \${message} \${Object.keys(meta).length ? JSON.stringify(meta) : ''}\`;
      })
    )
  }));
}

// Request logging middleware
const requestLogger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({
      filename: logFilePath.replace('.log', '.requests.log'),
      maxsize: 10485760, // 10MB
      maxFiles: 10
    })
  ]
});

module.exports = logger;
module.exports.requestLogger = requestLogger;
`;

// 6. src/middleware/auth.js
const authMiddleware = `
const jwtService = require('../config/jwt');
const logger = require('../config/logger');
const { ApiError } = require('../utils/apiResponse');

const authenticate = async (req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('crypto').randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  
  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      throw new ApiError(401, 'Authentication required', 'AUTH_REQUIRED');
    }
    
    const token = authHeader.substring(7);
    const decoded = jwtService.verifyAccessToken(token);
    
    // Add user info to request
    req.user = {
      id: decoded.id,
      email: decoded.email,
      username: decoded.username,
      role: decoded.role
    };
    
    logger.info('User authenticated', {
      correlationId,
      userId: req.user.id,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl
    });
    
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.warn('Authentication failed', {
      correlationId,
      error: error.message,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl
    });
    
    if (error.message.includes('expired')) {
      next(new ApiError(401, 'Token expired', 'TOKEN_EXPIRED'));
    } else {
      next(new ApiError(401, 'Invalid authentication token', 'INVALID_TOKEN'));
    }
  }
};

const authorize = (...roles) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return next(new ApiError(401, 'Authentication required', 'AUTH_REQUIRED'));
    }
    
    if (!roles.includes(req.user.role)) {
      logger.warn('Authorization failed', {
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        userId: req.user.id,
        requiredRoles: roles,
        userRole: req.user.role,
        endpoint: req.originalUrl
      });
      
      return next(new ApiError(403, 'Insufficient permissions', 'FORBIDDEN'));
    }
    
    next();
  };
};

module.exports = { authenticate, authorize };
`;

// 7. src/middleware/errorHandler.js
const errorHandler = `
const logger = require('../config/logger');

class ApiError extends Error {
  constructor(statusCode, message, errorCode = 'INTERNAL_ERROR') {
    super(message);
    this.statusCode = statusCode;
    this.errorCode = errorCode;
    this.isOperational = true;
    Error.captureStackTrace(this, this.constructor);
  }
}

const errorHandler = (err, req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.correlationId || 'unknown';
  
  // Default error
  let statusCode = err.statusCode || 500;
  let message = err.message || 'Internal server error';
  let errorCode = err.errorCode || 'INTERNAL_ERROR';
  
  // Log the error
  const logLevel = statusCode >= 500 ? 'error' : 'warn';
  logger[logLevel](\`\${statusCode} - \${message}\`, {
    correlationId,
    errorCode,
    stack: err.stack,
    userId: req.user?.id,
    endpoint: req.originalUrl,
    method: req.method,
    ip: req.ip
  });
  
  // Never expose stack trace in production
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && statusCode === 500) {
    message = 'Internal server error';
  }
  
  // Send response
 

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Boilerplate React

Vou criar um boilerplate React profissional com foco em performance, seguindo os padrões estabelecidos no papel. O sistema será estruturado para atingir Lighthouse Performance >90.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── public/
├── src/
│   ├── components/
│   ├── pages/
│   ├── hooks/
│   ├── stores/
│   ├── styles/
│   ├── utils/
│   ├── types/
│   └── services/
├── package.json
└── configurações de build
```
