## 2. Configuração do Vite (vite.config.ts)

```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import { VitePWA } from 'vite-plugin-pwa';
import compression from 'vite-plugin-compression';
import { visualizer } from 'rollup-plugin-visualizer';

// https://vitejs.dev/config/
export default defineConfig(({ mode }) => ({
  plugins: [
    react(),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      ext: '.gz',
    }),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'brotliCompress',
      ext: '.br',
    }),
    VitePWA({
      registerType: 'autoUpdate',
      includeAssets: ['favicon.ico', 'apple-touch-icon.png', 'masked-icon.svg'],
      manifest: {
        name: 'DIYAPP V12 Core',
        short_name: 'DIYAPP',
        description: 'DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core Application',
        theme_color: '#0f172a',
        background_color: '#0f172a',
        display: 'standalone',
        orientation: 'portrait',
        scope: '/',
        start_url: '/',
        icons: [
          {
            src: '/pwa-192x192.png',
            sizes: '192x192',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
          {
            src: '/pwa-512x512.png',
            sizes: '512x512',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
        ],
      },
    }),
    mode === 'analyze' && visualizer({
      open: true,
      filename: 'dist/stats.html',
      gzipSize: true,
      brotliSize: true,
    }),
  ],
  build: {
    target: 'es2020',
    minify: 'terser',
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: mode === 'production',
        drop_debugger: true,
      },
    },
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          ui: ['zustand', 'clsx', 'date-fns'],
        },
        chunkFileNames: 'assets/[name]-[hash].js',
        entryFileNames: 'assets/[name]-[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: 'assets/[name]-[hash].[ext]',
      },
    },
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1000,
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
  },
  preview: {
    port: 3001,
    host: true,
  },
}));
```

    --transition-fast: 0ms;
    --transition-normal: 0ms;
    --transition-slow: 0ms;
  }
}
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Documento de Arquitetura

## 1. Visão Geral da Arquitetura V12

**Status**: Aceita  
**Data**: 2024-01-15  
**Autores**: Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Backend  

### 1.1 Princípios Fundamentais
- **Autonomia Total**: Cada componente deve ser executável independentemente
- **Resiliência**: Tolerância a falhas com fallbacks automáticos
- **Observabilidade**: Métricas, logs e traces em todos os níveis
- **Segurança por Design**: Zero-trust, autenticação obrigatória

## 2. Stack Tecnológica

### 2.1 Frontend

    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"

  backend:
    build: ./backend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis

  frontend:
    build: ./frontend
    ports:
      - "5173:5173"
    depends_on:
      - backend

volumes:
  postgres_data:

## 4. Padrões de Código

### 4.1 Frontend - React/Vite
```typescript
// src/components/features/UserProfile.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { userService } from '../../services/userService';
import { LoadingSpinner, ErrorMessage } from '../common';

interface UserProfileProps {
  userId: string;
}

export const UserProfile: React.FC<UserProfileProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const { data: user, isLoading, error } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['user', userId],
    queryFn: () => userService.getUserById(userId),
    retry: 3,
    staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutos
  });

  if (isLoading) return <LoadingSpinner />;
  if (error) return <ErrorMessage message="Failed to load user" />;

  return (
    <div className="user-profile" data-testid="user-profile">
      <h2>{user.name}</h2>
      <p>Email: {user.email}</p>
      <p>Role: {user.role}</p>
    </div>
  );
};
```

### 4.2 Backend - Node.js/Express
```javascript
// src/controllers/userController.js
const userService = require('../services/userService');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const { validateUserCreate } = require('../validators/userValidator');

class UserController {
  async createUser(req, res) {
    try {
      // Validação de entrada
      const { error, value } = validateUserCreate(req.body);
      if (error) {
        return res.status(400).json({
          success: false,
          error: 'Validation failed',
          details: error.details
        });
      }

      // Lógica de negócio
      const user = await userService.createUser(value);
      
      logger.info(`User created: ${user.id}`);
      
      // Resposta padronizada
      return res.status(201).json({
        success: true,
        data: user,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('User creation failed:', error);
      
      return res.status(500).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Internal server error',
        requestId: req.requestId
      });
    }
  }

  async getUser(req, res) {
    const { id } = req.params;
    
    try {
      const user = await userService.getUserById(id);
      
      if (!user) {
        return res.status(404).json({
          success: false,
          error: 'User not found'
        });
      }
      
      return res.json({
        success: true,
        data: user
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Failed to get user ${id}:`, error);
      return res.status(500).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Failed to retrieve user'
      });
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new UserController();
```

### 4.3 Banco de Dados - PostgreSQL
```sql
-- database/migrations/001_create_users_table.sql
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'user',
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- Índices para performance
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at DESC);

-- Trigger para updated_at
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON users 
    FOR EACH ROW 
    EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
```

## 5. Fluxo CI/CD

### 5.1 Pipeline de Integração Contínua
```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-frontend.yml
name: CI Frontend

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
          cache-dependency-path: frontend/package-lock.json
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Lint
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Type check
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm run type-check
      
      - name: Test
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm test -- --coverage
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          directory: ./frontend/coverage
          flags: frontend
  
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: test
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '18'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Build
        working-directory: ./frontend
        run: npm run build
      
      - name: Upload artifact
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
        with:
          name: frontend-build
          path: frontend/dist
```

### 5.2 Pipeline de Deploy
```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd-production.yml
name: CD Production

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
    tags: ['v*']

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Configure AWS credentials
        uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v2
        with:
          aws-access-key-id: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
          aws-secret-access-key: ${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
          aws-region: us-east-1
      
      - name: Login to Amazon ECR
        id: login-ecr
        uses: aws-actions/amazon-ecr-login@v1
      
      - name: Build and push backend image
        env:
          ECR_REGISTRY: ${{ steps.login-ecr.outputs.registry }}
          ECR_REPOSITORY: diyapp-backend
          IMAGE_TAG: ${{ github.sha }}
        run: |
          docker build -t $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY:$IMAGE_TAG ./backend
          docker push $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY:$IMAGE_TAG
      
      - name: Deploy to ECS
        run: |
          aws ecs update-service \
            --cluster diyapp-cluster \
            --service backend-service \
            --force-new-deployment
      
      - name: Deploy frontend to S3
        run: |
          aws s3 sync ./frontend/dist s3://diyapp-frontend --delete
          aws cloudfront create-invalidation \
            --distribution-id ${{ secrets.CLOUDFRONT_DISTRIBUTION_ID }} \
            --paths "/*"
```

## 6. Engineering Standards

```markdown
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V12

## 1. Convenções de Código

### 1.1 Nomenclatura
- Variáveis/funções: camelCase
- Classes/Interfaces: PascalCase
- Constantes: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE
- Arquivos: kebab-case

### 1.2 Commits
Usar Conventional Commits:
- feat: Nova funcionalidade
- fix: Correção de bug
- docs: Documentação
- style: Formatação
- refactor: Refatoração
- test: Testes
- chore: Tarefas de manutenção

Exemplo: `feat(auth): implement login with 2FA`

## 2. Qualidade de Código

### 2.1 Testes
- Cobertura mínima: 80%
- Testes unitários para lógica de negócio
- Testes de integração para APIs
- Testes E2E para fluxos críticos

### 2.2 Linting
- ESLint com configuração Airbnb
- Prettier para formatação
- Husky para pre-commit hooks

## 3. Segurança

### 3.1 Autenticação
- JWT com tempo de expiração curto (15min)
- Refresh tokens com revogação
- Rate limiting por IP/user

### 3.2 Dados Sensíveis
- Nunca logar dados sensíveis
- Hash passwords com bcrypt (cost: 12)
- Criptografar dados em repouso

## 4. Performance

### 4.1 Frontend
- Code splitting por rota
- Lazy loading de componentes
- Cache de assets (1 ano)

### 4.2 Backend
- Cache com Redis (TTL: 5min)
- Connection pooling para DB
- Compression gzip
```

## 7. Ponto de Entrada - Dashboard

```html
<!-- frontend/public/index.html -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Dashboard</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/src/styles/global.css">
    <link rel="icon" type="image/x-icon" href="/favicon.ico">
</head>
<body>
    <div id="root">
        <div class="loading-container">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Loading DIYAPP V12...</p>
        </div>
    </div>
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
    
    <!-- Health check script -->
    <script>
        // Health check para serviços
        async function checkServices() {
            const services = [
                { name: 'API', url: '/api/health' },
                { name: 'Database', url: '/api/health/db' },
                { name: 'Cache', url: '/api/health/cache' }
            ];
            
            const results = await Promise.allSettled(
                services.map(s => fetch(s.url).then(r => r.ok))
            );
            
            console.log('Service Health:', results);
        }
        
        // Iniciar quando DOM estiver pronto
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', checkServices);
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

## 8. Script de Inicialização

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/start-dev.sh

echo "🚀 Starting DIYAPP V12 Development Environment..."

# Verificar dependências
command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1 || { 
    echo "Docker is required but not installed. Aborting." >&2; exit 1; 
}

command -v node >/dev/null 2>&1 || { 
    echo "Node.js is required but not installed. Aborting." >&2; exit 1; 
}

# Criar variáveis de ambiente se não existirem
if [ ! -f .env ]; then
    echo "Creating .env file from template..."
    cp .env.example .env
    echo "Please update .env file with your configuration"
    exit 1
fi

# Iniciar banco de dados
echo "Starting PostgreSQL and Redis..."
docker-compose up -d postgres redis

# Aguardar banco ficar pronto
echo "Waiting for database to be ready..."
until docker-compose exec postgres pg_isready -U diyapp_user; do
    sleep 2
done

# Executar migrações
echo "Running database migrations..."
npm run migrate:up

# Iniciar backend
echo "Starting backend server..."
cd backend && npm run dev &

# Iniciar frontend
echo "Starting frontend server..."
cd frontend && npm run dev &

echo "✅ DIYAPP V12 is running!"
echo "Frontend: http://localhost:5173"
echo "Backend API: http://localhost:3000"
echo "Database: localhost:5432"
echo "Redis: localhost:6379"

# Manter script rodando
wait
```

# ADR

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo para o DIYAPP V12, incluindo paleta de cores, tipografia, componentes de UI e wireframes de alta fidelidade para as 5 views principais. Como não posso criar um protótipo Figma diretamente, vou implementar um sistema de design funcional em HTML/CSS/JS com todos os estados especificados.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Design System</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <style>
        /* ===== RESET E BASE ===== */
        * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }

        :root {
            /* ===== TOKENS DE CORES (Design System V12) ===== */

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```terraform
# ============================================
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Terraform IaC
# Ambiente de Staging com 100% Uptime Target
# ============================================

# main.tf
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    docker = {
      source  = "kreuzwerker/docker"
      version = "3.0.2"
    }
  }
}

provider "docker" {
  host = "unix:///var/run/docker.sock"
}

# ============================================
# 1. REDIS CACHE
# ============================================
resource "docker_image" "redis" {
  name         = "redis:7-alpine"
  keep_locally = true
}

resource "docker_container" "redis" {
  name  = "diyapp-redis-staging"
  image = docker_image.redis.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 6379
    external = 6379
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/data"
    host_path      = "/var/lib/diyapp/redis"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
    interval = "10s"
    timeout  = "5s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "30s"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "cache"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
    "com.diyapp.slo"     = "availability-99.9"
  }
}

# ============================================
# 2. POSTGRESQL DATABASE
# ============================================
resource "docker_image" "postgres" {
  name         = "postgres:15-alpine"
  keep_locally = true
}

resource "docker_container" "postgres" {
  name  = "diyapp-postgres-staging"
  image = docker_image.postgres.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 5432
    external = 5432
  }

  env = [
    "POSTGRES_DB=diyapp_staging",
    "POSTGRES_USER=diyapp",
    "POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${random_password.db_password.result}",
    "POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS=--encoding=UTF-8 --locale=C"
  ]

  volumes {
    container_path = "/var/lib/postgresql/data"
    host_path      = "/var/lib/diyapp/postgres"
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
    interval = "15s"
    timeout  = "5s"
    retries  = 3
    start_period = "45s"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "database"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
    "com.diyapp.slo"     = "availability-99.9"
  }
}

resource "random_password" "db_password" {
  length  = 32
  special = false
}

# ============================================
# 3. DIYAPP APPLICATION
# ============================================
resource "docker_image" "diyapp" {
  name = "diyapp:v12-core"
  
  build {
    context = "."
    dockerfile = "Dockerfile.app"
    args = {
      NODE_ENV = "staging"
    }
  }
}

resource "docker_container" "diyapp" {
  count = 3  # 3 réplicas para alta disponibilidade
  name  = "diyapp-app-staging-${count.index}"
  image = docker_image.diyapp.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3000 + count.index
  }

  env = [
    "NODE_ENV=staging",
    "REDIS_URL=redis://diyapp-redis-staging:6379",
    "DATABASE_URL=postgresql://diyapp:${random_password.db_password.result}@diyapp-postgres-staging:5432/diyapp_staging",
    "PORT=3000",
    "INSTANCE_ID=${count.index}"
  ]

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "node", "/app/healthcheck.js"]
    interval = "30s"  # SLO: health check a cada 30s
    timeout  = "10s"
    retries  = 2
    start_period = "60s"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "application"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
    "com.diyapp.slo"     = "availability-99.9"
    "com.diyapp.replica" = count.index
  }

  depends_on = [
    docker_container.redis,
    docker_container.postgres
  ]
}

# ============================================
# 4. NGINX LOAD BALANCER
# ============================================
resource "docker_image" "nginx" {
  name         = "nginx:1.24-alpine"
  keep_locally = true
}

resource "docker_container" "nginx" {
  name  = "diyapp-lb-staging"
  image = docker_image.nginx.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 80
    external = 8080
  }

  ports {
    internal = 443
    external = 8443
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/etc/nginx/nginx.conf"
    host_path      = "${path.module}/nginx.conf"
    read_only      = true
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/etc/nginx/ssl"
    host_path      = "/etc/ssl/diyapp"
    read_only      = true
  }

  healthcheck {
    test     = ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
    interval = "30s"
    timeout  = "5s"
    retries  = 2
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "loadbalancer"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
    "com.diyapp.slo"     = "availability-99.9"
  }
}

# ============================================
# 5. MONITORING & OBSERVABILITY
# ============================================
resource "docker_image" "prometheus" {
  name         = "prom/prometheus:latest"
  keep_locally = true
}

resource "docker_container" "prometheus" {
  name  = "diyapp-prometheus-staging"
  image = docker_image.prometheus.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 9090
    external = 9090
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
    host_path      = "${path.module}/prometheus.yml"
    read_only      = true
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/prometheus"
    host_path      = "/var/lib/diyapp/prometheus"
  }

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "monitoring"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
  }
}

resource "docker_image" "grafana" {
  name         = "grafana/grafana:latest"
  keep_locally = true
}

resource "docker_container" "grafana" {
  name  = "diyapp-grafana-staging"
  image = docker_image.grafana.image_id
  restart = "unless-stopped"

  ports {
    internal = 3000
    external = 3001
  }

  volumes {
    container_path = "/var/lib/grafana"
    host_path      = "/var/lib/diyapp/grafana"
  }

  env = [
    "GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${random_password.grafana_password.result}",
    "GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel"
  ]

  networks_advanced {
    name = docker_network.staging_network.name
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.service" = "dashboard"
    "com.diyapp.env"     = "staging"
  }
}

resource "random_password" "grafana_password" {
  length  = 16
  special = true
}

# ============================================
# 6. DOCKER NETWORK
# ============================================
resource "docker_network" "staging_network" {
  name     = "diyapp-staging-network"
  driver   = "bridge"
  internal = false

  ipam_config {
    subnet  = "172.20.0.0/16"
    gateway = "172.20.0.1"
  }

  labels = {
    "com.diyapp.env" = "staging"
  }
}

# ============================================
# CONFIGURAÇÕES ADICIONAIS
# ============================================

# nginx.conf
resource "local_file" "nginx_config" {
  filename = "${path.module}/nginx.conf"
  content = <<-EOT
  events {
    worker_connections 1024;
  }

  http {
    upstream diyapp_backend {
      least_conn;
      server diyapp-app-staging-0:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
      server diyapp-app-staging-1:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
      server diyapp-app-staging-2:3000 max_fails=3 fail_timeout=30s;
      
      # Health check para SLO
      health_check interval=30s fails=2 passes=2 uri=/health match=status_ok;
    }

    match status_ok {
      status 200;
      body ~ "OK";
    }

    server {
      listen 80;
      listen 443 ssl;
      
      ssl_certificate /etc/nginx/ssl/diyapp.crt;
      ssl_certificate_key /etc/nginx/ssl/diyapp.key;

      location / {
        proxy_pass http://diyapp_backend;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        
        # Timeouts alinhados com SLOs
        proxy_connect_timeout 5s;
        proxy_send_timeout 10s;
        proxy_read_timeout 300s; # Para endpoints LLM
        
        # Circuit breaker
        proxy_next_upstream error timeout http_502 http_503 http_504;
        proxy_next_upstream_timeout 5s;
        proxy_next_upstream_tries 2;
      }

      location /health {
        access_log off;
        return 200 "OK";
        add_header Content-Type text/plain;
      }

      location /metrics {
        stub_status on;
        access_log off;
        allow 172.20.0.0/16;
        deny all;
      }
    }
  }
  EOT
}

# prometheus.yml
resource "local_file" "prometheus_config" {
  filename = "${path.module}/prometheus.yml"
  content = <<-EOT
  global:
    scrape_interval: 30s
    evaluation_interval: 30s

  scrape_configs:
    - job_name: 'diyapp-app'
      static_configs:
        - targets:
          - 'diyapp-app-staging-0:3000'
          - 'diyapp-app-staging-1:3000'
          - 'diyapp-app-staging-2:3000'
      metrics_path: '/metrics'

    - job_name: 'nginx'
      static_configs:
        - targets: ['diyapp-lb-staging:80']
      metrics_path: '/metrics'

    - job_name: 'redis'
      static_configs:
        - targets: ['diyapp-redis-staging:6379']

    - job_name: 'postgres'
      static_configs:
        - targets: ['diyapp-postgres-staging:5432']

  rule_files:
    - "alerts.yml"
  EOT
}

# alerts.yml para SLO monitoring
resource "local_file" "prometheus_alerts" {
  filename = "${path.module}/alerts.yml"
  content = <<-EOT
  groups:
    - name: diyapp_slo_alerts
      rules:
        # SLO: Disponibilidade 99.9%
        - alert: APIAvailabilityBelowSLO
          expr: |
            (1 - (sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5..",job="diyapp-app"}[5m]))
                  / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp-app"}[5m])))
            < 0.999
          for: 5m
          labels:
            severity: warning
            service: api
            slo: availability
          annotations:
            summary: "API availability below 99.9% SLO"
            description: "Error rate is consuming error budget. Current availability: {{ $value }}"
        
        # SLO: Latência P95 < 300ms
        - alert: APILatencyAboveSLO
          expr: |
            histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="diyapp-app"}[5m])) > 0.3
          for: 5m
          labels:
            severity: warning
            service: api
            slo: latency
          annotations:
            summary: "API P95 latency above 300ms SLO"
            description: "Current P95 latency: {{ $value }}s"
        
        # SLO: Error rate < 0.1%
        - alert: APIErrorRateAboveSLO
          expr: |
            (sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5..",job="diyapp-app"}[1h]))
             / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp-app"}[1h]))) > 0.001
          for: 5m
          labels:
            severity: critical
            service: api
            slo: error-rate
          annotations:
            summary: "API error rate above 0.1% SLO"
            description: "Current error rate: {{ $value }}"
        
        # Health check failures
        - alert: ServiceHealthCheckFailed
          expr: up{job=~"diyapp.*"} == 0
          for: 1m
          labels:
            severity: critical
          annotations:
            summary: "{{ $labels.job }} health check failed"
            description: "Service {{ $labels.instance }} is down"
        
        # Redis memory warning
        - alert: RedisMemoryHigh
          expr: redis_memory_used_bytes / redis_memory_max_bytes > 0.8
          for: 5m
          labels:
            severity: warning
            service: redis
          annotations:
            summary: "Redis memory usage high"
            description: "Redis is using {{ $value }}% of available memory"
        
        # Database connections warning
        - alert: PostgresConnectionsHigh
          expr: pg_stat_database_numbackends{datname="diyapp_staging"} > 50
          for: 5m
          labels:
            severity: warning
            service: postgres
          annotations:
            summary: "PostgreSQL connections high"
            description: "{{ $value }} active connections to database"
  EOT
}

# Dockerfile.app
resource "local_file" "dockerfile_app" {
  filename = "${path.module}/Dockerfile.app"
  content = <<-EOT
  FROM node:18-alpine AS builder
  
  WORKDIR /app
  
  COPY package*.json ./
  RUN npm ci --only=production
  
  FROM node:18-alpine
  
  WORKDIR /app
  
  COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
  COPY . .
  
  # Health check script para SLO monitoring
  RUN echo 'const http = require("http"); \
  const server = http.createServer((req, res) => { \
    if (req.url === "/health") { \
      res.writeHead(200); \
      res.end("OK"); \
    } else { \
      res.writeHead(404); \
      res.end(); \
    } \
  }); \
  server.listen(3001);' > /app/healthcheck.js
  
  # Métricas do Node.js
  ENV NODE_OPTIONS="--require @opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node/register"
  
  EXPOSE 3000
  EXPOSE 3001
  
  USER node
  
  CMD ["node", "server.js"]
  EOT
}

    name: 'http_requests_total',

```javascript
// src/index.js
require('dotenv').config();
require('express-async-errors');
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');

const logger = require('./utils/logger');
const errorHandler = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const requestLogger = require('./middleware/requestLogger');
const swaggerSpec = require('./config/swagger');
const database = require('./database/connection');

// Import routes
const authRoutes = require('./routes/auth.routes');
const projectRoutes = require('./routes/project.routes');
const healthRoutes = require('./routes/health.routes');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : '*',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});
app.use('/api/', limiter);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Request logging
app.use(requestLogger);

// API Documentation
app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerSpec));

// Health check (no auth required)
app.use('/api/health', healthRoutes);

// API Routes
app.use('/api/auth', authRoutes);
app.use('/api/projects', projectRoutes);

// 404 handler
app.use('*', (req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`
  });
});

// Error handling (must be last)
app.use(errorHandler);

// Database connection check and server start
async function startServer() {
  try {
    // Test database connection
    await database.raw('SELECT 1');
    logger.info('Database connection established successfully');

    app.listen(PORT, () => {
      logger.info(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
      logger.info(`API Documentation available at http://localhost:${PORT}/api-docs`);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to connect to database:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
  await database.destroy();
  process.exit(0);
});

process.on('SIGINT', async () => {
  logger.info('SIGINT received, shutting down gracefully');
  await database.destroy();
  process.exit(0);
});

startServer();

module.exports = app; // For testing
```

```javascript
// src/utils/logger.js
const winston = require('winston');
require('winston-daily-rotate-file');

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors, metadata } = winston.format;

// Mask sensitive data in logs
const maskSensitiveData = winston.format((info) => {
  const maskedInfo = { ...info };
  
  // Mask email
  if (maskedInfo.email) {
    maskedInfo.email = maskedInfo.email.replace(/(?<=.).(?=.*@)/g, '*');
  }
  
  // Mask tokens
  if (maskedInfo.token) {
    maskedInfo.token = '***MASKED***';
  }
  
  // Mask authorization headers
  if (maskedInfo.headers && maskedInfo.headers.authorization) {
    maskedInfo.headers.authorization = '***MASKED***';
  }
  
  // Mask any field containing 'password', 'secret', or 'key'
  Object.keys(maskedInfo).forEach(key => {
    if (typeof maskedInfo[key] === 'string' && 
        (key.toLowerCase().includes('password') || 
         key.toLowerCase().includes('secret') || 
         key.toLowerCase().includes('key'))) {
      maskedInfo[key] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return maskedInfo;
});

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: combine(
    errors({ stack: true }),
    timestamp(),
    maskSensitiveData(),
    metadata(),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v12-core' },
  transports: [
    // Console transport
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    }),
    // Daily rotate file transport
    new winston.transports.DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/application-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      maxFiles: '30d',
      maxSize: '20m'
    }),
    // Error log file
    new winston.transports.DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/error-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      level: 'error',
      maxFiles: '30d',
      maxSize: '20m'
    })
  ],
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/exceptions.log' })
  ],
  rejectionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/rejections.log' })
  ]
});

// Create a child logger with correlation ID
logger.childWithCorrelation = (correlationId) => {
  return logger.child({ correlationId });
};

module.exports = logger;
```

```javascript
// src/database/connection.js
const knex = require('knex');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

const environment = process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development';
const isTest = environment === 'test';

const config = {
  client: isTest ? 'sqlite3' : 'pg',
  connection: isTest 
    ? { filename: ':memory:' }
    : {
        host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
        port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
        user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
        password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
        database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v12',
        ssl: process.env.DB_SSL ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false
      },
  pool: {
    min: 2,
    max: 10,
    acquireTimeoutMillis: 30000,
    createTimeoutMillis: 30000,
    destroyTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
    reapIntervalMillis: 1000,
    createRetryIntervalMillis: 100
  },
  migrations: {
    directory: './src/database/migrations',
    tableName: 'knex_migrations'
  },
  seeds: {
    directory: './src/database/seeds'
  },
  debug: process.env.DB_DEBUG === 'true'
};

// SQLite specific configuration for tests
if (isTest) {
  config.pool = {
    afterCreate: (conn, cb) => {
      conn.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON', cb);
    }
  };
}

const db = knex(config);

// Add query logging in development
if (environment === 'development') {
  db.on('query', (query) => {
    logger.debug('Database query:', {
      sql: query.sql,
      bindings: query.bindings
    });
  });
}

// Health check function
db.healthCheck = async () => {
  try {
    await db.raw('SELECT 1');
    return { status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Database health check failed:', error);
    return { 
      status: 'unhealthy', 
      error: error.message,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString() 
    };
  }
};

module.exports = db;
```

```javascript
// src/database/migrations/20240101000000_create_users_table.js
/**
 * @param { import("knex").Knex } knex
 * @returns { Promise<void> }
 */
exports.up = async function(knex) {
  await knex.schema.createTable('users', (table) => {
    table.uuid('id').primary().defaultTo(knex.raw('gen_random_uuid()'));
    table.string('email').notNullable().unique();
    table.string('password_hash').notNullable();
    table.string('name');
    table.jsonb('metadata').defaultTo('{}');
    table.timestamp('created_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    table.timestamp('updated_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    
    table.index('email');
  });

  // Create updated_at trigger function for PostgreSQL
  if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
    await knex.raw(`
      CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
      RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
      BEGIN
        NEW.updated_at = NOW();
        RETURN NEW;
      END;
      $$ language 'plpgsql';
    `);

    await knex.raw(`
      CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at
      BEFORE UPDATE ON users
      FOR EACH ROW
      EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
    `);
  }
};

/**
 * @param { import("knex").Knex } knex
 * @returns { Promise<void> }
 */
exports.down = async function(knex) {
  if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
    await knex.raw('DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_users_updated_at ON users');
    await knex.raw('DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS update_updated_at_column');
  }
  
  await knex.schema.dropTableIfExists('users');
};
```

```javascript
// src/database/migrations/20240101000001_create_projects_table.js
/**
 * @param { import("knex").Knex } knex
 * @returns { Promise<void> }
 */
exports.up = async function(knex) {
  await knex.schema.createTable('projects', (table) => {
    table.uuid('id').primary().defaultTo(knex.raw('gen_random_uuid()'));
    table.string('name').notNullable();
    table.text('description');
    table.enum('status', ['draft', 'active', 'completed', 'archived']).defaultTo('draft');
    table.uuid('user_id').notNullable().references('id').inTable('users').onDelete('CASCADE');
    table.jsonb('metadata').defaultTo('{}');
    table.timestamp('created_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    table.timestamp('updated_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    
    table.index('user_id');
    table.index('status');
    table.index(['user_id', 'status']);
  });

  // Create updated_at trigger for projects
  if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
    await knex.raw(`
      CREATE TRIGGER update_projects_updated_at
      BEFORE UPDATE ON projects
      FOR EACH ROW
      EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
    `);
  }
};

/**
 * @param { import("knex").Knex } knex
 * @returns { Promise<void> }
 */
exports.down = async function(knex) {
  if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
    await knex.raw('DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_projects_updated_at ON projects');
  }
  
  await knex.schema.dropTableIfExists('projects');
};
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Boilerplate React

Vou criar um boilerplate React profissional com todas as configurações necessárias para atender aos critérios de performance (Lighthouse >90) e seguir os padrões estabelecidos no papel.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── public/
├── src/
│   ├── components/
│   ├── contexts/
│   ├── hooks/
│   ├── pages/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── stores/
│   ├── styles/
│   ├── types/
│   ├── utils/
│   ├── App.tsx
│   ├── index.tsx
│   └── routes.tsx
├── package.json
├── tsconfig.json
├── vite.config.ts
├── .eslintrc.json
├── .prettierrc
└── README.md
```

## 4. vite.config.ts

```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import { VitePWA } from 'vite-plugin-pwa';
import compression from 'vite-plugin-compression';
import { resolve } from 'path';

// https://vitejs.dev/config/
export default defineConfig(({ mode }) => ({
  plugins: [
    react(),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      ext: '.gz',
    }),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'brotliCompress',
      ext: '.br',
    }),
    VitePWA({
      registerType: 'autoUpdate',
      includeAssets: ['favicon.ico', 'apple-touch-icon.png', 'masked-icon.svg'],
      manifest: {
        name: 'DIYAPP V12 Core',
        short_name: 'DIYAPP',
        description: 'DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core Application',
        theme_color: '#2563eb',
        icons: [
          {
            src: 'pwa-192x192.png',
            sizes: '192x192',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
          {
            src: 'pwa-512x512.png',
            sizes: '512x512',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
        ],
      },
    }),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@components': resolve(__dirname, './src/components'),
      '@hooks': resolve(__dirname, './src/hooks'),
      '@pages': resolve(__dirname, './src/pages'),
      '@stores': resolve(__dirname, './src/stores'),
      '@styles': resolve(__dirname, './src/styles'),
      '@utils': resolve(__dirname, './src/utils'),
      '@types': resolve(__dirname, './src/types'),
    },
  },
  build: {
    target: 'es2020',
    minify: 'terser',
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: mode === 'production',
        drop_debugger: mode === 'production',
      },
    },
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          ui: ['lucide-react', 'clsx'],
          state: ['zustand'],
        },
        chunkFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        entryFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: ({ name }) => {
          if (/\.(gif|jpe?g|png|svg|webp|avif)$/.test(name ?? '')) {
            return 'assets/images/[name]-[hash][extname]';
          }
          if (/\.(woff2?|eot|ttf|otf)$/.test(name ?? '')) {
            return 'assets/fonts/[name]-[hash][extname]';
          }
          if (/\.css$/.test(name ?? '')) {
            return 'assets/css/[name]-[hash][extname]';
          }
          return 'assets/[name]-[hash][extname]';
        },
      },
    },
    cssCodeSplit: true,
    sourcemap: mode !== 'production',
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
  },
  preview: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
  },
}));
```

## 6. src/index.tsx

```typescript
import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client';
import { BrowserRouter } from 'react-router-dom';
import App from './App';
import

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura V12

### 1.1 Visão Geral
A V12 do DIYAPP evolui para uma arquitetura de microsserviços com foco em:
- **100% de autonomia** por squad
- **Zero-downtime deployments**
- **Observabilidade nativa** com OpenTelemetry
- **Resiliência automática** (circuit breaker, retry, fallback)

### 1.2 Princípios Arquiteturais
```yaml
architecture_principles:
  - Single Responsibility: Cada microsserviço gerencia um único domínio de negócio
  - Autonomous Squads: Cada squad é dona de seu ciclo de vida completo (DevOps)
  - Event-Driven: Comunicação assíncrona via eventos como padrão
  - API-First: Contratos de API definidos antes da implementação
  - Observability-by-Design: Telemetria embutida desde o dia 0
```

### 1.3 Topologia de Microsserviços

```
DIYAPP V12 - Arquitetura
├── API Gateway (Kong/NGINX)
│   ├── Rate limiting
│   ├── Authentication/Authorization
│   └── Request routing
├── Core Services
│   ├── User Service (Node.js/TypeScript)
│   │   ├── Gestão de usuários
│   │   ├── Autenticação JWT
│   │   └── Perfis e permissões
│   ├── Project Service (Python/FastAPI)
│   │   ├── Gestão de projetos DIY
│   │   ├── Templates e blueprints
│   │   └── Versionamento
│   └── AI Assistant Service (Python)
│       ├── Integração LLM
│       ├── Context management
│       └── Prompt engineering
├── Event Services
│   ├── Event Bus (Apache Kafka)
│   ├── Notification Service (Go)
│   │   ├── Email/SMS/Push
│   │   └── WhatsApp (Baileys)
│   └── Analytics Service (Node.js)
│       ├── Event processing
│       └── Real-time dashboards
├── Data Services
│   ├── PostgreSQL (dados transacionais)
│   ├── MongoDB (dados não estruturados)
│   ├── Redis (cache e sessões)
│   └── MinIO (armazenamento de arquivos)
└── Infrastructure
    ├── Kubernetes (EKS/GKE)
    ├── Istio (service mesh)
    ├── Prometheus + Grafana
    └── Jaeger (distributed tracing)
```

### 1.4 Padrões de Comunicação

```typescript
// ADR-001: Padrão de Comunicação entre Serviços
export interface ServiceCommunication {
  // 1. Síncrona (REST/gRPC) - apenas quando necessário
  synchronous: {
    protocol: 'REST' | 'gRPC';
    timeout: '2s';
    retryPolicy: {
      maxAttempts: 3;
      backoff: 'exponential';
    };
  };

  // 2. Assíncrona (Eventos) - padrão preferido
  asynchronous: {
    protocol: 'Apache Kafka';
    eventFormat: 'CloudEvents';
    schemaRegistry: 'Apicurio';
    deadLetterQueue: true;
  };

  // 3. Circuit Breaker obrigatório
  resilience: {
    circuitBreaker: {
      failureThreshold: '50%';
      resetTimeout: '30s';
      halfOpenMaxCalls: 10;
    };
  };
}
```

### 1.5 Observabilidade com OpenTelemetry

```yaml
# docker-compose.observability.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  # Collector
  otel-collector:
    image: otel/opentelemetry-collector:latest
    command: ["--config=/etc/otel-collector-config.yaml"]
    ports:
      - "4317:4317"   # gRPC
      - "4318:4318"   # HTTP
      - "8889:8889"   # Prometheus metrics
    volumes:
      - ./otel-config.yaml:/etc/otel-collector-config.yaml

  # Jaeger para tracing
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:latest
    ports:
      - "16686:16686" # UI
      - "14268:14268" # Collector

  # Prometheus + Grafana
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
```

### 1.6 Configuração OpenTelemetry para Node.js

```javascript
// src/instrumentation.js
const { NodeSDK } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-node');
const { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } = require('@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node');
const { OTLPTraceExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc');
const { OTLPMetricExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-grpc');
const { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics');
const { Resource } = require('@opentelemetry/resources');
const { SemanticResourceAttributes } = require('@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions');

// Configuração do recurso
const resource = new Resource({
  [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: process.env.SERVICE_NAME || 'user-service',
  [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: process.env.VERSION || '1.0.0',
  [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
});

// SDK de telemetria
const sdk = new NodeSDK({
  resource,
  traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter({
    url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4317',
  }),
  metricReader: new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
    exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
      url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4317',
    }),
    exportIntervalMillis: 60000, // 1 minuto
  }),
  instrumentations: [
    getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
      '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http': {
        ignoreIncomingPaths: ['/health', '/metrics'],
      },
      '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-express': {
        enabled: true,
      },
      '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-pg': {
        enabled: true,
      },
      '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-redis': {
        enabled: true,
      },
    }),
  ],
});

// Inicialização
sdk.start();

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  sdk.shutdown()
    .then(() => console.log('OpenTelemetry SDK shut down successfully'))
    .catch((error) => console.log('Error shutting down OpenTelemetry SDK', error))
    .finally(() => process.exit(0));
});
```

### 1.7 Padrões de Código por Linguagem

#### 1.7.1 Node.js/TypeScript
```typescript
// src/services/user.service.ts
import { Injectable, Inject } from '@nestjs/common';
import { OpentelemetryService } from '../telemetry/opentelemetry.service';
import { CircuitBreaker } from '../resilience/circuit-breaker.decorator';
import { Retry } from '../resilience/retry.decorator';
import { Logger } from '../logging/logger';

@Injectable()
export class UserService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(UserService.name);
  private readonly tracer;

  constructor(
    private readonly telemetry: OpentelemetryService,
    @Inject('USER_REPOSITORY') private userRepository,
  ) {
    this.tracer = telemetry.getTracer();
  }

  @CircuitBreaker({ failureThreshold: 0.5, resetTimeout: 30000 })
  @Retry({ maxAttempts: 3, backoff: 'exponential' })
  async getUserById(userId: string): Promise<User> {
    const span = this.tracer.startSpan('UserService.getUserById');
    
    try {
      span.setAttribute('user.id', userId);
      
      // Business logic
      const user = await this.userRepository.findById(userId);
      
      if (!user) {
        span.setStatus({ code: SpanStatusCode.ERROR, message: 'User not found' });
        throw new NotFoundException('User not found');
      }
      
      // Log structured
      this.logger.info('User retrieved successfully', {
        userId,
        executionTime: span.endTime - span.startTime,
      });
      
      return user;
    } catch (error) {
      span.recordException(error);
      span.setStatus({ code: SpanStatusCode.ERROR });
      this.logger.error('Failed to retrieve user', { userId, error });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      span.end();
    }
  }
}
```

#### 1.7.2 Python/FastAPI
```python
# app/services/project_service.py
from opentelemetry import trace
from opentelemetry.trace import Status, StatusCode
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import logging
from typing import Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
tracer = trace.get_tracer(__name__)

class ProjectService:
    def __init__(self, project_repository):
        self.project_repository = project_repository
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, expected_exception=Exception)
    def get_project(self, project_id: str, user_id: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        span = tracer.start_span("ProjectService.get_project")
        
        try:
            span.set_attribute("project.id", project_id)
            span.set_attribute("user.id", user_id)
            
            # Business logic
            project = self.project_repository.find_by_id(project_id, user_id)
            
            if not project:
                span.set_status(Status(StatusCode.ERROR, "Project not found"))
                logger.warning(f"Project not found", extra={
                    "project_id": project_id,
                    "user_id": user_id
                })
                return None
            
            # Log structured
            logger.info("Project retrieved successfully", extra={
                "project_id": project_id,
                "execution_time": span.end_time - span.start_time
            })
            
            return project
            
        except Exception as e:
            span.record_exception(e)
            span.set_status(Status(StatusCode.ERROR))
            logger.error(f"Failed to retrieve project: {str(e)}", extra={
                "project_id": project_id,
                "error": str(e)
            })
            raise
        finally:
            span.end()
```

### 1.8 Configuração do Service Mesh (Istio)

```yaml
# istio-config.yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: VirtualService
metadata:
  name: user-service
spec:
  hosts:
  - user-service
  http:
  - route:
    - destination:
        host: user-service
        subset: v1
      weight: 90
    - destination:
        host: user-service
        subset: v2
      weight: 10
    retries:
      attempts: 3
      perTryTimeout: 2s
      retryOn: gateway-error,connect-failure,refused-stream
---
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: DestinationRule
metadata:
  name: user-service
spec:
  host: user-service
  subsets:
  - name: v1
    labels:
      version: v1.0.0
  - name: v2
    labels:
      version: v1.1.0
  trafficPolicy:
    connectionPool:
      tcp:
        maxConnections: 100
      http:
        http1MaxPendingRequests: 10
        maxRequestsPerConnection: 10
    outlierDetection:
      consecutive5xxErrors: 5
      interval: 30s
      baseEjectionTime: 30s
      maxEjectionPercent: 50
```

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes de alta-fidelidade e fluxos de onboarding refinados, implementado como um dashboard premium funcional.

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO DIYAPP V12 CORE
# Backend com GraphQL + REST, PostgreSQL, RabbitMQ, JWT, Swagger, Testes
# Arquitetura limpa com separação de responsabilidades

# ==================== ESTRUTURA DE DIRETÓRIOS ====================
"""
diyapp-v12-core/
├── src/
│   ├── __init__.py
│   ├── main.py                      # Ponto de entrada da aplicação
│   ├── config.py                    # Configurações
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── connection.py           # Conexão PostgreSQL
│   │   ├── models.py               # SQLAlchemy models
│   │   └── migrations/             # Alembic migrations
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── rest/
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── routers/
│   │   │   │   ├── auth.py
│   │   │   │   ├── users.py
│   │   │   │   ├── projects.py
│   │   │   │   └── tasks.py
│   │   │   └── dependencies.py     # Dependências FastAPI
│   │   └── graphql/
│   │       ├── __init__.py
│   │       ├── schema.py           # Schema GraphQL
│   │       ├── resolvers/
│   │       │   ├── auth.py
│   │       │   ├── user.py
│   │       │   ├── project.py
│   │       │   └── task.py
│   │       └── mutations.py
│   ├── core/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── security.py             # JWT, hash, autenticação
│   │   ├── exceptions.py           # Exceções customizadas
│   │   └── logger.py               # Logging estruturado
│   ├── domain/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── entities.py             # Entidades de domínio
│   │   ├── repositories.py         # Interfaces de repositório
│   │   └── services.py             # Lógica de negócio
│   ├── infrastructure/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── repositories/
│   │   │   ├── user_repository.py
│   │   │   ├── project_repository.py
│   │   │   └── task_repository.py
│   │   └── queue/
│   │       ├── __init__.py
│   │       ├── connection.py       # Conexão RabbitMQ
│   │       ├── producer.py         # Produtor de mensagens
│   │       └── consumer.py         # Consumidor de mensagens
│   └── schemas/
│       ├── __init__.py
│       ├── auth.py
│       ├── user.py
│       ├── project.py
│       └── task.py
├── tests/
│   ├── __init__.py
│   ├── conftest.py                 # Fixtures pytest
│   ├── test_rest_api/
│   ├── test_graphql_api/
│   ├── test_services/
│   └── test_repositories/
├── alembic.ini                     # Configuração Alembic
├── requirements.txt
├── docker-compose.yml
├── Dockerfile
├── .env.example
└── README.md
"""

# ==================== requirements.txt ====================
"""
fastapi==0.104.1
uvicorn[standard]==0.24.0
sqlalchemy==2.0.23
alembic==1.12.1
psycopg2-binary==2.9.9
pydantic==2.5.0
pydantic-settings==2.1.0
python-jose[cryptography]==3.3.0
passlib[bcrypt]==1.7.4
python-multipart==0.0.6
strawberry-graphql==0.215.2
aio-pika==9.4.1
redis==5.0.1
httpx==0.25.1
python-dotenv==1.0.0
structlog==23.2.0
prometheus-client==0.19.0
pytest==7.4.3
pytest-asyncio==0.21.1
pytest-cov==4.1.0
factory-boy==3.3.0
faker==21.3.1
"""

# ==================== src/config.py ====================
import os
from typing import Optional
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings
from pydantic import PostgresDsn, RedisDsn, AmqpDsn, Field


class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP V12 Core"
    VERSION: str = "12.0.0"
    
    # Security
    SECRET_KEY: str = Field(default=os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-here-change-in-production"))
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS: int = 7
    
    # Database
    POSTGRES_SERVER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_SERVER", "localhost")
    POSTGRES_USER: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_USER", "diyapp")
    POSTGRES_PASSWORD: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_PASSWORD", "diyapp123")
    POSTGRES_DB: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_DB", "diyapp_v12")
    POSTGRES_PORT: str = os.getenv("POSTGRES_PORT", "5432")
    
    @property
    def SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI(self) -> PostgresDsn:
        return f"postgresql://{self.POSTGRES_USER}:{self.POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@{self.POSTGRES_SERVER}:{self.POSTGRES_PORT}/{self.POSTGRES_DB}"
    
    # RabbitMQ
    RABBITMQ_HOST: str = os.getenv("RABBITMQ_HOST", "localhost")
    RABBITMQ_PORT: int = int(os.getenv("RABBITMQ_PORT", "5672"))
    RABBITMQ_USER: str = os.getenv("RABBITMQ_USER", "guest")
    RABBITMQ_PASSWORD: str = os.getenv("RABBITMQ_PASSWORD", "guest")
    RABBITMQ_VHOST: str = os.getenv("RABBITMQ_VHOST", "/")
    
    @property
    def RABBITMQ_URL(self) -> str:
        return f"amqp://{self.RABBITMQ_USER}:{self.RABBITMQ_PASSWORD}@{self.RABBITMQ_HOST}:{self.RABBITMQ_PORT}{self.RABBITMQ_VHOST}"
    
    # Redis (para rate limiting)
    REDIS_URL: RedisDsn = Field(default="redis://localhost:6379/0")
    
    # CORS
    BACKEND_CORS_ORIGINS: list[str] = ["http://localhost:3000", "http://localhost:8000"]
    
    # Logging
    LOG_LEVEL: str = os.getenv("LOG_LEVEL", "INFO")
    
    # Feature flags
    ENABLE_GRAPHQL: bool = True
    ENABLE_REST: bool = True
    ENABLE_QUEUE: bool = True
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True


settings = Settings()

# ==================== src/core/logger.py ====================
import logging
import sys
import uuid
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Any, Dict
import structlog


class StructuredLogger:
    """Logger estruturado com correlation ID"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        structlog.configure(
            processors=[
                structlog.contextvars.merge_contextvars,
                structlog.processors.add_log_level,
                structlog.processors.StackInfoRenderer(),
                structlog.dev.set_exc_info,
                structlog.processors.TimeStamper(fmt="iso"),
                structlog.processors.JSONRenderer()
            ],
            wrapper_class=structlog.BoundLogger,
            logger_factory=structlog.PrintLoggerFactory(),
            cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
        )
        
        self._logger = structlog.get_logger()
    
    def bind(self, **kwargs):
        return self._logger.bind(**kwargs)
    
    def info(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        self._logger.info(event, **kwargs)
    
    def error(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        self._logger.error(event, **kwargs)
    
    def warning(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        self._logger.warning(event, **kwargs)
    
    def debug(self, event: str, **kwargs):
        self._logger.debug(event, **kwargs)
    
    def get_correlation_id(self) -> str:
        """Gera ou retorna correlation ID atual"""
        return str(uuid.uuid4())


logger = StructuredLogger()

# ==================== src/core/security.py ====================
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional, Union
from jose import JWTError, jwt
from passlib.context import CryptContext
from fastapi import HTTPException, status, Depends
from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials

from src.config import settings
from src.core.logger import logger


pwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")
security = HTTPBearer()


def verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    """Verifica senha com bcrypt"""
    return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)


def get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:
    """Gera hash bcrypt da senha"""
    return pwd_context.hash(password)


def create_access_token(
    data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None
) -> str:
    """Cria JWT access token"""
    to_encode = data.copy()
    if expires_delta:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta
    else:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
    
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "access"})
    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
    return encoded_jwt


def create_refresh_token(
    data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None
) -> str:
    """Cria JWT refresh token"""
    to_encode = data.copy()
    if expires_delta:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta
    else:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
    
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "refresh"})
    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
    return encoded_jwt


async def get_current_user(
    credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Dependency para obter usuário atual do token JWT"""
    credentials_exception = HTTPException(
        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
        detail="Could not validate credentials",
        headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
    )
    
    try:
        token = credentials.credentials
        payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
        
        if payload.get("type") != "access":
            raise credentials_exception
        
        user_id: str = payload.get("sub")
        if user_id is None:
            raise credentials_exception
        
        # Log seguro (sem dados sensíveis)
        logger.info("token_validated", user_id=user_id[:8] + "...")
        
        return {"id": user_id, "email": payload.get("email"), "role": payload.get("role")}
    
    except JWTError as e:
        logger.error("jwt_validation_failed", error=str(e))
        raise credentials_exception


async def get_current_active_user(
    current_user: Dict[str, Any] = Depends(get_current_user)
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Dependency para verificar se usuário está ativo"""
    # Aqui poderia verificar no banco se o usuário está ativo
    if not current_user.get("is_active", True):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Inactive user")
    return current_user


async def require_role(required_role: str):
    """Factory para verificar role do usuário"""
    async def role_checker(current_user: Dict[str, Any] = Depends(get_current_active_user)):
        if current_user.get("role") != required_role:
            logger.warning("insufficient_permissions", 
                         user_id=current_user.get("id")[:8] + "...",
                         required_role=required_role,
                         user_role=current_user.get("role"))
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,
                detail="Insufficient permissions"
            )
        return current_user
    return role_checker

# ==================== src/database/connection.py ====================
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from typing import AsyncGenerator, Optional
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession, create_async_engine, async_sessionmaker
from sqlalchemy.orm import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.pool import NullPool

from src.config import settings
from src.core.logger import logger


# Configuração do SQLAlchemy para PostgreSQL
DATABASE_URL = settings.SQLALCHEMY_DATABASE_URI.replace("postgresql://", "postgresql+asyncpg://")

engine = create_async_engine(
    DATABASE_URL,
    echo=False,
    pool_pre_ping=True,
    pool_recycle=300,
    pool_size=20,
    max_overflow=10,
)

AsyncSessionLocal = async_sessionmaker(
    engine,
    class_=AsyncSession,
    expire_on_commit=False,
    autocommit=False,
    autoflush=False,
)

Base = declarative_base()


@asynccontextmanager
async def get_db_session() -> AsyncGenerator[AsyncSession, None]:
    """Context manager para sessões de banco de dados"""
    session = AsyncSessionLocal()
    try:
        yield session
        await session.commit()
    except Exception as e:
        await session.rollback()
        logger.error("database_session_failed", error=str(e))
        raise
    finally:
        await session.close()


async def init_db():
    """Inicializa o banco de dados (cria tabelas)"""
    async with engine.begin() as conn:
        # Em produção, use Alembic migrations
        # await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
        pass
    
    logger.info("database_initialized")


async def close_db():
    """Fecha conexões do banco de dados"""
    await engine.dispose()
    logger.info("database_connections_closed")

# ==================== src/database/models.py ====================
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, Boolean, DateTime, ForeignKey, Text, JSON, Float
from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship
from sqlalchemy.sql import func
from datetime import datetime

from src.database.connection import Base


class User(Base):
    __tablename__ = "users"
    
    id = Column(String, primary_key=True, index=True)
    email = Column(String, unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    username = Column(String, unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    hashed_password = Column(String, nullable=False)
    full_name = Column(String)
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    is_verified = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    role = Column(String, default="user")  # user, admin, moderator
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    
    # Relationships
    projects = relationship("Project", back_populates="owner", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
    tasks = relationship("Task", back_populates="assigned_to")


class Project(Base):
    __tablename__ = "projects"
    
    id = Column(String, primary_key=True, index=True)
    name = Column(String, nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    status = Column(String, default="active")  # active, completed, archived
    visibility = Column(String, default="private")  # private, public, shared
    metadata = Column(JSON, default=dict)
    owner_id = Column(String, ForeignKey("users.id", ondelete="CASCADE"), nullable=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())
    
    # Relationships
    owner = relationship("User", back_populates="projects")
    tasks = relationship("Task", back_populates="project", cascade="all, delete-orphan")


class Task(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tasks"
    
    id = Column(String, primary_key=True, index=True)
    title = Column(String, nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    status = Column(String, default="pending")  # pending, in_progress, completed, blocked
    priority = Column(String, default="medium")  # low, medium, high, critical
    due_date = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))
    estimated_hours = Column(Float)
    actual_hours = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    metadata = Column(JSON, default=dict)
    project_id = Column(String, ForeignKey("projects.id", ondelete="CASCADE"), nullable=False)
    assigned_to_id = Column(String, ForeignKey("users.id", ondelete="SET

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Dashboard SPA

Vou criar um dashboard SPA React com TypeScript, Redux Toolkit para gerenciamento de estado, e componentes reutilizáveis que atendam aos critérios de performance e responsividade.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── public/
│   ├── index.html

├── package.json

└── README.md
```
