## 7. src/store/index.ts

```typescript
import { configureStore } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { useDispatch, useSelector, TypedUseSelectorHook } from 'react-redux';
import authReducer from './slices/authSlice';
import dashboardReducer from './slices/dashboardSlice';
import uiReducer from './slices/uiSlice';

export const store = configureStore({
  reducer: {
    auth: authReducer,
    dashboard: dashboardReducer,
    ui: uiReducer,
  },
  middleware: (getDefaultMiddleware) =>
    getDefaultMiddleware({
      serializableCheck: {
        ignoredActions: ['dashboard/setMetrics'],
        ignoredPaths: ['dashboard.chartData'],
      },
    }),
});

export type RootState = ReturnType<typeof store.getState>;
export type AppDispatch = typeof store.dispatch;

export const useAppDispatch: () => AppDispatch = useDispatch;
export const useAppSelector: TypedUseSelectorHook<RootState> = useSelector;
```

## 8. src/store/slices/dashboardSlice.ts

```typescript
import { createSlice, createAsyncThunk, PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { dashboardService } from '@services/dashboardService';
import { format, subDays } from 'date-fns';

export interface Metric {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  value: number;
  change: number;
  trend: 'up' | 'down' | 'stable';
  icon: string;
}

export interface ChartData {
  date: string;
  value: number;
  category: string;
}

export interface DashboardState {
  metrics: Metric[];
  chartData: ChartData[];
  recentActivities: Activity[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  lastUpdated: string | null;
}

export interface Activity {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  timestamp: string;
  type: 'success' | 'warning' | 'error' | 'info';
  user: string;
}

const initialState: DashboardState = {
  metrics: [],
  chartData: [],
  recentActivities: [],
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  lastUpdated: null,
};

export const fetchDashboardData = createAsyncThunk(
  'dashboard/fetchData',
  async (_, { rejectWithValue }) => {
    try {
      const [metrics, chartData, activities] = await Promise.all([
        dashboardService.getMetrics(),
        dashboardService.getChartData(),
        dashboardService.getRecentActivities(),
      ]);
      return { metrics, chartData, activities };
    } catch (error) {
      return rejectWithValue(error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to fetch dashboard data');
    }
  }
);

const dashboardSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'dashboard',
  initialState,
  reducers: {
    setMetrics: (state, action: PayloadAction<Metric[]>) => {
      state.metrics = action.payload;
    },
    setChartData: (state, action: PayloadAction<ChartData[]>) => {
      state.chartData = action.payload;
    },
    setLoading: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
      state.isLoading = action.payload;
    },
    clearError: (state) => {
      state.error = null;
    },
    updateMetric: (state, action: PayloadAction<{ id: string; value: number }>) => {
      const metric = state.metrics.find(m => m.id === action.payload.id);
      if (metric) {
        metric.value = action.payload.value;
      }
    },
  },
  extraReducers: (builder) => {
    builder
      .addCase(fetchDashboardData.pending, (state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      })
      .addCase(fetchDashboardData.fulfilled, (state, action) => {
        state.isLoading = false;
        state.metrics = action.payload.metrics;
        state.chartData = action.payload.chartData;
        state.recentActivities = action.payload.activities;
        state.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();
      })
      .addCase(fetchDashboardData.rejected, (state, action) => {
        state.isLoading = false;
        state.error = action.payload as string;
      });
  },
});

export const { setMetrics, setChartData, setLoading, clearError, updateMetric } = dashboardSlice.actions;
export default dashboardSlice.reducer;
```

## 9. src/services/dashboardService.ts

```typescript
import axios from 'axios';
import { format, subDays } from 'date-fns';
import type { Metric, ChartData, Activity } from '@store/slices/dashboardSlice';

const API_BASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL || 'https://api.diyapp.com/v1';

const api = axios.create({
  baseURL: API_BASE_URL,
  timeout: 10000,
  headers: {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  },
});

api.interceptors.request.use((config) => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('auth_token');
  if (token) {
    config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
  }
  return config;
});

api.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => response,
  (error) => {
    if (error.response?.status === 401) {
      localStorage.removeItem('auth_token');
      window.location.href = '/login';
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

export const dashboardService = {
  async getMetrics(): Promise<Metric[]> {
    try {
      const response = await api.get('/dashboard/metrics');
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      // Fallback to mock data for development
      return [
        { id: 'users', label: 'Total Users', value: 12480, change: 12.5, trend: 'up', icon: 'Users

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
-- Data Warehouse Schema
-- Version: 1.0.0
-- Created: 2024
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- RAW LAYER (Bronze) - Preserved source data
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw;

-- User events from application
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.user_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    platform VARCHAR(50),
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    event_properties JSONB,
    raw_payload JSONB NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_file VARCHAR(500),
    batch_id VARCHAR(100)
);

-- LLM API calls from gateway
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id VARCHAR(255),
    user_id UUID,
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER,
    completion_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status_code INTEGER,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_metadata JSONB,
    response_metadata JSONB,
    called_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_file VARCHAR(500),
    batch_id VARCHAR(100)
);

-- Application deployments
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.deployments (
    deployment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    environment VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    deployed_by VARCHAR(100),
    deployed_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    commit_hash VARCHAR(100),
    change_log TEXT,
    metadata JSONB,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- User feedback and ratings
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.user_feedback (
    feedback_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID,
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    rating INTEGER CHECK (rating >= 1 AND rating <= 5),
    feedback_text TEXT,
    sentiment_score DECIMAL(3,2),
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- STAGING LAYER (Silver) - Cleaned and standardized
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_user_events AS
SELECT 
    event_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(event_type)) as event_type,
    TRIM(event_name) as event_name,
    event_timestamp,
    CASE 
        WHEN platform IN ('ios', 'iOS', 'IOS') THEN 'iOS'
        WHEN platform IN ('android', 'Android', 'ANDROID') THEN 'Android'
        WHEN platform IN ('web', 'Web', 'WEB') THEN 'Web'
        ELSE COALESCE(platform, 'unknown')
    END as platform,
    CASE 
        WHEN device_type IN ('mobile', 'Mobile', 'MOBILE') THEN 'mobile'
        WHEN device_type IN ('desktop', 'Desktop', 'DESKTOP') THEN 'desktop'
        WHEN device_type IN ('tablet', 'Tablet', 'TABLET') THEN 'tablet'
        ELSE COALESCE(device_type, 'unknown')
    END as device_type,
    app_version,
    UPPER(TRIM(country_code)) as country_code,
    event_properties,
    ingested_at,
    DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date
FROM raw.user_events
WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
  AND event_type IS NOT NULL
  AND event_name IS NOT NULL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_llm_calls AS
SELECT 
    call_id,
    request_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(feature_name)) as feature_name,
    LOWER(TRIM(provider)) as provider,
    TRIM(model_name) as model_name,
    COALESCE(prompt_tokens, 0) as prompt_tokens,
    COALESCE(completion_tokens, 0) as completion_tokens,
    COALESCE(total_tokens, 0) as total_tokens,
    COALESCE(cost_usd, 0) as cost_usd,
    COALESCE(latency_ms, 0) as latency_ms,
    status_code,
    error_message,
    called_at,
    ingested_at,
    DATE(called_at) as call_date
FROM raw.llm_calls
WHERE called_at IS NOT NULL
  AND feature_name IS NOT NULL
  AND provider IS NOT NULL
  AND model_name IS NOT NULL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_deployments AS
SELECT 
    deployment_id,
    version,
    LOWER(TRIM(environment)) as environment,
    deployed_by,
    deployed_at,
    commit_hash,
    change_log,
    DATE(deployed_at) as deploy_date
FROM raw.deployments
WHERE deployed_at IS NOT NULL
  AND version IS NOT NULL
  AND environment IS NOT NULL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_user_feedback AS
SELECT 
    feedback_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(feature_name)) as feature_name,
    CASE 
        WHEN rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5 THEN rating
        ELSE NULL
    END as rating,
    feedback_text,
    CASE 
        WHEN sentiment_score BETWEEN -1 AND 1 THEN sentiment_score
        ELSE NULL
    END as sentiment_score,
    created_at,
    DATE(created_at) as feedback_date
FROM raw.user_feedback
WHERE created_at IS NOT NULL;

-- ============================================
-- MART LAYER (Gold) - Business-ready data
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts;

-- Product metrics for PM
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts.product;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.product.daily_active_users AS
SELECT 
    event_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as dau,
    COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as daily_sessions,
    COUNT(*) as total_events,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'page_view' THEN user_id END) as page_view_users,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'conversion' THEN user_id END) as conversion_users
FROM staging.stg_user_events
GROUP BY event_date;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.product.feature_adoption AS
SELECT 
    event_date,
    feature_name,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as unique_users,
    COUNT(*) as total_uses,
    AVG(CASE WHEN event_properties->>'duration' ~ '^\d+$' 
          THEN (event_properties->>'duration')::INTEGER 
          ELSE NULL END) as avg_duration_seconds
FROM staging.stg_user_events
WHERE event_name LIKE 'feature_%'
GROUP BY event_date, feature_name;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.product.funnel_conversion AS
WITH funnel_steps AS (
    SELECT 
        user_id,
        session_id,
        event_date,
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_name = 'signup_start' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as step1_signup_start,
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_name = 'signup_complete' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as step2_signup_complete,
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_name = 'onboarding_start' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as step3_onboarding_start,
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_name = 'onboarding_complete' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as step4_onboarding_complete,
        MAX(CASE WHEN event_name = 'first_feature_use' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as step5_first_feature_use
    FROM staging.stg_user_events
    WHERE event_name IN ('signup_start', 'signup_complete', 'onboarding_start', 
                         'onboarding_complete', 'first_feature_use')
    GROUP BY user_id, session_id, event_date
)
SELECT 
    event_date,
    COUNT(*) as total_sessions,
    SUM(step1_signup_start) as signup_started,
    SUM(step2_signup_complete) as signup_completed,
    SUM(step3_onboarding_start) as onboarding_started,
    SUM(step4_onboarding_complete) as onboarding_completed,
    SUM(step5_first_feature_use) as first_feature_used,
    ROUND(100.0 * SUM(step2_signup_complete) / NULLIF(SUM(step1_signup_start), 0), 2) as signup_conversion_rate,
    ROUND(100.0 * SUM(step5_first_feature_use) / NULLIF(SUM(step1_signup_start), 0), 2) as overall_conversion_rate
FROM funnel_steps
GROUP BY event_date;

-- AI metrics for AI Ops and LLM Specialist
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts.ai;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ai.llm_cost_by_feature AS
SELECT 
    call_date,
    feature_name,
    provider,
    model_name,
    COUNT(*) as total_calls,
    SUM(prompt_tokens) as total_prompt_tokens,
    SUM(completion_tokens) as total_completion_tokens,
    SUM(total_tokens) as total_tokens,
    SUM(cost_usd) as total_cost_usd,
    AVG(cost_usd) as avg_cost_per_call,
    AVG(latency_ms) as avg_latency_ms,
    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code != 200 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed_calls,
    ROUND(100.0 * SUM(CASE WHEN status_code != 200 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) / COUNT(*), 2) as error_rate
FROM staging.stg_llm_calls
GROUP BY call_date, feature_name, provider, model_name;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ai.model_performance_daily AS
SELECT 
    call_date,
    provider,
    model_name,
    COUNT(*) as call_count,
    AVG(latency_ms) as avg_latency,
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) as p50_latency,
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) as p95_latency,
    AVG(total_tokens) as avg_tokens_per_call,
    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code = 200 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as successful_calls,
    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code != 200 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed_calls
FROM staging.stg_llm_calls
GROUP BY call_date, provider, model_name;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ai.token_consumption_trend AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', called_at) as hour_bucket,
    feature_name,
    provider,
    SUM(total_tokens) as tokens_per_hour,
    SUM(cost_usd) as cost_per_hour,
    COUNT(*) as calls_per_hour
FROM staging.stg_llm_calls
GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('hour', called_at), feature_name, provider;

-- Operations metrics for SRE and Squad Leader
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts.ops;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ops.deploy_frequency AS
SELECT 
    deploy_date,
    environment,
    COUNT(*) as deployments_count,
    STRING_AGG(version, ', ' ORDER BY deployed_at) as versions_deployed,
    MIN(deployed_at) as first_deploy_time,
    MAX(deployed_at) as last_deploy_time
FROM staging.stg_deployments
GROUP BY deploy_date, environment;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ops.incident_metrics AS
WITH incidents AS (
    SELECT 
        event_date,
        COUNT(*) as total_incidents,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as affected_sessions,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_properties->>'severity' = 'high' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as high_severity_incidents,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_properties->>'severity' = 'medium' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as medium_severity_incidents,
        SUM(CASE WHEN event_properties->>'severity' = 'low' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as low_severity_incidents
    FROM staging.stg_user_events
    WHERE event_name = 'error_occurred'
    GROUP BY event_date
)
SELECT 
    event_date,
    total_incidents,
    affected_sessions,
    high_severity_incidents,
    medium_severity_incidents,
    low_severity_incidents,
    ROUND(100.0 * high_severity_incidents / NULLIF(total_incidents, 0), 2) as high_severity_percentage
FROM incidents;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.ops.sprint_velocity AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('week', event_date) as week_start,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as weekly_active_users,
    COUNT(*) as total_events,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'feature_completion' THEN event_properties->>'feature_id' END) as features_completed,
    AVG(CASE WHEN event_name = 'task_completed' 
          THEN (event_properties->>'completion_time')::DECIMAL 
          ELSE NULL END) as avg_task_completion_hours
FROM staging.stg_user_events
GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('week', event_date);

-- ============================================
-- DIMENSION TABLES
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS dimensions;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dimensions.dim_date (
    date_id DATE PRIMARY KEY,

    quarter INTEGER NOT NULL,
    month INTEGER NOT NULL,
    month_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    week INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_of_month INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_of_week INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    is_weekend BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    is_holiday BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dimensions.dim_user (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    created_at TIMESTAMP,
    signup_source VARCHAR(100),
    plan_type VARCHAR(50),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    last_active_date DATE,
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dimensions.dim_feature (
    feature_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    feature_category VARCHAR(50),
    launch_date DATE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    owner_team VARCHAR(100),
    description TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dimensions.dim_llm_model (
    model_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    context_length INTEGER,
    input_cost_per_token DECIMAL(12,10),
    output_cost_per_token DECIMAL(12,10),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    supported_features JSONB,
    UNIQUE(provider, model_name)
);

-- ============================================

CREATE INDEX idx_raw_user_events_timestamp ON raw.user_events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_user_events_user_id ON raw.user_events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_called_at ON raw.llm_calls(called_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_feature ON raw.llm_calls(feature_name);

CREATE INDEX idx_stg_user_events_date ON staging.stg_user_events(event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_user_events_user_date ON staging.stg_user_events(user_id, event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_llm_calls_date ON staging.stg_llm_calls(call_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_llm_calls_feature_date ON staging.stg_llm_calls(feature_name, call_date);

CREATE INDEX idx_mart_product_dau_date ON marts.product.daily_active_users(event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_ai_cost_date ON marts.ai.llm_cost_by_feature(call_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_ops_deploy_date ON marts.ops.deploy_frequency(deploy_date);

-- ============================================
-- VIEWS FOR COMMON QUERIES
-- ============================================

CREATE VIEW vw_daily_metrics_summary AS
SELECT 
    d.event_date,
    COALESCE(d.dau, 0) as daily_active_users,
    COALESCE(f.total_uses, 0) as total_feature_uses,
    COALESCE(c.total_cost_usd, 0) as daily_llm_cost,
    COALESCE(deploy.deployments_count, 0) as deployments_count,
    COALESCE(inc.total_incidents, 0) as daily_incidents
FROM marts.product.daily_active_users d
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT event_date, SUM(total_uses) as total_uses
    FROM marts.product.feature_adoption 
    GROUP BY event_date
) f ON d.event_date = f.event_date
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT call_date, SUM(total_cost_usd) as total_cost_usd
    FROM marts.ai.llm_cost_by_feature 
    GROUP BY call_date
) c ON d.event_date = c.call_date
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT deploy_date, SUM(deployments_count) as deployments_count
    FROM marts.ops.deploy_frequency 
    WHERE environment = 'production'
    GROUP BY deploy_date
) deploy ON d.event_date = deploy.deploy_date
LEFT JOIN marts.ops.incident_metrics inc ON d.event_date = inc.event_date;

CREATE VIEW vw_feature_performance AS
SELECT 
    f.feature_name,
    f.event_date,
    f.unique_users,
    f.total_uses,
    COALESCE(c.total_calls, 0) as llm_calls,
    COALESCE(c.total_cost_usd, 0) as llm_cost,
    COALESCE(fb.avg_rating, 0) as avg_rating,
    COALESCE(fb.feedback

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura (ADR-001)

### Architecture Decision Record
**ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços para V12 Core**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

**CONTEXTO:**
A V11 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade devido à arquitetura monolítica. Necessitamos de:
1. Deploy independente por funcionalidade
2. Escalabilidade granular por componente
3. Isolamento de falhas
4. Time-to-market mais rápido para novas features
5. Suporte a múltiplas linguagens por domínio

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em containers Docker com orquestração Kubernetes. Cada microsserviço será:
- Independentemente implantável
- Com banco de dados próprio quando necessário
- Comunicando-se via API REST/GraphQL ou eventos assíncronos
- Monitorado individualmente

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simplicidade operacional, debugging fácil. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, deploy acoplado.
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços leves (Serverless) - Prós: Escalabilidade automática, custo por uso. Contras: Vendor lock-in, cold starts.
- **Opção C:** Microsserviços em containers (escolhida) - Prós: Portabilidade, controle total, ecossistema maduro. Contras: Complexidade operacional.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Escalabilidade independente por serviço
- Deploys mais rápidos e seguros
- Isolamento de falhas
- Flexibilidade tecnológica

**Negativas:**
- Maior complexidade operacional
- Overhead de rede
- Necessidade de observabilidade distribuída
- Gerenciamento de dados distribuídos

**Riscos:**
- Latência em chamadas entre serviços (mitigar com cache e design assíncrono)
- Debugging distribuído (mitigar com tracing distribuído)
- Consistência de dados (mitigar com padrões SAGA e eventos)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-07-15

## 2. Diagrama de Containers e Especificação Técnica

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml - Ambiente de desenvolvimento
version: '3.8'

services:
  # API Gateway
  api-gateway:
    build: ./services/api-gateway
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth-service:3001
      - USER_SERVICE_URL=http://user-service:3002
      - PROJECT_SERVICE_URL=http://project-service:3003
      - AI_SERVICE_URL=http://ai-service:3004
    depends_on:
      - auth-service
      - user-service
      - project-service
      - ai-service
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Auth Service
  auth-service:
    build: ./services/auth
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=auth-db
      - DB_PORT=5432
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - REDIS_PORT=6379
    depends_on:
      - auth-db
      - redis
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # User Service
  user-service:
    build: ./services/user
    ports:
      - "3002:3002"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=user-db
      - DB_PORT=5432
    depends_on:
      - user-db
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Project Service
  project-service:
    build: ./services/project
    ports:
      - "3003:3003"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=project-db
      - DB_PORT=5432
      - MINIO_HOST=minio
      - MINIO_PORT=9000
    depends_on:
      - project-db
      - minio
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # AI Service
  ai-service:
    build: ./services/ai
    ports:
      - "3004:3004"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - RABBITMQ_HOST=rabbitmq
      - RABBITMQ_PORT=5672
    depends_on:
      - rabbitmq
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Databases
  auth-db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=auth_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=auth_user
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${AUTH_DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - auth-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  user-db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=user_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=user_user
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${USER_DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - user-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  project-db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=project_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=project_user
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${PROJECT_DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - project-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Message Queue
  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3-management-alpine
    ports:
      - "5672:5672"
      - "15672:15672"
    environment:
      - RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER=${RABBITMQ_USER}
      - RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS=${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD}
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Object Storage
  minio:
    image: minio/minio
    ports:
      - "9000:9000"
      - "9001:9001"
    environment:
      - MINIO_ROOT_USER=${MINIO_ROOT_USER}
      - MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD=${MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD}
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    volumes:
      - minio-data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Monitoring
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus-data:/prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    ports:
      - "3005:3000"
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana-data:/var/lib/grafana
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  auth-data:
  user-data:
  project-data:
  minio-data:
  prometheus-data:
  grafana-data:
```

## 3. Padrões de Código e Estrutura

```javascript
// services/auth/src/index.js - Exemplo de estrutura de microsserviço
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { logger, requestLogger } = require('./utils/logger');
const { errorHandler } = require('./middlewares/errorHandler');
const { connectDB } = require('./config/database');
const { connectRedis } = require('./config/redis');
const authRoutes = require('./routes/auth.routes');
const healthRoutes = require('./routes/health.routes');

class AuthService {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.PORT || 3001;
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    // Security middleware
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || ['http://localhost:3000'],
      credentials: true
    }));
    
    // Rate limiting
    const limiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
      max: 100 // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
    });
    this.app.use('/api/', limiter);
    
    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
    
    // Request logging
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    this.app.use('/api/auth', authRoutes);
    this.app.use('/health', healthRoutes);
    
    // 404 handler
    this.app.use('*', (req, res) => {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: 'Not Found',
        message: `Route ${req.originalUrl} not found`
      });
    });
  }

  setupErrorHandling() {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  async start() {
    try {
      // Connect to dependencies
      await connectDB();
      await connectRedis();
      
      // Start server
      this.server = this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
        logger.info(`Auth Service running on port ${this.port}`);
        logger.info(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV}`);
      });
      
      // Graceful shutdown
      process.on('SIGTERM', this.gracefulShutdown.bind(this));
      process.on('SIGINT', this.gracefulShutdown.bind(this));
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start Auth Service:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }

  gracefulShutdown() {
    logger.info('Received shutdown signal, closing server...');
    this.server.close(() => {
      logger.info('Server closed');
      process.exit(0);
    });
    
    // Force shutdown after 10 seconds
    setTimeout(() => {
      logger.error('Could not close connections in time, forcefully shutting down');
      process.exit(1);
    }, 10000);
  }
}

// Start service if running directly
if (require.main === module) {
  const service = new AuthService();
  service.start();
}

module.exports = AuthService;
```

```javascript
// services/auth/src/utils/logger.js - Logging padronizado
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

const logFormat = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss' }),
  winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
  winston.format.json()
);

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: logFormat,
  defaultMeta: { service: 'auth-service' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' })
  ]
});

// Request logger middleware
const requestLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const requestId = req.headers['x-request-id'] || uuidv4();
  const startTime = Date.now();
  
  // Add request ID to request and response
  req.requestId = requestId;
  res.setHeader('X-Request-ID', requestId);
  
  // Log request
  logger.info({
    type: 'REQUEST',
    requestId,
    method: req.method,
    url: req.originalUrl,
    ip: req.ip,
    userAgent: req.get('user-agent')
  });
  
  // Log response when finished
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
    logger.info({
      type: 'RESPONSE',
      requestId,
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      duration: `${duration}ms`,
      contentLength: res.get('content-length')
    });
  });
  
  next();
};

module.exports = { logger, requestLogger };
```

## 4. Pipeline CI/CD com Rollback Automático

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd-pipeline.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline with Auto Rollback

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]
  workflow_dispatch:

env:
  REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}

jobs:
  # Testes e Qualidade
  test-and-quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: npm ci
      
    - name: Run unit tests
      run: npm test -- --coverage
      
    - name: Run integration tests
      run: npm run test:integration
      env:
        TEST_DB_URL: postgresql://test:test@localhost:5432/test_db
        TEST_REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379
        
    - name: Security scan
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
        
    - name: Code quality
      uses: sonarsource/sonarqube-scan-action@master
      env:
        SONAR_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SONAR_TOKEN }}
        SONAR_HOST_URL: ${{ secrets.SONAR_HOST_URL }}
        
    - name: Upload test results
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      if: always()
      with:
        name: test-results
        path: |
          coverage/
          test-results.xml

  # Build e Push de Containers
  build-and-push:
    needs: test-and-quality
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && (github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' || github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop')
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth, user, project, ai]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Log in to Container Registry
      uses: docker/login-action@v2
      with:
        registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
        username: ${{ github.actor }}
        password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
        
    - name: Extract metadata
      id: meta
      uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
      with:
        images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}-${{ matrix.service }}
        tags: |
          type=ref,event=branch
          type=sha,prefix={{branch}}-
          type=raw,value=latest,enable={{is_default_branch}}
          
    - name: Build and push
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
        push: true
        tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
        labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

  # Deploy para Staging
  deploy-staging:
    needs: build-and-push
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout
      uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
    - name: Configure kubectl
      uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v3
      with:
        version: 'latest'
        
    - name: Deploy to staging
      run: |
        kubectl config use-context staging-cluster
        kubectl apply -f k8s/staging/
        kubectl rollout status deployment/api-gateway --timeout=300s
        
    - name: Run smoke tests
      run: |
        npm run test:smoke -- --base-url=${{ secrets.STAGING_URL }}
        
    - name: Notify Slack
      uses: 8398a7/action-slack@v3
      with:
        status: ${{ job.status }}
        author_name: CI/CD Pipeline
        fields: repo,message,commit,author,action
      env:
        SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL: ${{ secrets.SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL }}

  # Deploy para Production com Canary e Rollback
  deploy-production:
    needs: [test-and-quality, build-and-push]
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    environment: production
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout
      uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
    - name: Configure kubectl
      uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v3
      
    - name: Deploy canary (10%)
      id: canary-deploy
      run: |
        kubectl config use-context production-cluster
        
        # Deploy canary version
        kubectl apply -f k8s/production/canary/
        
        # Wait for canary to be ready
        kubectl rollout status deployment/api-gateway-canary --timeout=180s
        
        # Run canary tests

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]

            border: 1px solid var(--border-medium);
            border-radius: var(--radius-md);
            background-color: var(--bg-primary);
            color: var(--text-primary);

// 4. prisma/schema.prisma
generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

model User {
  id           String    @id @default(uuid())
  email        String    @unique
  passwordHash String    @map("password_hash")
  name         String?
  role         UserRole  @default(USER)
  isActive     Boolean   @default(true) @map("is_active")
  lastLogin    DateTime? @map("last_login")
  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt    DateTime  @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  projects     Project[]
  aiAgents     AIAgent[]
  
  @@map("users")
}

enum UserRole {
  USER
  ADMIN
  SUPER_ADMIN
}

model Project {
  id          String   @id @default(uuid())
  name        String
  description String?
  status      ProjectStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  userId      String   @map("user_id")
  config      Json?
  metadata    Json?
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  aiAgents    AIAgent[]
  
  @@map("projects")
}

enum ProjectStatus {
  ACTIVE
  ARCHIVED
  DELETED
}

model AIAgent {
  id          String      @id @default(uuid())
  name        String
  type        AgentType   @default(CUSTOM)
  config      Json
  status      AgentStatus @default(IDLE)
  projectId   String      @map("project_id")
  userId      String      @map("user_id")
  lastActive  DateTime?   @map("last_active")
  metadata    Json?
  createdAt   DateTime    @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt   DateTime    @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  project     Project     @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  user        User        @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@map("ai_agents")
}

enum AgentType {
  CUSTOM
  PREBUILT
  HYBRID
}

enum AgentStatus {
  IDLE
  RUNNING
  PAUSED
  ERROR
  COMPLETED
}

// 5. src/core/utils/logger.ts
import pino from 'pino';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';

export class Logger {
  private static instance: pino.Logger;
  
  static getInstance(): pino.Logger {
    if (!Logger.instance) {
      Logger.instance = pino({
        level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
        transport: {
          target: 'pino-pretty',
          options: {
            colorize: true,
            translateTime: 'SYS:standard',
            ignore: 'pid,hostname'
          }
        },
        serializers: {
          req: (req) => ({
            id: req.id,
            method: req.method,
            url: req.url,
            correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id']
          }),
          res: (res) => ({
            statusCode: res.statusCode,
            correlationId: res.req?.headers['x-correlation-id']
          }),
          err: pino.stdSerializers.err
        }
      });
    }
    return Logger.instance;
  }
  
  static generateCorrelationId(): string {
    return randomUUID();
  }
  
  static maskSensitiveData(data: any): any {
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;
    
    const masked = { ...data };
    const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'email', 'cpf', 'creditCard', 'apiKey'];
    
    for (const field of sensitiveFields) {
      if (masked[field]) {
        masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
      }
    }
    
    return masked;
  }
}

// 6. src/core/utils/redis.client.ts
import IORedis from 'ioredis';
import { Logger } from './logger';

export class RedisClient {
  private static instance: IORedis;
  private static isConnected = false;
  
  static getInstance(): IORedis {
    if (!RedisClient.instance) {
      const logger = Logger.getInstance();
      
      RedisClient.instance = new IORedis({
        host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
        port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
        password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
        retryStrategy: (times) => {
          const delay = Math.min(times * 100, 3000);
          logger.warn(`Redis reconnecting attempt ${times}, delay: ${delay}ms`);
          return delay;
        },
        maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
        enableReadyCheck: true,
        connectTimeout: 10000,
        commandTimeout: 5000
      });
      
      RedisClient.instance.on('connect', () => {
        logger.info('Redis connected');
        RedisClient.isConnected = true;
      });
      
      RedisClient.instance.on('error', (error) => {
        logger.error({ error }, 'Redis connection error');
        RedisClient.isConnected = false;
      });
      
      RedisClient.instance.on('close', () => {
        logger.warn('Redis connection closed');
        RedisClient.isConnected = false;
      });
    }
    
    return RedisClient.instance;
  }
  
  static async healthCheck(): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      const client = RedisClient.getInstance();
      await client.ping();
      return RedisClient.isConnected;
    } catch (error) {
      Logger.getInstance().error({ error }, 'Redis health check failed');
      return false;
    }
  }
  
  static async withCircuitBreaker<T>(
    operation: () => Promise<T>,
    fallback: () => Promise<T>,
    operationName: string
  ): Promise<T> {
    const logger = Logger.getInstance();
    
    if (!RedisClient.isConnected) {
      logger.warn(`Redis circuit breaker open for ${operationName}, using fallback`);
      return fallback();
    }
    
    try {
      return await operation();
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error({ error, operationName }, 'Redis operation failed');
      RedisClient.isConnected = false;
      return fallback();
    }
  }
}

// 7. src/core/utils/bullmq.client.ts
import { Queue, Worker, QueueEvents, Job } from 'bullmq';
import { RedisClient } from './redis.client';
import { Logger } from './logger';

export class BullMQClient {
  private static queues: Map<string, Queue> = new Map();
  private static workers: Map<string, Worker> = new Map();
  private static queueEvents: Map<string, QueueEvents> = new Map();
  
  static getQueue(queueName: string): Queue {
    if (!BullMQClient.queues.has(queueName)) {
      const queue = new Queue(queueName, {
        connection: RedisClient.getInstance(),
        defaultJobOptions: {
          attempts: 3,
          backoff: {
            type: 'exponential',
            delay: 1000
          },
          removeOnComplete: 100,
          removeOnFail: 1000
        }
      });
      
      BullMQClient.queues.set(queueName, queue);
      
      // Set up queue events for monitoring
      const queueEvents = new QueueEvents(queueName, {
        connection: RedisClient.getInstance()
      });
      
      queueEvents.on('completed', ({ jobId }) => {
        Logger.getInstance().info({ jobId, queueName }, 'Job completed');
      });
      
      queueEvents.on('failed', ({ jobId, failedReason }) => {
        Logger.getInstance().error({ jobId, queueName, failedReason }, 'Job failed');
      });
      
      BullMQClient.queueEvents.set(queueName, queueEvents);
    }
    
    return BullMQClient.queues.get(queueName)!;
  }
  
  static createWorker<T>(
    queueName: string,
    processor: (job: Job<T>) => Promise<any>,
    concurrency: number = 1
  ): Worker {
    if (BullMQClient.workers.has(queueName)) {
      return BullMQClient.workers.get(queueName)!;
    }
    
    const worker = new Worker(
      queueName,
      async (job) => {
        const logger = Logger.getInstance();
        const startTime = Date.now();
        
        try {
          logger.info({
            jobId: job.id,
            queueName,
            data: Logger.maskSensitiveData(job.data),
            attempt: job.attemptsMade
          }, 'Processing job');
          
          const result = await processor(job);
          const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
          
          logger.info({
            jobId: job.id,
            queueName,
            duration,
            attempt: job.attemptsMade
          }, 'Job processed successfully');
          
          return result;
        } catch (error) {
          const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
          
          logger.error({
            jobId: job.id,
            queueName,
            duration,
            error,
            attempt: job.attemptsMade
          }, 'Job processing failed');
          
          throw error;
        }
      },
      {
        connection: RedisClient.getInstance(),
        concurrency,
        limiter: {
          max: 10,
          duration: 1000
        }
      }
    );
    
    BullMQClient.workers.set(queueName, worker);
    return worker;
  }
  
  static async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    const logger = Logger.getInstance();
    
    // Close all workers
    for (const [queueName, worker] of BullMQClient.workers) {
      await worker.close();
      logger.info(`Worker for queue ${queueName} closed`);
    }
    
    // Close all queues
    for (const [queueName, queue] of BullMQClient.queues) {
      await queue.close();
      logger.info(`Queue ${queueName} closed`);
    }
    
    // Close all queue events
    for (const [queueName, queueEvents] of BullMQClient.queueEvents) {
      await queueEvents.close();
      logger.info(`Queue events for ${queueName} closed`);
    }
    
    BullMQClient.workers.clear();
    BullMQClient.queues.clear();
    BullMQClient.queueEvents.clear();
  }
}

export const UserRole = {
  USER: 'USER',
  ADMIN: 'ADMIN',
  SUPER_ADMIN: 'SUPER_ADMIN'
} as const;

export type UserRole = typeof UserRole

  }
  
  body {

    min-height: 100vh;

  /* Focus styles for accessibility */
  :focus-visible {
    outline: 2px solid theme('colors.primary.500');
    outline-offset: 2px;
  }
  
  /* Reduced motion */
  @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
    * {
      animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
      animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
      transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    }
  }
}

@layer components {
  .btn {
    @apply px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors duration-200 
           focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 
           disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed;
  }
  
  .btn-primary {
    @apply btn bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 
           focus:ring-primary-500;
  }
  
  .btn-secondary {
    @apply btn bg-secondary-200 text-secondary-800 hover:bg-secondary-300 
           focus:ring-secondary-500;
  }
  
  .card {
    @apply bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-secondary-200 
           p-6 transition-shadow hover:shadow-md;
  }
  
  .input {
    @apply w-full px-3 py-2 border border-secondary-300 rounded-lg 
           focus:border-primary-500 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-primary-500 
           placeholder:text-secondary-400 disabled:bg-secondary-100 
           disabled:cursor-not-allowed;
  }
  
  .badge {
    @apply inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium;
  }
  
  .badge-success {
    @apply badge bg-success-50 text-success-700;
  }
  
  .badge-warning {
    @apply badge bg-warning-50 text-warning-700;
  }
  
  .badge-error {
    @apply badge bg-error-50 text-error-700;
  }
}

```typescript
// src/types/index.ts
export interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  role: 'admin' | 'editor' | 'viewer';
  avatar?: string;
  lastActive: string;
}

export interface Project {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  status: 'active' | 'completed' | 'on-hold';
  progress: number;
  dueDate: string;
  members: number;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface Activity {
  id: string;
  user: {
    name: string;
    avatar?: string;
  };
  action: string;
  target: string;
  timestamp: string;
  type: 'create' | 'update' | 'delete' | 'comment';
}

export interface Metric {
  label: string;
  value: number | string;
  change: number;
  icon: string;
  color: 'primary' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
}

export interface DashboardState {
  user: User | null;
  projects: Project[];
  activities: Activity[];
  metrics: Metric[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
}

export interface ApiResponse<T> {
  data: T;
  success: boolean;
  message?: string;
  timestamp: string;
}
```

// src/stores/dashboard.store.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { DashboardState, User, Project, Activity, Metric } from '@/types';

interface DashboardStore extends DashboardState {
  // Actions
  setUser: (user: User) => void;
  setProjects: (projects: Project[]) => void;
  setActivities: (activities: Activity[]) => void;
  setMetrics: (metrics: Metric[]) => void;
  setLoading: (loading: boolean) => void;
  setError: (error: string | null) => void;
  
  // Selectors
  getActiveProjects: () => Project[];
  getRecentActivities: (limit?: number) => Activity[];
  getProjectById: (id: string) => Project | undefined;
  
  // Async actions
  fetchDashboardData: () => Promise<void>;
  updateProjectStatus: (projectId: string, status: Project['status']) => Promise<void>;
}

export const useDashboardStore = create<DashboardStore>((set, get) => ({
  // Initial state
  user: null,
  projects: [],
  activities: [],
  metrics: [],
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  
  // Actions
  setUser: (user) => set({ user }),
  setProjects: (projects) => set({ projects }),
  setActivities: (activities) => set({ activities }),
  setMetrics: (metrics) => set({ metrics }),
  setLoading: (isLoading) => set({ isLoading }),
  setError: (error) => set({ error }),
  
  // Selectors
  getActiveProjects: () => {
    const { projects } = get();
    return projects.filter(project => project.status === 'active');
  },
  
  getRecentActivities: (limit = 5) => {
    const { activities } = get();
    return activities
      .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(a.timestamp).getTime())
      .slice(0, limit);
  },
  
  getProjectById: (id) => {
    const { projects } = get();
    return projects.find(project => project.id === id);
  },
  
  // Async actions
  fetchDashboardData: async () => {
    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    
    try {
      const [user, projects, activities, metrics] = await Promise.all([
        mockApi.getUser(),
        mockApi.getProjects(),
        mockApi.getActivities(),
        mockApi.getMetrics(),
      ]);
      
      set({


### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
# Data Warehouse & ETL Pipeline for Agent Analytics
# Data Engineer Senior Squad

"""
ARQUITETURA:
- Data Warehouse: PostgreSQL (local para desenvolvimento, compatível com BigQuery/Snowflake)
- ETL: Apache Airflow (local com Docker)
- Transformação: dbt (models em SQL)
- Ingestão: Python custom (simulando Airbyte)
- Visualização: Dashboard HTML com Chart.js
- Catálogo: DataHub metadata integrado
"""

# ==================== ESTRUTURA DE PASTAS ====================
"""
diyapp-v12-data-warehouse/
├── docker-compose.yml              # Airflow + PostgreSQL
├── dags/                           # Pipelines Airflow
│   ├── agent_analytics_dag.py
│   └── data_quality_dag.py
├── dbt/                            # Transformações
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── staging/
│   │   │   ├── stg_agent_events.sql
│   │   │   ├── stg_user_sessions.sql
│   │   │   └── stg_llm_calls.sql
│   │   └── marts/
│   │       ├── mart_agent_performance.sql
│   │       ├── mart_user_engagement.sql
│   │       └── mart_llm_cost_metrics.sql
│   ├── tests/
│   └── dbt_project.yml
├── src/                            # Código fonte
│   ├── ingestion/
│   │   ├── agent_event_ingestor.py
│   │   └── llm_log_ingestor.py
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── schema.sql
│   │   └── seed_data.py
│   └── dashboard/
│       └── index.html
├── data/                           # Dados brutos
│   ├── raw/
│   └── processed/
├── config/                         # Configurações
│   ├── airflow.cfg
│   └── dbt_profiles.yml
└── README.md
"""

# ==================== 1. DOCKER-COMPOSE (AIRFLOW + POSTGRESQL) ====================
# docker-compose.yml
docker_compose_content = """
version: '3.8'
x-airflow-common:
  &airflow-common
  image: apache/airflow:2.7.3
  environment:
    &airflow-common-env
    AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
    AIRFLOW__CORE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres/airflow
    AIRFLOW__CORE__FERNET_KEY: ''
    AIRFLOW__CORE__DAGS_ARE_PAUSED_AT_CREATION: 'true'
    AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
    AIRFLOW__API__AUTH_BACKENDS: 'airflow.api.auth.backend.basic_auth'
    _PIP_ADDITIONAL_REQUIREMENTS: psycopg2-binary dbt-postgres
  volumes:
    - ./dags:/opt/airflow/dags
    - ./logs:/opt/airflow/logs
    - ./plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
    - ./data:/opt/airflow/data
    - ./dbt:/opt/airflow/dbt
    - ./src:/opt/airflow/src
  user: "${AIRFLOW_UID:-50000}:${AIRFLOW_GID:-50000}"
  depends_on:
    postgres:
      condition: service_healthy

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: airflow
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: airflow
      POSTGRES_DB: airflow
      POSTGRES_MULTIPLE_DATABASES: airflow,diyapp_dw
    volumes:
      - postgres-db-volume:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/database/schema.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/schema.sql
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "pg_isready", "-U", "airflow"]
      interval: 10s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s

  airflow-webserver:
    <<: *airflow-common
    command: webserver
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "--fail", "http://localhost:8080/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s

  airflow-scheduler:
    <<: *airflow-common
    command: scheduler
    restart: on-failure

  airflow-init:
    <<: *airflow-common
    command: version
    environment:
      <<: *airflow-common-env
      _AIRFLOW_DB_UPGRADE: 'true'
      _AIRFLOW_WWW_USER_CREATE: 'true'
      _AIRFLOW_WWW_USER_USERNAME: admin
      _AIRFLOW_WWW_USER_PASSWORD: admin

volumes:
  postgres-db-volume:
"""

# ==================== 2. SCHEMA DIMENSIONAL DO DATA WAREHOUSE ====================
# src/database/schema.sql
schema_sql = """
-- DIYAPP V12 Data Warehouse Schema
-- Dimensões e Fatos para Analytics de Agentes

-- Database para Data Warehouse
CREATE DATABASE diyapp_dw;
\\c diyapp_dw;

-- ==================== DIMENSÕES ====================

-- Dim_Date: Dimensão de data completa
CREATE TABLE dim_date (
    date_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    date_date DATE NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    year INTEGER NOT NULL,
    quarter INTEGER NOT NULL,
    month INTEGER NOT NULL,
    month_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    week INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_of_month INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_of_week INTEGER NOT NULL,
    day_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    is_weekend BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    is_holiday BOOLEAN DEFAULT false
);

-- Dim_Time: Dimensão de hora (granularidade por hora)
CREATE TABLE dim_time (
    time_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    hour_of_day INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (hour_of_day >= 0 AND hour_of_day <= 23),
    period_of_day VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- morning, afternoon, evening, night
    is_business_hours BOOLEAN NOT NULL
);

-- Dim_Agent: Dimensão do agente/squad
CREATE TABLE dim_agent (
    agent_id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    agent_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    agent_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'data_engineer', 'llm_specialist', 'ai_ops', etc.
    squad_name VARCHAR(100),
    version VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true
);

-- Dim_User: Dimensão do usuário (anonimizado)
CREATE TABLE dim_user (
    user_hash VARCHAR(64) PRIMARY KEY, -- SHA256 do user_id real
    user_tier VARCHAR(20), -- free, pro, enterprise
    signup_date DATE,
    country_code VARCHAR(2),
    timezone VARCHAR(50)
);

-- Dim_Feature: Dimensão de funcionalidade/endpoint
CREATE TABLE dim_feature (
    feature_id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    feature_group VARCHAR(50), -- 'analytics', 'automation', 'monitoring'
    squad_owner VARCHAR(50),
    complexity_level VARCHAR(20) -- simple, medium, complex
);

-- Dim_LLM_Model: Dimensão dos modelos de LLM
CREATE TABLE dim_llm_model (
    model_id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- openai, anthropic, google, etc.
    context_window INTEGER,
    input_cost_per_1k NUMERIC(10,6),
    output_cost_per_1k NUMERIC(10,6),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true
);

-- ==================== FATOS ====================

-- Fact_Agent_Event: Eventos de uso dos agentes
CREATE TABLE fact_agent_event (
    event_id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    date_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_date(date_id),
    time_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_time(time_id),
    agent_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES dim_agent(agent_id),
    user_hash VARCHAR(64) REFERENCES dim_user(user_hash),
    feature_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES dim_feature(feature_id),
    event_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 'execution_start', 'execution_end', 'error', 'timeout'
    execution_time_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_code VARCHAR(50),
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    metadata JSONB
);

-- Fact_LLM_Call: Chamadas aos modelos LLM
CREATE TABLE fact_llm_call (
    call_id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    call_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    date_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_date(date_id),
    time_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_time(time_id),
    agent_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES dim_agent(agent_id),
    model_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES dim_llm_model(model_id),
    feature_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES dim_feature(feature_id),
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cost_usd NUMERIC(12,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_hash VARCHAR(64) -- Para deduplicação
);

-- Fact_User_Session: Sessões de usuário
CREATE TABLE fact_user_session (
    session_id VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_hash VARCHAR(64) REFERENCES dim_user(user_hash),
    start_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
    date_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_date(date_id),
    session_duration_seconds INTEGER,
    agent_interactions_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    features_used_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);

-- ==================== TABELAS DE QUALIDADE ====================

-- Data_Quality_Metrics: Monitoramento de qualidade
CREATE TABLE data_quality_metrics (
    metric_id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    metric_date DATE NOT NULL,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, -- 'completeness', 'freshness', 'uniqueness'
    metric_value NUMERIC(10,4) NOT NULL,
    threshold NUMERIC(10,4),
    passed BOOLEAN,
    checked_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Pipeline_Runs: Log de execução dos pipelines
CREATE TABLE pipeline_runs (
    run_id VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- 'success', 'failed', 'running'
    rows_processed INTEGER,
    error_message TEXT,
    dag_id VARCHAR(100),
    task_id VARCHAR(100)
);

-- ==================== ÍNDICES ====================

CREATE INDEX idx_fact_agent_event_date ON fact_agent_event(date_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_agent_event_agent ON fact_agent_event(agent_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_agent_event_user ON fact_agent_event(user_hash);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_agent_event_timestamp ON fact_agent_event(event_timestamp);

CREATE INDEX idx_fact_llm_call_date ON fact_llm_call(date_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_llm_call_model ON fact_llm_call(model_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_llm_call_agent ON fact_llm_call(agent_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_llm_call_timestamp ON fact_llm_call(call_timestamp);

CREATE INDEX idx_fact_user_session_date ON fact_user_session(date_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_user_session_user ON fact_user_session(user_hash);

-- ==================== VIEWS PARA CONSUMO ====================

CREATE VIEW mart_agent_performance AS
SELECT 
    d.date_date,
    a.agent_name,
    a.agent_type,
    f.feature_name,
    COUNT(DISTINCT e.user_hash) as unique_users,
    COUNT(*) as total_executions,
    AVG(e.execution_time_ms) as avg_execution_time,
    SUM(CASE WHEN e.success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*) as success_rate,
    SUM(e.input_tokens + COALESCE(e.output_tokens, 0)) as total_tokens
FROM fact_agent_event e
JOIN dim_date d ON e.date_id = d.date_id
JOIN dim_agent a ON e.agent_id = a.agent_id
JOIN dim_feature f ON e.feature_id = f.feature_id
GROUP BY d.date_date, a.agent_name, a.agent_type, f.feature_name;

CREATE VIEW mart_llm_cost_metrics AS
SELECT 
    d.date_date,
    m.model_name,
    m.provider,
    a.agent_name,
    f.feature_name,
    COUNT(*) as total_calls,
    SUM(c.prompt_tokens) as total_prompt_tokens,
    SUM(c.completion_tokens) as total_completion_tokens,
    SUM(c.total_tokens) as total_tokens,
    SUM(c.cost_usd) as total_cost_usd,
    AVG(c.latency_ms) as avg_latency_ms,
    SUM(CASE WHEN c.success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*) as success_rate
FROM fact_llm_call c
JOIN dim_date d ON c.date_id = d.date_id
JOIN dim_llm_model m ON c.model_id = m.model_id
JOIN dim_agent a ON c.agent_id = a.agent_id
JOIN dim_feature f ON c.feature_id = f.feature_id
GROUP BY d.date_date, m.model_name, m.provider, a.agent_name, f.feature_name;

CREATE VIEW mart_user_engagement AS
SELECT 
    d.date_date,
    u.user_tier,
    u.country_code,
    COUNT(DISTINCT s.session_id) as total_sessions,
    AVG(s.session_duration_seconds) as avg_session_duration,
    SUM(s.agent_interactions_count) as total_interactions,
    SUM(s.total_tokens_used) as total_tokens_used
FROM fact_user_session s
JOIN dim_date d ON s.date_id = d.date_id
JOIN dim_user u ON s.user_hash = u.user_hash
GROUP BY d.date_date, u.user_tier, u.country_code;
"""

# ==================== 3. PIPELINE AIRFLOW (DAG) ====================
# dags/agent_analytics_dag.py
airflow_dag = """
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from airflow import DAG
from airflow.operators.python import PythonOperator
from airflow.operators.bash import BashOperator
from airflow.operators.email import EmailOperator
from airflow.providers.postgres.operators.postgres import PostgresOperator
import sys
import os

sys.path.append('/opt/airflow/src')

from ingestion.agent_event_ingestor import AgentEventIngestor
from ingestion.llm_log_ingestor import LLMLogIngestor
from database.seed_data import generate_test_data

default_args = {
    'owner': 'data_engineer',
    'depends_on_past': False,
    'email': ['alerts@diyapp.com'],
    'email_on_failure': True,
    'email_on_retry': False,
    'retries': 3,
    'retry_delay': timedelta(minutes=5),
    'sla': timedelta(hours=1)  # SLA de 1h para dados de custo LLM
}

dag = DAG(
    'agent_analytics_pipeline',
    default_args=default_args,
    description='ETL Pipeline para Analytics de Agentes DIYAPP V12',
    schedule_interval='0 * * * *',  # A cada hora
    start_date=datetime(2024, 1, 1),
    catchup=False,
    tags=['diyapp', 'analytics', 'agents'],
    max_active_runs=1
)

# ==================== TAREFAS ====================

# 1. Ingestão de dados brutos
def ingest_agent_events(**context):
    '''Ingere eventos de agentes do sistema de logs'''
    ingestor = AgentEventIngestor()
    stats = ingestor.ingest_last_hour()
    context['ti'].xcom_push(key='agent_events_stats', value=stats)
    return stats

task_ingest_agent_events = PythonOperator(
    task_id='ingest_agent_events',
    python_callable=ingest_agent_events,
    dag=dag
)

def ingest_llm_logs(**context):
    '''Ingere logs de chamadas LLM do gateway'''
    ingestor = LLMLogIngestor()
    stats = ingestor.ingest_last_hour()
    context['ti'].xcom_push(key='llm_logs_stats', value=stats)
    return stats

task_ingest_llm_logs = PythonOperator(
    task_id='ingest_llm_logs',
    python_callable=ingest_llm_logs,
    dag=dag
)

# 2. Transformação com dbt
task_dbt_run = BashOperator(
    task_id='dbt_run',
    bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt && dbt run --profiles-dir .',
    dag=dag
)

task_dbt_test = BashOperator(
    task_id='dbt_test',
    bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt && dbt test --profiles-dir .',
    dag=dag
)

# 3. Qualidade de dados
def run_data_quality_checks(**context):
    '''Executa checks de qualidade nos dados transformados'''


### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-core/
├── terraform/
│   ├── modules/
│   │   ├── vpc/

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura Principal

### `terraform/modules/vpc/main.tf`
```hcl
# VPC Module
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (staging/production)"
  type        = string
}

variable "region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-vpc"
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count             = 3
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = cidrsubnet(var.vpc_cidr, 8, count.index)
  availability_zone = "${var.region}${element(["a", "b", "c"], count.index)}"
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-public-${count.index + 1}"
    Environment = var.environment
    Type        = "public"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = 3
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = cidrsubnet(var.vpc_cidr, 8, count.index + 10)
  availability_zone = "${var.region}${element(["a", "b", "c"], count.index)}"
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-private-${count.index + 1}"
    Environment = var.environment
    Type        = "private"
  }
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-igw"
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = 3
  domain = "vpc"
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-nat-eip-${count.index + 1}"
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = 3
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[count.index].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-nat-${count.index + 1}"
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-public-rt"
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = 3
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = 3
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
    nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[count.index].id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-private-rt-${count.index + 1}"
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = 3
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[count.index].id
}

output "vpc_id" {
  value = aws_vpc.main.id
}

output "public_subnet_ids" {
  value = aws_subnet.public[*].id
}

output "private_subnet_ids" {
  value = aws_subnet.private[*].id
}
```

### `terraform/modules/ecs/main.tf`
```hcl
# ECS Cluster Module
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "ECS cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-cluster"
}

variable "vpc_id" {
  description = "VPC ID"
  type        = string
}

variable "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "Private subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "public_subnet_ids" {
  description = "Public subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

# ECS Cluster
resource "aws_ecs_cluster" "main" {
  name = "${var.cluster_name}-${var.environment}"
  
  setting {
    name  = "containerInsights"
    value = "enabled"
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# ECS Capacity Provider - Fargate
resource "aws_ecs_cluster_capacity_providers" "main" {
  cluster_name = aws_ecs_cluster.main.name
  
  capacity_providers = ["FARGATE", "FARGATE_SPOT"]
  
  default_capacity_provider_strategy {
    capacity_provider = "FARGATE"
    weight            = 1
    base              = 1
  }
}

# Security Group for ECS Tasks
resource "aws_security_group" "ecs_tasks" {
  name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-ecs-tasks-sg"
  description = "Security group for ECS tasks"
  vpc_id      = var.vpc_id
  
  ingress {
    protocol        = "tcp"
    from_port       = 3000
    to_port         = 3000
    cidr_blocks     = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
    description     = "HTTP access"
  }
  
  ingress {
    protocol        = "tcp"
    from_port       = 5432
    to_port         = 5432
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.rds.id]
    description     = "PostgreSQL access"
  }
  
  egress {
    protocol    = "-1"
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# Application Load Balancer
resource "aws_lb" "main" {
  name               = "diyapp-${var.environment}-alb"
  internal           = false
  load_balancer_type = "application"
  security_groups    = [aws_security_group.alb.id]
  subnets           = var.public_subnet_ids
  
  enable_deletion_protection = var.environment == "production"
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

resource "aws_security_group" "alb" {
  name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-alb-sg"
  description = "Security group for ALB"
  vpc_id      = var.vpc_id
  
  ingress {
    protocol    = "tcp"
    from_port   = 80
    to_port     = 80
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  ingress {
    protocol    = "tcp"
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  egress {
    protocol    = "-1"
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# Target Group
resource "aws_lb_target_group" "main" {
  name        = "diyapp-${var.environment}-tg"
  port        = 3000
  protocol    = "HTTP"
  vpc_id      = var.vpc_id
  target_type = "ip"
  
  health_check {
    enabled             = true
    interval            = 30
    path                = "/health"
    port                = "traffic-port"
    protocol            = "HTTP"
    timeout             = 5
    healthy_threshold   = 3
    unhealthy_threshold = 3
    matcher             = "200"
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# Listener
resource "aws_lb_listener" "http" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "80"
  protocol          = "HTTP"
  
  default_action {
    type = "redirect"
    
    redirect {
      port        = "443"
      protocol    = "HTTPS"
      status_code = "HTTP_301"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_lb_listener" "https" {
  load_balancer_arn = aws_lb.main.arn
  port              = "443"
  protocol          = "HTTPS"
  ssl_policy        = "ELBSecurityPolicy-2016-08"
  certificate_arn   = aws_acm_certificate.main.arn
  
  default_action {
    type             = "forward"
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
  }
}

# ACM Certificate
resource "aws_acm_certificate" "main" {
  domain_name       = var.environment == "production" ? "diyapp.com" : "staging.diyapp.com"
  validation_method = "DNS"
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
  
  lifecycle {
    create_before_destroy = true
  }
}

# ECS Task Definition
resource "aws_ecs_task_definition" "main" {
  family                   = "diyapp-${var.environment}-task"
  network_mode             = "awsvpc"
  requires_compatibilities = ["FARGATE"]
  cpu                      = var.environment == "production" ? "1024" : "512"
  memory                   = var.environment == "production" ? "2048" : "1024"
  execution_role_arn       = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_execution_role.arn
  task_role_arn           = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_role.arn
  
  container_definitions = jsonencode([{
    name      = "diyapp"
    image     = "${aws_ecr_repository.main.repository_url}:latest"
    cpu       = var.environment == "production" ? 1024 : 512
    memory    = var.environment == "production" ? 2048 : 1024
    essential = true
    
    portMappings = [{
      containerPort = 3000
      hostPort      = 3000
      protocol      = "tcp"
    }]
    
    environment = [
      {
        name  = "NODE_ENV"
        value = var.environment
      },
      {
        name  = "DATABASE_URL"
        value = "postgresql://${aws_db_instance.main.username}:${aws_db_instance.main.password}@${aws_db_instance.main.endpoint}/${aws_db_instance.main.db_name}"
      }
    ]
    
    logConfiguration = {
      logDriver = "awslogs"
      options = {
        "awslogs-group"         = "/ecs/diyapp-${var.environment}"
        "awslogs-region"        = var.region
        "awslogs-stream-prefix" = "ecs"
      }
    }
    
    healthCheck = {
      command     = ["CMD-SHELL", "curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1"]
      interval    = 30
      timeout     = 5
      retries     = 3
      startPeriod = 60
    }
  }])
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# ECS Service with Auto Scaling
resource "aws_ecs_service" "main" {
  name            = "diyapp-${var.environment}-service"
  cluster         = aws_ecs_cluster.main.id
  task_definition = aws_ecs_task_definition.main.arn
  desired_count   = var.environment == "production" ? 3 : 2
  launch_type     = "FARGATE"
  
  network_configuration {
    security_groups = [aws_security_group.ecs_tasks.id]
    subnets         = var.private_subnet_ids
    assign_public_ip = false
  }
  
  load_balancer {
    target_group_arn = aws_lb_target_group.main.arn
    container_name   = "diyapp"
    container_port   = 3000
  }
  
  depends_on = [aws_lb_listener.https]
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    ManagedBy   = "terraform"
  }
}

# Auto Scaling Policy
resource "aws_appautoscaling_target" "ecs_target" {
  max_capacity       = var.environment == "production" ? 10 : 5
  min_capacity       = var.environment == "production" ? 3 : 2
  resource_id        = "service/${aws_ecs_cluster.main.name}/${aws_ecs_service.main.name}"
  scalable_dimension = "ecs:service:DesiredCount"
  service_namespace  = "ecs"
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "cpu_scaling" {
  name               = "diyapp-${var.environment}-cpu-scaling"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace
  
  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageCPUUtilization"
    }
    
    target_value       = 70
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}

resource "aws_appautoscaling_policy" "memory_scaling" {
  name               = "diyapp-${var.environment}-memory-scaling"
  policy_type        = "TargetTrackingScaling"
  resource_id        = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.resource_id
  scalable_dimension = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.scalable_dimension
  service_namespace  = aws_appautoscaling_target.ecs_target.service_namespace
  
  target_tracking_scaling_policy_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ECSServiceAverageMemoryUtilization"
    }
    
    target_value       = 80
    scale_in_cooldown  = 300
    scale_out_cooldown = 60
  }
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Segurança

Vou implementar um sistema de segurança completo para o DIYAPP V12, incluindo threat modeling, WAF, revisão de segurança e gestão de secrets.

## 1. Estrutura do Projeto
