## 2. Módulo de Retenção e Exclusão de Dados (src/compliance/data_retention.py)

```python
"""
Módulo de Gerenciamento de Retenção e Exclusão de Dados - LGPD/GDPR Compliant
"""
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from enum import Enum
import json
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import hashlib

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RetentionPolicy(Enum):
    """Políticas de retenção conforme finalidade"""
    ACCOUNT_ACTIVITY = "account_activity"
    LEGAL_REQUIREMENT = "legal_requirement"
    MARKETING = "marketing"
    ANALYTICS = "analytics"
    AI_TRAINING = "ai_training"

@dataclass
class DataSubject:
    """Titular de dados conforme LGPD"""
    user_id: str
    email: str
    data_categories: List[str]
    consent_given: Dict[str, datetime]
    retention_policies: Dict[str, datetime]
    deletion_requested: Optional[datetime] = None

class DataRetentionManager:
    """Gerenciador central de retenção e exclusão de dados"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_connection):
        self.db = db_connection
        self.retention_config = self._load_retention_policies()
        
    def _load_retention_policies(self) -> Dict:
        """Carrega políticas de retenção do arquivo de configuração"""
        import yaml
        with open('config/retention_policies.yaml', 'r') as f:
            return yaml.safe_load(f)
    
    async def schedule_deletion(self, user_id: str, data_category: str) -> bool:
        """
        Agenda exclusão automática de dados conforme política de retenção
        """
        try:
            retention_period = self.retention_config['periods'].get(data_category)
            if not retention_period:
                logger.warning(f"Política não definida para categoria: {data_category}")
                return False
            
            # Calcula data de expiração
            expiry_date = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=retention_period['days'])
            
            # Agenda tarefa de exclusão
            await self.db.execute(
                """
                INSERT INTO data_retention_schedule 
                (user_id, data_category, expiry_date, status)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'scheduled')
                """,
                (user_id, data_category, expiry_date)
            )
            
            logger.info(f"Exclusão agendada para {user_id}/{data_category} em {expiry_date}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao agendar exclusão: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def execute_scheduled_deletions(self):
        """
        Executa exclusões agendadas (rodar como cron job diário)
        """
        try:
            # Busca registros com expiração vencida
            expired_records = await self.db.fetch_all(
                """
                SELECT id, user_id, data_category 
                FROM data_retention_schedule 
                WHERE expiry_date <= ? AND status = 'scheduled'
                """,
                (datetime.now(),)
            )
            
            for record in expired_records:
                await self._delete_user_data(
                    record['user_id'], 
                    record['data_category']
                )
                
                # Marca como processado
                await self.db.execute(
                    "UPDATE data_retention_schedule SET status = 'deleted' WHERE id = ?",
                    (record['id'],)
                )
                
            logger.info(f"Processadas {len(expired_records)} exclusões agendadas")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao executar exclusões agendadas: {e}")
    
    async def _delete_user_data(self, user_id: str, data_category: str) -> bool:
        """
        Exclui dados do usuário de forma segura e auditável
        """
        try:
            # 1. Pseudonimização/anonymização (quando aplicável)
            if data_category in ['analytics', 'ai_training']:
                await self._anonymize_data(user_id, data_category)
            else:
                # 2. Exclusão física
                await self._physical_deletion(user_id, data_category)
            
            # 3. Log da exclusão
            await self._log_deletion_activity(user_id, data_category)
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro na exclusão de dados: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def _anonymize_data(self, user_id: str, data_category: str):
        """Pseudonimiza dados mantendo valor analítico"""
        # Gera hash irreversível para identificador
        anonymized_id = hashlib.sha256(f"{user_id}{datetime.now().timestamp()}".encode()).hexdigest()[:32]
        
        await self.db.execute(
            f"""
            UPDATE {data_category}_data 
            SET user_id = ?, personal_identifiers = NULL 
            WHERE user_id = ?
            """,
            (anonymized_id, user_id)
        )
    
    async def _physical_deletion(self, user_id: str, data_category: str):
        """Exclusão física de dados"""
        await self.db.execute(
            f"DELETE FROM {data_category}_data WHERE user_id = ?",
            (user_id,)
        )
    
    async def _log_deletion_activity(self, user_id: str, data_category: str):
        """Registra atividade de exclusão para auditoria"""
        await self.db.execute(
            """
            INSERT INTO compliance_audit_log 
            (user_id, action, data_category, timestamp, metadata)
            VALUES (?, 'data_deletion', ?, ?, ?)
            """,
            (user_id, data_category, datetime.now(), 
             json.dumps({'method': 'scheduled_retention'}))
        )

class DataDeletionRequestHandler:
    """Processa solicitações de exclusão de titulares (LGPD Art. 18)"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_connection):
        self.db = db_connection
        self.sla_days = 15
    
    async def process_deletion_request(self, user_id: str, request_type: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Processa solicitação de exclusão do titular
        Tipos: 'full_deletion', 'partial_deletion', 'anonymization'
        """
        try:
            # Valida identidade do titular
            if not await self._verify_data_subject_identity(user_id):
                return {"success": False, "error": "Identity verification failed"}
            
            # Registra solicitação
            request_id = await self._register_request(user_id, request_type)
            
            # Executa exclusão conforme tipo
            if request_type == 'full_deletion':
                await self._execute_full_deletion(user_id)
            elif request_type == 'partial_deletion':
                await self._execute_partial_deletion(user_id)
            elif request_type == 'anonymization':
                await self._execute_anonymization(user_id)
            
            # Atualiza status
            await self._update_request_status(request_id, 'completed')
            
            # Gera comprovante
            receipt = await self._generate_deletion_receipt(request_id)
            
            return {
                "success": True,
                "request_id": request_id,
                "receipt": receipt,
                "completion_date": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                "sla_met": True
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro no processamento de exclusão: {e}")
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}
    
    async def _verify_data_subject_identity(self, user_id: str) -> bool:
        """Verifica identidade do titular (2-factor verification)"""
        # Implementação de verificação de identidade
        return True
    
    async def _register_request(self, user_id: str, request_type: str) -> str:
        """Registra solicitação no sistema"""
        request_id = f"DSR-{hashlib.md5(f'{user_id}{datetime.now()}'.encode()).hexdigest()[:8]}"
        
        await self.db.execute(
            """
            INSERT INTO data_subject_requests 
            (request_id, user_id, request_type, status, requested_at, sla_deadline)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'pending', ?, ?)
            """,
            (request_id, user_id, request_type, datetime.now(),
             datetime.now() + timedelta(days=self.sla_days))
        )
        
        return request_id
    
    async def _execute_full_deletion(self, user_id: str):
        """Exclusão completa de todos os dados pessoais"""
        tables_to_clean = [
            'users', 'user_profiles', 'user_activity',
            'user_preferences', 'user_sessions'
        ]
        
        for table in tables_to_clean:
            try:
                await self.db.execute(
                    f"DELETE FROM {table} WHERE user_id = ?",
                    (user_id,)
                )
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"Erro ao limpar tabela {table}: {e}")
    
    async def _generate_deletion_receipt(self, request_id: str) -> Dict:
        """Gera comprovante de exclusão para o titular"""
        record = await self.db.fetch_one(
            "SELECT * FROM data_subject_requests WHERE request_id = ?",
            (request_id,)
        )
        
        return {
            "receipt_id": f"REC-{request_id}",
            "request_type": record['request_type'],
            "requested_at": record['requested_at'].isoformat(),
            "completed_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "data_categories_deleted": await self._get_deleted_categories(request_id),
            "legal_basis": "LGPD Artigo 18, GDPR Article 17",
            "dpo_contact": "dpo@diyapp.com"
        }
```

## 3. Módulo de Consentimento (src/compliance/consent_manager.py)

```python
"""
Gerenciador de Consentimento LGPD/GDPR - Base Legal: Consentimento
"""
import json
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from enum import Enum
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class ConsentType(Enum):
    """Tipos de consentimento conforme finalidade"""
    MARKETING = "marketing_communications"
    ANALYTICS = "analytics_tracking"
    THIRD_PARTY = "third_party_sharing"
    AI_PROCESSING = "ai_data_processing"
    COOKIES = "cookies_storage"

class ConsentManager:
    """Gerencia consentimentos de forma granular e auditável"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_connection):
        self.db = db_connection
    
    async def record_consent(self, user_id: str, consent_data: Dict) -> bool:
        """
        Registra consentimento granular conforme LGPD
        """
        try:
            # Valida dados mínimos
            required_fields = ['consent_type', 'purpose', 'version', 'ip_address']
            if not all(field in consent_data for field in required_fields):
                raise ValueError("Missing required consent fields")
            
            # Gera ID único do consentimento
            consent_id = self._generate_consent_id(user_id, consent_data['consent_type'])
            
            # Registra consentimento
            await self.db.execute(
                """
                INSERT INTO user_consents 
                (consent_id, user_id, consent_type, purpose, granted, 
                 granted_at, version, ip_address, user_agent, metadata)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                """,
                (consent_id, user_id, consent_data['consent_type'],
                 consent_data['purpose'], True, datetime.now(),
                 consent_data['version'], consent_data.get('ip_address'),
                 consent_data.get('user_agent'), 
                 json.dumps(consent_data.get('metadata', {})))
            )
            
            # Atualiza preferências do usuário
            await self._update_user_preferences(user_id, consent_data['consent_type'], True)
            
            logger.info(f"Consentimento registrado: {consent_id}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao registrar consentimento: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def withdraw_consent(self, user_id: str, consent_type: str) -> bool:
        """
        Revoga consentimento (LGPD Art. 8º)
        """
        try:
            # Registra revogação
            await self.db.execute(
                """
                UPDATE user_consents 
                SET revoked = TRUE, revoked_at = ?, revocation_reason = 'user_request'
                WHERE user_id = ? AND consent_type = ? AND granted = TRUE AND revoked = FALSE
                """,
                (datetime.now(), user_id, consent_type)
            )
            
            # Atualiza preferências
            await self._update_user_preferences(user_id, consent_type, False)
            
            # Para processamentos em andamento
            await self._stop_data_processing(user_id, consent_type)
            
            logger.info(f"Consentimento revogado: {user_id}/{consent_type}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao revogar consentimento: {e}")
            return False
    
    async def get_valid_consent(self, user_id: str, consent_type: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """
        Verifica se há consentimento válido para determinada finalidade
        """
        consent = await self.db.fetch_one(
            """
            SELECT * FROM user_consents 
            WHERE user_id = ? AND consent_type = ? 
            AND granted = TRUE AND revoked = FALSE
            ORDER BY granted_at DESC LIMIT 1
            """,
            (user_id, consent_type)
        )
        
        return dict(consent) if consent else None
    
    def _generate_consent_id(self, user_id: str, consent_type: str) -> str:
        """Gera ID único para rastreabilidade"""
        import hashlib
        base_string = f"{user_id}_{consent_type}_{datetime.now().timestamp()}"
        return f"CONS-{hashlib.sha256(base_string.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]}"
    
    async def _update_user_preferences(self, user_id: str, consent_type: str, granted: bool):
        """Atualiza preferências do usuário"""
        await self.db.execute(
            """
            INSERT INTO user_preferences (user_id, preference_key, preference_value, updated_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(user_id, preference_key) 
            DO UPDATE SET preference_value = ?, updated_at = ?
            """,
            (user_id, f"consent

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Writer]

└── README.md
```

## 1. Documentação OpenAPI (Swagger) - `api-documentation/openapi/openapi.yaml`

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core API
  description: |
    API RESTful para o sistema DIYAPP Evolution V12.
    Sistema de gerenciamento de projetos autônomo com IA integrada.
    
    **Versão:** 12.0.0
    **Data de Publicação:** 2024-01-15
    **Status:** Production
    
    ### Autenticação
    Esta API utiliza JWT (JSON Web Tokens) para autenticação.
    Inclua o token no header: `Authorization: Bearer <seu_token>`
    
    ### Rate Limiting
    - Usuários padrão: 100 requisições/hora
    - Administradores: 1000 requisições/hora
    - Agentes IA: 5000 requisições/hora
    
    ### Base URL
    - Produção: `https://api.diyapp.com/v12`
    - Sandbox: `https://sandbox-api.diyapp.com/v12`
    - Local: `http://localhost:3000/v12`
    
  version: "12.0.0"
  contact:
    name: Suporte DIYAPP
    email: suporte@diyapp.com
    url: https://docs.diyapp.com
  license:
    name: Proprietary
    url: https://diyapp.com/terms

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.com/v12
    description: Produção
  - url: https://sandbox-api.diyapp.com/v12
    description: Ambiente de testes
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v12
    description: Desenvolvimento local

tags:
  - name: Autenticação
    description: Endpoints para login, logout e gerenciamento de tokens
  - name: Usuários
    description: Gerenciamento de usuários e perfis
  - name: Projetos
    description: Operações CRUD para projetos
  - name: Tarefas
    description: Gerenciamento de tarefas dentro dos projetos
  - name: Agentes IA
    description: Controle e monitoramento de agentes de IA autônomos
  - name: Monitoramento
    description: Métricas e health checks do sistema
  - name: Administração
    description: Endpoints administrativos (requer permissões de admin)

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags:
        - Autenticação
      summary: Autenticar usuário
      description: |
        Realiza login no sistema e retorna token JWT.
        
        **Notas:**
        - Tokens expiram em 24 horas
        - Use o refresh token para obter novo token sem precisar fazer login novamente
        - Logs de tentativas falhas são monitorados por segurança
      operationId: loginUser
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
            examples:
              adminLogin:
                summary: Login de administrador
                value:
                  email: "admin@diyapp.com"
                  password: "SenhaSegura123!"
                  remember_me: true
              userLogin:
                summary: Login de usuário regular
                value:
                  email: "usuario@exemplo.com"
                  password: "MinhaSenha456"
                  remember_me: false
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginResponse'
              examples:
                successResponse:
                  summary: Resposta de sucesso
                  value:
                    success: true
                    token: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
                    refresh_token: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
                    user:
                      id: "usr_123456789"
                      email: "usuario@exemplo.com"
                      name: "João Silva"
                      role: "user"
                      permissions: ["project:read", "project:write"]
                    expires_at: "2024-01-16T10:30:00Z"
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
              examples:
                invalidCredentials:
                  summary: Credenciais inválidas
                  value:
                    error: "INVALID_CREDENTIALS"
                    message: "Email ou senha incorretos"
                    code: 401
                    details:
                      remaining_attempts: 4
                      lockout_time: null
        '429':
          description: Muitas tentativas de login
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
              examples:
                tooManyAttempts:
                  summary: Muitas tentativas
                  value:
                    error: "TOO_MANY_ATTEMPTS"
                    message: "Muitas tentativas de login. Tente novamente em 15 minutos"
                    code: 429
                    retry_after: 900

  /auth/logout:
    post:
      tags:
        - Autenticação
      summary: Encerrar sessão
      description: |
        Invalida o token JWT atual.
        
        **Importante:** Após logout, o token não pode mais ser usado.
        Para acesso futuro, será necessário fazer login novamente.
      operationId: logoutUser
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Logout bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  success:
                    type: boolean
                    example: true
                  message:
                    type: string
                    example: "Sessão encerrada com sucesso"
        '401':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/UnauthorizedError'

  /auth/refresh:
    post:
      tags:
        - Autenticação
      summary: Renovar token
      description: |
        Obtém um novo token JWT usando o refresh token.
        
        **Fluxo recomendado:**
        1. Token expira (recebe erro 401)
        2. Chama este endpoint com refresh token
        3. Recebe novo token e continua operações
      operationId: refreshToken
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required:
                - refresh_token
              properties:
                refresh_token:
                  type: string
                  description: Refresh token válido
                  example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token renovado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/RefreshResponse'
        '401':
          description: Refresh token inválido ou expirado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

  /users:
    get:
      tags:
        - Usuários
      summary: Listar usuários
      description: |
        Retorna lista paginada de usuários.
        
        **Permissões necessárias:** `users:read`
        **Filtros disponíveis:**
        - role: Filtrar por papel (user, admin, agent)
        - status: Filtrar por status (active, inactive, suspended)
        - search: Busca textual em nome e email
      operationId: listUsers
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/PageParam'
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/LimitParam'
        - in: query
          name: role
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [user, admin, agent]
          description: Filtrar por papel do usuário
        - in: query
          name: status
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, inactive, suspended]
          description: Filtrar por status do usuário
        - in: query
          name: search
          schema:
            type: string
          description: Termo de busca (nome ou email)
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de usuários retornada com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/UserListResponse'
        '403':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ForbiddenError'

    post:
      tags:
        - Usuários
      summary: Criar novo usuário
      description: |
        Cria um novo usuário no sistema.
        
        **Permissões necessárias:** `users:write`
        **Validações:**
        - Email deve ser único
        - Senha deve ter pelo menos 8 caracteres
        - Senha deve conter letras e números
      operationId: createUser
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/CreateUserRequest'
            examples:
              regularUser:
                summary: Usuário regular
                value:
                  name: "Maria Santos"
                  email: "maria@exemplo.com"
                  password: "Senha1234"
                  role: "user"
              adminUser:
                summary: Administrador
                value:
                  name: "Admin Sistema"
                  email: "admin2@diyapp.com"
                  password: "Admin@1234"
                  role: "admin"
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Usuário criado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
          headers:
            Location:
              description: URL do usuário criado
              schema:
                type: string
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
        '409':
          description: Email já cadastrado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

  /users/{id}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Usuários
      summary: Obter usuário por ID
      description: |
        Retorna detalhes de um usuário específico.
        
        **Permissões necessárias:**
        - `users:read` OU
        - Acesso ao próprio perfil (mesmo ID do token)
      operationId: getUser
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/UserIdParam'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Usuário encontrado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
        '404':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/NotFoundError'

    put:
      tags:
        - Usuários
      summary: Atualizar usuário
      description: |
        Atualiza informações de um usuário.
        
        **Permissões necessárias:**
        - `users:write` OU
        - Acesso ao próprio perfil (mesmo ID do token)
        
        **Nota:** Para alterar senha, use endpoint específico `/users/{id}/password`
      operationId: updateUser
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/UserIdParam'
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpdateUserRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Usuário atualizado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
        '403':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ForbiddenError'
        '404':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/NotFoundError'

    delete:
      tags:
        - Usuários
      summary: Excluir usuário
      description: |
        Remove um usuário do sistema (soft delete).
        
        **Permissões necessárias:** `users:write`
        **Nota:** Usuários são marcados como inativos, não removidos permanentemente.
      operationId: deleteUser
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/UserIdParam'
      responses:
        '204':
          description: Usuário excluído com sucesso
        '403':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/ForbiddenError'
        '404':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/NotFoundError'

  /projects:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projetos
      summary: Listar projetos
      description: |
        Retorna lista paginada de projetos.
        
        **Filtros disponíveis:**
        - status: Filtrar por status (planning, active, completed, archived)
        - owner: Filtrar por ID do proprietário
        - team: Filtrar por ID de membro da equipe
        - search: Busca textual em nome e descrição
      operationId: listProjects
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/PageParam'
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/LimitParam'
        - in: query
          name: status
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [planning, active, completed, archived]
          description: Status do projeto
        - in: query
          name: owner
          schema:
            type: string
          description: ID do proprietário do projeto
        - in: query
          name: team
          schema:
            type: string
          description: ID de membro da equipe
        - in: query
          name: search
          schema:
            type: string
          description: Termo de busca
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de projetos
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectListResponse'

    post:
      tags:
        - Projetos
      summary: Criar novo projeto
      description: |
        Cria um novo projeto no sistema.
        
        **Validações:**
        - Nome deve ser único por usuário
        - Data de início não pode ser no passado
        - Data de término deve ser após data de início
      operationId: createProject
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/CreateProjectRequest'
            examples:
              softwareProject:
                summary: Projeto de software
                value:
                  name: "DIYAPP Mobile App"
                  description: "Desenvolvimento do aplicativo móvel DIYAPP"
                  start_date: "2024-02-01"
                  end_date: "2024-06-30"
                  status: "planning"
                  tags: ["mobile", "react-native", "ia"]
                  settings:
                    auto_assign_tasks: true
                    daily_standup_enabled: true
                    ai_assistant_enabled: true
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Projeto criado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
          headers:
            Location:
              description: URL do projeto criado
              schema:
                type: string

  /projects/{id}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projetos
      summary: Obter projeto por ID
      description: |
        Retorna detalhes completos de um projeto.
        Inclui tarefas, membros e métricas.
      operationId: getProject
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/ProjectIdParam'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Projeto encontrado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectDetail'
        '404':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/NotFoundError'

  /agents:
    get:
      tags:
        - Agentes IA
      summary: Listar agentes IA
      description: |
        Retorna lista de agentes de IA disponíveis.
        
        **Permissões necessárias:** `agents:read`
      operationId: listAgents
     

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infra as Code & Monitoring Setup

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   ├── providers.tf
│   ├── modules/
│   │   ├── vpc/
│   │   ├── ecs/
│   │   ├── rds/
│   │   └── monitoring/
│   └── environments/
│       ├── dev/
│       └── prod/
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   │   └── prometheus.yml
│   ├── grafana/
│   │   ├── dashboards/
│   │   │   ├── diyapp-overview.json
│   │   │   ├── api-metrics.json
│   │   │   └── llm-metrics.json
│   │   └── datasources/
│   │       └── prometheus.yml
│   └── alertmanager/
│       └── alertmanager.yml
├── docker-compose.yml
├── scripts/
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   ├── monitoring-setup.sh
│   └── health-check.sh
└── README.md
```

## 1. Terraform Configuration (AWS)

### terraform/providers.tf
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    
    random = {
      source  = "hashicorp/random"
      version = "~> 3.5"
    }
    
    local = {
      source  = "hashicorp/local"
      version = "~> 2.4"
    }
  }
  
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v12/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V12"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-Senior-Squad"
    }
  }
}
```

### terraform/variables.tf
```hcl
variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (dev/staging/prod)"
  type        = string
  validation {
    condition     = contains(["dev", "staging", "prod"], var.environment)
    error_message = "Environment must be dev, staging, or prod."
  }
}

variable "project_name" {
  description = "Project name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-v12"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
}

variable "instance_type" {
  description = "EC2 instance type for ECS"
  type        = string
  default     = "t3.medium"
}

variable "min_size" {
  description = "Minimum number of instances in ASG"
  type        = number
  default     = 2
}

variable "max_size" {
  description = "Maximum number of instances in ASG"
  type        = number
  default     = 6
}

variable "desired_size" {
  description = "Desired number of instances in ASG"
  type        = number
  default     = 3
}

variable "db_instance_class" {
  description = "RDS instance class"
  type        = string
  default     = "db.t3.medium"
}

variable "db_allocated_storage" {
  description = "RDS allocated storage in GB"
  type        = number
  default     = 20
}

variable "db_name" {
  description = "Database name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp"
}

variable "db_username" {
  description = "Database username"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_admin"
}

variable "slo_availability" {
  description = "SLO for availability (e.g., 0.999 for 99.9%)"
  type        = number
  default     = 0.999
}

variable "slo_latency_p95" {
  description = "SLO for P95 latency in milliseconds"
  type        = number
  default     = 300
}

variable "slo_error_rate" {
  description = "SLO for error rate (e.g., 0.001 for 0.1%)"
  type        = number
  default     = 0.001
}

variable "slo_llm_latency" {
  description = "SLO for LLM P95 latency in seconds"
  type        = number
  default     = 8
}
```

### terraform/main.tf
```hcl
# VPC Module
module "vpc" {
  source = "./modules/vpc"
  
  project_name     = var.project_name
  environment      = var.environment
  vpc_cidr         = var.vpc_cidr
  availability_zones = var.availability_zones
}

# ECS Cluster Module
module "ecs" {
  source = "./modules/ecs"
  
  project_name     = var.project_name
  environment      = var.environment
  vpc_id           = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnets  = module.vpc.private_subnets
  public_subnets   = module.vpc.public_subnets
  
  instance_type    = var.instance_type
  min_size         = var.min_size
  max_size         = var.max_size
  desired_size     = var.desired_size
}

# RDS Module
module "rds" {
  source = "./modules/rds"
  
  project_name          = var.project_name
  environment           = var.environment
  vpc_id                = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnets       = module.vpc.private_subnets
  db_instance_class     = var.db_instance_class
  db_allocated_storage  = var.db_allocated_storage
  db_name               = var.db_name
  db_username           = var.db_username
  security_group_ids    = [module.ecs.ecs_security_group_id]
}

# Monitoring Module
module "monitoring" {
  source = "./modules/monitoring"
  
  project_name     = var.project_name
  environment      = var.environment
  vpc_id           = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnets  = module.vpc.private_subnets
  
  # SLO Configuration
  slo_availability   = var.slo_availability
  slo_latency_p95    = var.slo_latency_p95
  slo_error_rate     = var.slo_error_rate
  slo_llm_latency    = var.slo_llm_latency
  
  # Alert Configuration
  alert_email        = "sre-alerts@diyapp.com"
  slack_webhook_url  = var.slack_webhook_url
  
  # ECS Service Info for Service Discovery
  ecs_cluster_name   = module.ecs.ecs_cluster_name
  ecs_service_name   = "diyapp-api"
}
```

### terraform/modules/vpc/main.tf
```hcl
resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-vpc"
  }
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-igw"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count                   = length(var.availability_zones)
  vpc_id                  = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block              = cidrsubnet(var.vpc_cidr, 8, count.index)
  availability_zone       = var.availability_zones[count.index]
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = length(var.availability_zones)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = cidrsubnet(var.vpc_cidr, 8, count.index + 10)
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index]
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-public-rt"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = length(aws_subnet.public)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}

resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = length(var.availability_zones)
  domain = "vpc"
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-eip-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = length(var.availability_zones)
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[count.index].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-nat-${count.index}"
  }
  
  depends_on = [aws_internet_gateway.main]
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = length(var.availability_zones)
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
    nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[count.index].id
  }
  
  tags = {
    Name = "${var.project_name}-${var.environment}-private-rt-${count.index}"
  }
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = length(aws_subnet.private)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[count.index].id
}

# Security Groups

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Implementação de Segurança

Vou implementar um sistema de segurança completo com autenticação JWT, sanitização de inputs, scan de vulnerabilidades e WAF. Vou usar o Modo Hive para refatoração paralela, focando em estabilidade 100% autônoma.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
src/
├── auth/
│   ├── jwt.js
│   ├── middleware.js
│   └── validator.js
├── security/
│   ├── sanitizer.js
│   ├── waf.js
│   └── scanner.js
├── controllers/
│   └── authController.js
├── routes/
│   └── authRoutes.js
├── models/
│   └── User.js
├── config/
│   └── security.js
├── tests/
│   └── security.test.js
└── index.js
public/
├── index.html
└── assets/
    └── style.css
```

## 1. Configuração de Segurança (`src/config/security.js`)

```javascript
// Configurações de segurança centralizadas
const securityConfig = {
  // JWT Configuration
  jwt: {
    accessTokenSecret: process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET || 'your-access-secret-key-change-in-production',
    refreshTokenSecret: process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || 'your-refresh-secret-key-change-in-production',
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m', // 15 minutos conforme SLA
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d', // 7 dias conforme SLA
    issuer: 'diyapp-v12-core',
    audience: 'diyapp-users'
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    auth: {
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 5, // 5 tentativas por IP
      message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later'
    },
    api: {
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
      max: 100
    }
  },
  
  // WAF Rules
  waf: {
    enabled: true,
    maxPayloadSize: '1mb',
    blockSQLi: true,
    blockXSS: true,
    blockPathTraversal: true,
    blockCommandInjection: true
  },
  
  // Security Headers
  headers: {
    contentSecurityPolicy: "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net;",
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000,
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    },
    xFrameOptions: 'DENY',
    xContentTypeOptions: 'nosniff',
    referrerPolicy: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin'
  },
  
  // Password Policy
  passwordPolicy: {
    minLength: 12,
    requireUppercase: true,
    requireLowercase: true,
    requireNumbers: true,
    requireSpecialChars: true,
    blockCommonPasswords: true
  }
};

module.exports = securityConfig;
```

## 2. Implementação JWT (`src/auth/jwt.js`)

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

class JWTHandler {
  constructor() {
    this.accessSecret = securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenSecret;
    this.refreshSecret = securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenSecret;
    this.accessExpiry = securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenExpiry;
    this.refreshExpiry = securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenExpiry;
  }

  // Gera access token
  generateAccessToken(payload) {
    return jwt.sign(
      {
        ...payload,
        type: 'access'
      },
      this.accessSecret,
      {
        expiresIn: this.accessExpiry,
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      }
    );
  }

  // Gera refresh token com jti (JWT ID) para revogação
  generateRefreshToken(payload) {
    const jti = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
    const token = jwt.sign(
      {
        ...payload,
        type: 'refresh',
        jti: jti
      },
      this.refreshSecret,
      {
        expiresIn: this.refreshExpiry,
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      }
    );
    
    return { token, jti };
  }

  // Verifica access token
  verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.accessSecret, {
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Invalid access token: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Verifica refresh token
  verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.refreshSecret, {
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Invalid refresh token: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Decodifica token sem verificar (apenas para inspeção)
  decodeToken(token) {
    return jwt.decode(token);
  }

  // Rotação de tokens
  rotateTokens(refreshToken) {
    const decoded = this.verifyRefreshToken(refreshToken);
    
    // Remove campos específicos do refresh token
    const { type, jti, exp, iat, ...userPayload } = decoded;
    
    // Gera novos tokens
    const newAccessToken = this.generateAccessToken(userPayload);
    const { token: newRefreshToken, jti: newJti } = this.generateRefreshToken(userPayload);
    
    return {
      accessToken: newAccessToken,
      refreshToken: newRefreshToken,
      jti: newJti
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTHandler();
```

## 3. Middleware de Autenticação (`src/auth/middleware.js`)

```javascript
const jwtHandler = require('./jwt');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

// Rate limiter para autenticação
const authLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: securityConfig.rateLimit.auth.windowMs,
  max: securityConfig.rateLimit.auth.max,
  message: securityConfig.rateLimit.auth.message,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  skipSuccessfulRequests: true
});

// Middleware de autenticação JWT
const authenticateJWT = (req, res, next) => {
  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
  
  if (!authHeader) {
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Authentication required',
      code: 'AUTH_REQUIRED'
    });
  }

  const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];
  
  if (!token) {
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Invalid authorization format',
      code: 'INVALID_AUTH_FORMAT'
    });
  }

  try {
    const decoded = jwtHandler.verifyAccessToken(token);
    req.user = decoded;
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    return res.status(403).json({
      error: 'Invalid or expired token',
      code: 'INVALID_TOKEN',
      details: error.message
    });
  }
};

// Middleware de autorização baseada em roles
const authorize = (...roles) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Authentication required',
        code: 'AUTH_REQUIRED'
      });
    }

    if (!roles.includes(req.user.role)) {
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Insufficient permissions',
        code: 'INSUFFICIENT_PERMISSIONS',
        required: roles,
        current: req.user.role
      });
    }

    next();
  };
};

// Middleware para validação de CSRF (para formulários)
const csrfProtection = (req, res, next) => {
  if (req.method === 'GET' || req.method === 'HEAD' || req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return next();
  }

  const csrfToken = req.headers['x-csrf-token'] || req.body._csrf;
  const sessionToken = req.session?.csrfToken;

  if (!csrfToken || csrfToken !== sessionToken) {
    return res.status(403).json({
      error: 'Invalid CSRF token',
      code: 'INVALID_CSRF'
    });
  }

  next();
};

// Middleware para logging de auditoria
const auditLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const startTime = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
    const auditLog = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      duration: `${duration}ms`,
      user: req.user?.id || 'anonymous',
      ip: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
    };

    // Log apenas operações críticas
    if (req.method !== 'GET' || res.statusCode >= 400) {
      console.log('[AUDIT]', JSON.stringify(auditLog));
    }
  });

  next();
};

module.exports = {
  authenticateJWT,
  authorize,
  csrfProtection,
  authLimiter,
  auditLogger
};
```

## 4. Sanitizador de Inputs (`src/security/sanitizer.js`)

```javascript
const validator = require('validator');
const xss = require('xss');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    this.xssOptions = {
      whiteList: {}, // Nenhuma tag permitida por padrão
      stripIgnoreTag: true,
      stripIgnoreTagBody: ['script', 'style', 'iframe', 'object', 'embed']
    };
  }

  // Sanitiza string contra XSS
  sanitizeString(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    return xss(input, this.xssOptions);
  }

  // Sanitiza objeto completo
  sanitizeObject(obj) {
    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return obj;

    const sanitized = {};
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
      if (typeof value === 'string') {
        sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeString(value);
      } else if (Array.isArray(value)) {
        sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeArray(value);
      } else if (value && typeof value === 'object') {
        sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeObject(value);
      } else {
        sanitized[key] = value;
      }
    }

    return sanitized;
  }

  // Sanitiza array
  sanitizeArray(arr) {
    if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return arr;
    return arr.map(item => {
      if (typeof item === 'string') {
        return this.sanitizeString(item);
      } else if (Array.isArray(item)) {
        return this.sanitizeArray(item);
      } else if (item && typeof item === 'object') {
        return this.sanitizeObject(item);
      }
      return item;
    });
  }

  // Valida e sanitiza email
  sanitizeEmail(email) {
    if (!validator.isEmail(email)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid email format');
    }
    return validator.normalizeEmail(email);
  }

  // Valida e sanitiza URL
  sanitizeURL(url) {
    if (!validator.isURL(url, { require_protocol: true })) {
      throw new Error('Invalid URL format');
    }
    return validator.escape(url);
  }

  // Valida senha conforme política
  validatePassword(password) {
    const policy = securityConfig.passwordPolicy;
    const errors = [];

    if (password.length < policy.minLength) {
      errors.push(`Password must be at least ${policy.minLength} characters long`);
    }

    if (policy.requireUppercase && !/[A-Z]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('Password must contain at least one uppercase letter');
    }

    if (policy.requireLowercase && !/[a-z]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('Password must contain at least one lowercase letter');
    }

    if (policy.requireNumbers && !/\d/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('Password must contain at least one number');
    }

    if (policy.requireSpecialChars && !/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('Password must contain at least one special character');
    }

    if (policy.blockCommonPasswords) {
      const commonPasswords = ['password', '123456', 'qwerty', 'admin', 'letmein'];
      if (commonPasswords.includes(password.toLowerCase())) {
        errors.push('Password is too common');
      }
    }

    if (errors.length > 0) {
      throw new Error(`Password validation failed: ${errors.join(', ')}`);
    }

    return password;
  }

  // Prevenção contra SQL Injection
  sanitizeSQL(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove caracteres perigosos para SQL
    return input.replace(/['"\\;()\-\-]/g, '');
  }

  // Prevenção contra Path Traversal
  sanitizePath(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove sequências de path traversal
    return input.replace(/\.\.\//g, '').replace(/\.\.\\/g, '');
  }

  // Middleware para sanitização automática
  middleware() {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (req.body) {
        req.body = this.sanitizeObject(req.body);
      }
      
      if (req.query) {
        req.query = this.sanitizeObject(req.query);
      }
      
      if (req.params) {
        req.params = this.sanitizeObject(req.params);
      }
      
      next();
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new InputSanitizer();
```

## 5. Web Application Firewall (`src/security/waf.js`)

```javascript
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');

class WAF {
  constructor() {
    this.rules = this.initializeRules();
    this.blockedIPs = new Map();
    this.suspiciousPatterns = [
      // SQL Injection patterns
      /(\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%23)|(#)/gi,
      /((\%3D)|(=))[^\n]*((\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%3B)|(;))/gi,
      /\w*((\%27)|(\'))((\%6F)|o|(\%4F))((\%72)|r|(\%52))/gi,
      
      // XSS patterns
      /((\%3C)|<)((\%2F)|\/)*[a-z0-9\%]+((\%3E)|>)/gi,
      /((\%3C)|<)((\%69)|i|(\%49))((\%6D)|m|(\%4D))((\%67)|g|(\%47))[^\n]+((\%3E)|>)/gi,
      /((\%3C)|<)[^\n]+((\%3E)|>)/gi,
      
      // Command Injection patterns
      /;|\||&|`|\$\(|\n|\r/gi,
      
      // Path Traversal patterns
      /\.\.\/|\.\.\\/gi,
      
      // File Inclusion patterns
      /(\.\.\/)+/gi
    ];
  }

  initializeRules() {
    return {
      maxPayloadSize: securityConfig.waf.maxPayloadSize,
      blockSQLi: securityConfig.waf.blockSQLi,
      blockXSS: securityConfig.waf.blockXSS,
      blockPathTraversal: securityConfig.waf.blockPathTraversal,
      blockCommandInjection: securityConfig.waf.blockCommandInjection,
      maxRequestLength: 8192, // 8KB
      maxUrlLength: 2048,
      maxHeaderCount: 50
    };
  }

  // Verifica se há padrões maliciosos no input
  checkForMaliciousPatterns(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return false;

    for (const pattern of this.suspiciousPatterns) {
      if (pattern.test(input)) {
        return {
          blocked: true,
          pattern: pattern.toString(),
          input: input.substring(0, 100) // Log apenas parte do input
        };
      }
    }

    return { blocked: false };
  }

  // Valida tamanho do payload
  validatePayloadSize(req) {
    const contentLength = parseInt(req.headers['content-length']) || 0;
    const maxSize = this.parseSize(this.rules.maxPayloadSize);
    
    if (contentLength > maxSize) {
      return {
        blocked: true,
        reason: `Payload too large: ${contentLength} > ${maxSize}`,
        code: 'PAYLOAD_TOO_LARGE'
      };
    }
    
    return { blocked: false };
  }

  // Valida headers da requisição
  validateHeaders(req) {
    const headerCount = Object.keys(req.headers).length;
    
    if (headerCount > this.rules.maxHeaderCount) {
      return {
        blocked: true,
        reason: `Too many headers: ${headerCount}`,
        code: 'TOO_MANY_HEADERS'
      };
    }
    
    // Verifica headers maliciosos
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(req.headers)) {
      const result = this.checkForMaliciousPatterns(`${key}: ${value}`);
      if (result.blocked) {
        return {
          blocked: true,
          reason: `Malicious header detected: ${key}`,
          code: 'MALICIOUS_HEADER',
          details: result
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { blocked: false };
  }

  // Valida URL
  validate

## 1. Circuit Breaker para APIs de IA

```python
# src/llm_gateway/circuit_breaker.py
import time
import asyncio
from typing import Dict, Optional, Callable
from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CircuitState(Enum):
    CLOSED = "CLOSED"
    OPEN = "OPEN"
    HALF_OPEN = "HALF_OPEN"

@dataclass
class CircuitBreakerConfig:
    failure_threshold: int = 5
    reset_timeout: int = 60  # seconds
    half_open_max_attempts: int = 3
    success_threshold: int = 3

class CircuitBreaker:
    def __init__(self, name: str, config: Optional[CircuitBreakerConfig] = None):
        self.name = name
        self.config = config or CircuitBreakerConfig()
        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.success_count = 0
        self.last_failure_time = None
        self.last_state_change = time.time()
        
    def can_execute(self) -> bool:
        """Check if circuit breaker allows execution"""
        if self.state == CircuitState.CLOSED:
            return True
            
        if self.state == CircuitState.OPEN:
            # Check if reset timeout has passed
            if time.time() - self.last_failure_time > self.config.reset_timeout:
                self._transition_to_half_open()
                return True
            return False
            
        if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
            return self.success_count < self.config.half_open_max_attempts
            
        return False
    
    def record_success(self):
        """Record successful execution"""
        if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
            self.success_count += 1
            if self.success_count >= self.config.success_threshold:
                self._transition_to_closed()
        elif self.state == CircuitState.CLOSED:
            self.failure_count = 0
            
    def record_failure(self):
        """Record failed execution"""
        self.failure_count += 1
        self.last_failure_time = time.time()
        
        if self.state == CircuitState.CLOSED:
            if self.failure_count >= self.config.failure_threshold:
                self._transition_to_open()
        elif self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
            self._transition_to_open()
    
    def _transition_to_open(self):
        self.state = CircuitState.OPEN
        self.last_state_change = time.time()
        logger.warning(f"Circuit breaker {self.name} transitioned to OPEN state")
        
    def _transition_to_half_open(self):
        self.state = CircuitState.HALF_OPEN
        self.success_count = 0
        self.last_state_change = time.time()
        logger.info(f"Circuit breaker {self.name} transitioned to HALF_OPEN state")
        
    def _transition_to_closed(self):
        self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.success_count = 0
        self.last_state_change = time.time()
        logger.info(f"Circuit breaker {self.name} transitioned to CLOSED state")
    
    def get_status(self) -> Dict:
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "state": self.state.value,
            "failure_count": self.failure_count,
            "success_count": self.success_count,
            "last_failure_time": self.last_failure_time,
            "last_state_change": self.last_state_change,
            "can_execute": self.can_execute()
        }

class CircuitBreakerManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.breakers: Dict[str, CircuitBreaker] = {}
        
    def get_breaker(self, name: str, config: Optional[CircuitBreakerConfig] = None) -> CircuitBreaker:
        if name not in self.breakers:
            self.breakers[name] = CircuitBreaker(name, config)
        return self.breakers[name]
    
    async def execute_with_breaker(self, breaker_name: str, func: Callable, *args, **kwargs):
        """Execute function with circuit breaker protection"""
        breaker = self.get_breaker(breaker_name)
        
        if not breaker.can_execute():
            raise CircuitBreakerOpenError(f"Circuit breaker {breaker_name} is OPEN")
        
        try:
            result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
            breaker.record_success()
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            breaker.record_failure()
            logger.error(f"Circuit breaker {breaker_name} recorded failure: {str(e)}")
            raise
    
    def get_all_statuses(self) -> Dict[str, Dict]:
        return {name: breaker.get_status() for name, breaker in self.breakers.items()}

class CircuitBreakerOpenError(Exception):
    pass
```

## 2. Sistema de Fallback para LLMs

```python
# src/llm_gateway/fallback_manager.py
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
import asyncio
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class LLMProvider(Enum):
    OPENAI_GPT4 = "openai_gpt4"
    OPENAI_GPT35 = "openai_gpt35"
    CLAUDE_OPUS = "claude_opus"
    CLAUDE_SONNET = "claude_sonnet"
    GEMINI_PRO = "gemini_pro"
    GEMINI_FLASH = "gemini_flash"

@dataclass
class ProviderConfig:
    provider: LLMProvider
    model_name: str
    api_key_env: str
    base_url: Optional[str] = None
    max_tokens: int = 4000
    temperature: float = 0.7
    timeout: int = 30
    cost_per_1k_input: float = 0.0
    cost_per_1k_output: float = 0.0

class FallbackManager:
    def __init__(self, provider_configs: List[ProviderConfig]):
        self.provider_configs = provider_configs
        self.fallback_chains = self._build_fallback_chains()
        self.active_providers: Dict[LLMProvider, bool] = {
            config.provider: True for config in provider_configs
        }
        
    def _build_fallback_chains(self) -> Dict[str, List[LLMProvider]]:
        """Define fallback chains for different use cases"""
        return {
            "high_quality": [
                LLMProvider.CLAUDE_OPUS,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT4,
                LLMProvider.GEMINI_PRO,
                LLMProvider.CLAUDE_SONNET,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT35
            ],
            "balanced": [
                LLMProvider.CLAUDE_SONNET,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT35,
                LLMProvider.GEMINI_FLASH,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT4
            ],
            "cost_effective": [
                LLMProvider.GEMINI_FLASH,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT35,
                LLMProvider.CLAUDE_SONNET
            ],
            "fast": [
                LLMProvider.GEMINI_FLASH,
                LLMProvider.OPENAI_GPT35,
                LLMProvider.CLAUDE_SONNET
            ]
        }
    
    def disable_provider(self, provider: LLMProvider):
        """Disable a provider (e.g., due to circuit breaker opening)"""
        self.active_providers[provider] = False
        logger.warning(f"Provider {provider.value} disabled")
    
    def enable_provider(self, provider: LLMProvider):
        """Re-enable a provider"""
        self.active_providers[provider] = True
        logger.info(f"Provider {provider.value} enabled")
    
    def get_fallback_chain(self, chain_type: str = "balanced") -> List[LLMProvider]:
        """Get active providers in fallback order"""
        chain = self.fallback_chains.get(chain_type, self.fallback_chains["balanced"])
        return [p for p in chain if self.active_providers.get(p, False)]
    
    async def execute_with_fallback(self, chain_type: str, prompt: str, **kwargs):
        """Execute LLM call with automatic fallback"""
        fallback_chain = self.get_fallback_chain(chain_type)
        
        if not fallback_chain:
            raise NoActiveProvidersError("No active LLM providers available")
        
        last_exception = None
        
        for provider in fallback_chain:
            try:
                logger.info(f"Attempting LLM call with provider: {provider.value}")
                result = await self._call_provider(provider, prompt, **kwargs)
                
                # Log successful call for monitoring
                self._log_successful_call(provider, prompt, result)
                
                return {
                    "provider": provider.value,
                    "result": result,
                    "fallback_used": provider != fallback_chain[0]
                }
                
            except Exception as e:
                last_exception = e
                logger.warning(f"Provider {provider.value} failed: {str(e)}")
                
                # Log failed call for monitoring
                self._log_failed_call(provider, prompt, str(e))
                
                # Continue to next provider in chain
                continue
        
        # All providers failed
        raise AllProvidersFailedError(
            f"All providers in chain {chain_type} failed. Last error: {str(last_exception)}"
        )
    
    async def _call_provider(self, provider: LLMProvider, prompt: str, **kwargs):
        """Make actual LLM API call"""
        # This would be implemented with actual API calls
        # For now, simulating with a mock
        await asyncio.sleep(0.1)  # Simulate API call
        
        # Simulate occasional failures for testing
        import random
        if random.random() < 0.1:  # 10% failure rate for testing
            raise Exception("Simulated API failure")
            
        return f"Response from {provider.value}: Processed prompt"
    
    def _log_successful_call(self, provider: LLMProvider, prompt: str, result: str):
        """Log successful call for monitoring"""
        # This would log to monitoring system
        pass
    
    def _log_failed_call(self, provider: LLMProvider, prompt: str, error: str):
        """Log failed call for monitoring"""
        # This would log to monitoring system
        pass

class NoActiveProvidersError(Exception):
    pass

class AllProvidersFailedError(Exception):
    pass
```

## 3. Otimizador de Prompts

```python
# src/llm_gateway/prompt_optimizer.py
import re
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
import tiktoken
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class PromptOptimizer:
    def __init__(self):
        self.tokenizers = {}
        
    def optimize_prompt(self, prompt: str, target_model: str, max_tokens: Optional[int] = None) -> Dict:
        """Optimize prompt for specific model"""
        optimization_result = {
            "original_prompt": prompt,
            "original_token_count": self.count_tokens(prompt, target_model),
            "optimizations_applied": [],
            "optimized_prompt": prompt,
            "optimized_token_count": self.count_tokens(prompt, target_model),
            "suggestions": []
        }
        
        # Apply optimizations
        optimized = prompt
        
        # Remove excessive whitespace
        if self._has_excessive_whitespace(prompt):
            optimized = self._remove_excessive_whitespace(optimized)
            optimization_result["optimizations_applied"].append("removed_excessive_whitespace")
        
        # Remove redundant instructions
        if self._has_redundant_instructions(prompt):
            optimized = self._remove_redundant_instructions(optimized)
            optimization_result["optimizations_applied"].append("removed_redundant_instructions")
        
        # Optimize system prompts
        if self._has_verbose_system_prompt(prompt):
            optimized = self._optimize_system_prompt(optimized)
            optimization_result["optimizations_applied"].append("optimized_system_prompt")
        
        # Check for prompt injection patterns
        injection_patterns = self._detect_prompt_injection(prompt)
        if injection_patterns:
            optimization_result["suggestions"].append({
                "type": "security_warning",
                "message": f"Potential prompt injection patterns detected: {injection_patterns}"
            })
        
        # Update optimization result
        optimization_result["optimized_prompt"] = optimized
        optimization_result["optimized_token_count"] = self.count_tokens(optimized, target_model)
        
        # Calculate savings
        original_tokens = optimization_result["original_token_count"]
        optimized_tokens = optimization_result["optimized_token_count"]
        
        if original_tokens > 0:
            token_savings = ((original_tokens - optimized_tokens) / original_tokens) * 100
            optimization_result["token_savings_percentage"] = round(token_savings, 2)
        
        # Check if prompt needs chunking
        if max_tokens and optimized_tokens > max_tokens * 0.8:  # 80% of max tokens
            optimization_result["suggestions"].append({
                "type": "warning",
                "message": f"Prompt uses {optimized_tokens} tokens ({(optimized_tokens/max_tokens)*100:.1f}% of max). Consider chunking."
            })
        
        return optimization_result
    
    def count_tokens(self, text: str, model: str) -> int:
        """Count tokens for a specific model"""
        try:
            if "gpt" in model.lower():
                encoding = tiktoken.encoding_for_model(model)
                return len(encoding.encode(text))
            elif "claude" in model.lower():
                # Claude approximate token count (4 chars ~= 1 token)
                return len(text) // 4
            else:
                # Default approximation
                return len(text.split())
        except:
            # Fallback to word count approximation
            return len(text.split())
    
    def _has_excessive_whitespace(self, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """Check for excessive whitespace"""
        return bool(re.search(r'\n\s*\n\s*\n', prompt)) or bool(re.search(r' {4,}', prompt))
    
    def _remove_excessive_whitespace(self, prompt: str) -> str:
        """Remove excessive whitespace"""
        # Replace multiple newlines with double newlines
        prompt = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n\s*\n+', '\n\n', prompt)
        # Replace multiple spaces with single space
        prompt = re.sub(r' {2,}', ' ', prompt)
        return prompt.strip()
    
    def _has_redundant_instructions(self, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """Check for redundant instructions"""
        redundant_patterns = [
            r'please\s+make\s+sure\s+to',
            r'be\s+sure\s+to',
            r'it\s+is\s+important\s+to',
            r'remember\s+to',
            r'don\'t\s+forget\s+to',
        ]
        count = 0
        for pattern in redundant_patterns:
            if re.search(pattern, prompt, re.IGNORECASE):
                count += 1
        return count > 2
    
    def _remove_redundant_instructions(self, prompt: str) -> str:
        """Remove redundant instructions"""
        # This is a simplified version - in production would be more sophisticated
        lines = prompt.split('\n')
        cleaned_lines = []
        redundant_count = 0
        
        for line in lines:
            if not any(re.search(pattern, line, re.IGNORECASE) 
                      for pattern in [r'please\s+make\s+sure', r'be\s+sure\s+to', r'remember\s+to']):
                cleaned_lines.append(line)
            else:
                redundant_count += 1
                if redundant_count <= 1:  # Keep first occurrence
                    cleaned_lines.append(line)
        
        return '\n'.join(cleaned_lines)
    
    def _has_verbose_system_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """Check if system prompt is verbose"""
        system_prompts = re.findall(r'(?i)system:|you are|assistant:|ai:', prompt)
        return len
